<script>
var famNum = 100;
layui.use(['form','easyutils','easybankutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easybankutils=layui.easybankutils
,easyUpload = layui.easyUpload;
//日期控件绑定
easyutils.renderDate('layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYSTU');
easyUpload.initAllFilesUpload(0);
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
var isP = easyutils.checkboxValues('IS_PROMISE');
if(isP==null || isP==''){
return layer.msg('请勾选资料真实性申明');
}
field.IS_PROMISE = isP;
field.exeStatus=1;
field.attrfileids = easyutils.splitNameValues('attrfileids');
field.FAMILY_DFAMILY_UID = easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_DFAMILY_UID');
field.FAMILY_MEMBER_NAME =
easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_MEMBER_NAME');
field.FAMILY_RELATION_CODE =
easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_RELATION_CODE');
field.FAMILY_BIRTHDAY_DATE =
easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_BIRTHDAY_DATE');
field.FAMILY_WORK_UNIT = easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_WORK_UNIT');
field.FAMILY_TITLES_NAME = easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_TITLES_NAME');
field.FAMILY_INCOME_YEAR =
easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_INCOME_YEAR');
field.FAMILY_HEALTH_CODE = easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_HEALTH_CODE');
field.SPECIAL_TYPE = easyutils.checkboxValues('SPECIAL_TYPE');
layer.confirm('确认提交困难生认定申请资料至辅导员审核吗？请核对填写内
容是否完善准确！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultStuManage/saveStuApply',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_applyUidDifficult_search").click();//刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-save)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus=0;
field.attrfileids = easyutils.splitNameValues('attrfileids');
field.FAMILY_DFAMILY_UID = easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_DFAMILY_UID');
field.FAMILY_MEMBER_NAME =
easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_MEMBER_NAME');
field.FAMILY_RELATION_CODE =
easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_RELATION_CODE');
field.FAMILY_BIRTHDAY_DATE =
easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_BIRTHDAY_DATE');
field.FAMILY_WORK_UNIT = easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_WORK_UNIT');
field.FAMILY_TITLES_NAME = easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_TITLES_NAME');
field.FAMILY_INCOME_YEAR =
easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_INCOME_YEAR');
field.FAMILY_HEALTH_CODE = easyutils.splitNameValues('FAMILY_HEALTH_CODE');
field.SPECIAL_TYPE = easyutils.checkboxValues('SPECIAL_TYPE');
layer.confirm('确认保存困难生认定申请资料，不提交审核吗？', function(index)
{
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultStuManage/saveStuApply',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_applyUidDifficult_search").click();//刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_close").click(function(){
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
$('#dfamilynewatt_btn').click(function(){
famNum=parseFloat(famNum)+1;
var data={num:famNum};
var getTpl = document.getElementById('TPL_dfamily_value').innerHTML;
layui.laytpl(getTpl).render(data, function(html){
layui.$("#dfamilyTbodyId").append(html);
//日期控件绑定
easyutils.renderDate('layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYSTU');
var rObj=$("#FAMILY_RELATION_CODE_"+famNum);
// rObj.attr("src","SYS_DM_RELATION");
// rObj.attr("kind","dic");
// rObj.attr("defaultValue",null);
// rObj.html('');
easyutils.reloadSelectDic(rObj);
var hObj = $("#FAMILY_HEALTH_CODE_"+famNum);
easyutils.reloadSelectDic(hObj);
form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYSTU');
});
});
});
function verifyBankFun(){
var bankCode = layui.$("#DIFF_BANK_CODE_ID").val();
var v = layui.easybankutils.verifyBankCardNumber(bankCode);
// console.log(v);
if(!v){
layui.$("#DIFF_BANK_CODE_ID_mes").html("银行卡格式不对，请核对");
}
// var b = layui.easybankutils.bankCardAttribution(bankCode);
// console.log(b);
}
function deleteAttSpan(t){
layui.$(t).parent().parent().remove();
countIncomeFun();
}
//人均年收入
function countIncomeFun(o){
var child = layui.$('.layui-form').find('input[name="FAMILY_INCOME_YEAR"]');
if(child!=null && child.size()){
var allIncome = 0.0;
child.each(function(index,item){
if(item.value!=null && item.value!=''){
allIncome = allIncome + parseFloat(item.value);
}
})
var perNum = child.size()+1;//算上学生自己
var perIncome = allIncome/perNum;
perIncome = Math.round(perIncome);
layui.$("#PER_CAPITA_INCOME_ID").val(perIncome);
layui.$("#FAMILY_NUM_ID").val(perNum);
}
}
</script>

<script type="text/html" id="opttoolapplyUidDifficultBar">
{{# if(d.tableType=='applyData'){ }}
{{# if(d.AUDIT_STATUS==null && d.isApply=='1'){ }}

title="申请">申请</a>
{{# } }}

{{# if(d.tableType=='returnData'){ }}

<script>
var tableObj;
layui.use(['element','easytable','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,element = layui.element
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
element.on('tab(apply_DIFFICULT-tabs-brief)', function(data){
var tabObject=$(this);
var dType= tabObject.attr('data_type');
initTabFun(dType);
});
initTabFun('getData');
$("#btn_applyUidDifficult_search").click(function(){
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYSTU-formlist');
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYSTU)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'del'){
layer.confirm("确定取消困难生的申请吗？撤销需要重新填写资料进行申请，此操
作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID,dataStatus:"-1"};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultStuManage/deleteStu',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_applyUidDifficult_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'retu'){
layer.confirm("确定撤回困难生的申请吗？撤回需要重新修改资料并提交申请，此
操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID,dataStatus:"0"};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultStuManage/deleteStu',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_applyUidDifficult_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
});
}else if(obj.event === 'apply'){
var data1 = {setupUid:data.SETUP_UID,applyUid:data.APPLY_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 申 请 困 难 生
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/apply/input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYSTU','e
asyajax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
var selects1=[null,null];
if(d.STU_NATIVE_CODE){
var pn = d.STU_NATIVE_CODE.substr(0,2)+"0000";
selects1=[pn,d.STU_NATIVE_CODE];
$("#STUINFINPUT_SELVALUE_NATIVE").val(pn+","+d.STU_NATIVE_CODE);
}
layui.easyutils.selectCityCode('#STUINFINPUT_SELID_NATIVE',selects1, function stuDifNativeCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#STUINFINPUT_SELVALUE_NATIVE").val(o.values.join(","));
});//籍贯地区
easyutils.val('layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYSTU',d);
easyutils.checkboxSetV("SPECIAL_TYPE",d.SPECIAL_TYPE);
if(d.APPLY_UID){//初始化文件
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,true);
}
});
} else if(obj.event === 'exp'){
var formData="applyUid="+data.APPLY_UID;
layer.confirm("确定导出困难生申请表吗？确认请点确定！", {icon: 3, title:'提示
'}, function(index){
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/difficultStuManage/expPdf',data.ST
U_NO+"_困难生申请表.docx",formData);
layer.close(index);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
if(data.APPLY_UID){
var data1 = {setupUid:data.SETUP_UID,applyUid:data.APPLY_UID,isView:"1"};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/apply/view','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY','easyaj
ax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY');
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,false);
if(d.recodeList){
layui.each(d.recodeList, function(index, item){
if(item.DATA_TYPE=='college'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(11,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}else if(item.DATA_TYPE=='counselor'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(10,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}
});
}
});
}else{
var data1 = {setupUid:data.SETUP_UID};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'70%','95%','support/difficult/setup/view','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP','easya
jax/difficultSetupManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
}
}
});
});
function initTabFun(dType){
layui.$('table[lay-filter="easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYSTU"]').find('thead>tr').each(
function(i){
layui.$(this).children().each(function(ii){
var th = layui.$(this), itemData = th.attr('easy-data');
var obj = eval('(' + itemData + ')');
if(dType=='getData'){
for(var p in obj){
if(obj[p] == 'APPLY_DATE' || obj[p] == 'END_DATE'){
obj.hide = true;
break;
}
}
}else if(dType=='applyData'){
for(var p in obj){
if(obj[p] == 'APPLY_DATE'){
obj.hide = true;
break;
}else if(obj[p] == 'END_DATE'){
obj.hide = false;
break;
}
}
}else if(dType=='auditData' || dType=='returnData'){
for(var p in obj){
if(obj[p] == 'END_DATE'){
obj.hide = true;
break;
}else if(obj[p] == 'APPLY_DATE'){
obj.hide = false;
break;
}
}
}
th.attr("easy-data",JSON.stringify(obj));
});
});
layui.$("#DIFFICULT_DATA_TYPE").val(dType);
tableObj =
layui.easytable.init('easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYSTU',"layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_ APPLYSTU-formlist");
layui.$("#btn_applyUidDifficult_search").click(); //刷新
}
</script>

</style>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
easyUpload.initAllFilesUpload(1);
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT_close").click(function(){
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus = '1' field.APPLY_REASON = easyutils.checkboxValues('APPLY_REASON');
field.auditfileids = easyutils.splitNameValues('auditfileids');
if(field.OLD_DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID !=field.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID){
if(field.exeRemark==null || field.exeRemark==''){
return layer.msg('推荐档次有变化，请在审核意见处填入原因！');
}
if(field.auditfileids==false || field.auditfileids.length==0){
return layer.msg('推荐档次有变化，请上传对应的佐证材料！');
}
}
layer.confirm('确定审核通过吗？审核后进入下一个流程环节，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/batchAudit',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_search").click(); //刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-return)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus = '0' layer.confirm('确定审核退回吗？审核后进入起始环节，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/batchAudit',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_search").click(); //刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-unpass)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus = '-1' layer.confirm('确定审核拒绝吗？拒绝后立即终止流转，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/batchAudit',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_search").click(); //刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT-formlist');
var selects1=[null,null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_SELID_COLLEGE',selects
1,function difficultApAuditCollCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
});//学院专业班级
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT',"layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFI
CULT_APPLYAUDIT-formlist");
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_search").click(function(){
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT-formlist');
});
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'batchAudit':
var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id)
,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
if(checkData.length === 0){
return layer.msg('请选择数据');
}
var checkUids="" ;
var checkNames = [],checkNos=[];
layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){
checkUids+=item.APPLY_UID+",";
checkNames.push(item.STU_STU_NAME);
checkNos.push(item.STU_NO);
});
var data1 = {checkNames:checkNames,checkNos:checkNos};
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 困 难 生 批 量 审 核
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/audit/bat_input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAU
DIT',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_UIDS").val(checkUids);
});
break;
case 'addFile':
var successData={MODULE_TYPE:'difficult',DATA_TYPE:'college'};
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 公 示 材 料 上 传
",'80%','95%','base/filerecord/college_file','layuiadmin-form-MFILE',successData,function
renderDoneFun(d){
$("#MFILE_LEGEND_TITLE").html("公示材料上传");
});
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'audit'){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID,isView:"1"};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 困 难 生 审 核
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/audit/audit_input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYA
UDIT','easyajax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#SUPPORT_OLD_DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID").val(d.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID);
easyutils.val('layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT',d);
easyutils.checkboxSetV("SPECIAL_TYPE",d.SPECIAL_TYPE);
easyutils.checkboxSetV("APPLY_REASON",d.APPLY_REASON);
//初始化文件
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,false);
if(d.recodeList){
layui.each(d.recodeList, function(index, item){
if(item.DATA_TYPE=='college'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(11,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}else if(item.DATA_TYPE=='counselor'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(10,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}
});
}
});
}else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID,isView:"1"};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/apply/view','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY','easyaj
ax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY');
//初始化文件
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,false);
if(d.recodeList){
layui.each(d.recodeList, function(index, item){
if(item.DATA_TYPE=='college'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(11,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}else if(item.DATA_TYPE=='counselor'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(10,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}
});
}
});
}
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload = layui.easyUpload;
easyUpload.initAllFilesUpload(1);
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus = '1';
field.isBat = '1';
field.auditfileids = easyutils.splitNameValues('auditfileids');
layer.confirm('确定批量审核通过吗？审核后进入下一个流程环节，此操作不能撤销！
', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/batchAudit',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_search").click(); //刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-return)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus = '0';
field.isBat = '1';
layer.confirm('确定批量审核退回吗？审核后进入上一个流程环节，此操作不能撤销！
', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/batchAudit',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_search").click(); //刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-unpass)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus = '-1';
field.isBat = '1';
layer.confirm('确定批量审核拒绝吗？审核后进入起始环节，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/batchAudit',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAUDIT_search").click(); //刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT_close").click(function(){
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
});
</script>

<div class="layui-form-item text-center">
<input type="hidden" name="APPLY_UID" >
<input type="button" lay-submit lay-filter="LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-submit" value="通过" class="layui-btn">
<input type="button" lay-submit lay-filter="LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-return" value="退回" class="layui-btn layui-btn-warm">
<input type="button" lay-submit lay-filter="LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-unpass" value="拒绝" class="layui-btn layui-btn-danger">
<input type="button" class="layui-btn lay-btn-close" value=" 取 消 "
id="btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT_close">
</div>
</div>
<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT_close").click(function(){
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus = '1'
field.SPECIAL_TYPE = easyutils.checkboxValues('SPECIAL_TYPE');
field.APPLY_REASON = easyutils.checkboxValues('APPLY_REASON');
layer.confirm('确定审核通过吗？审核后进入下一个流程环节，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/counselorAudit',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR_search").click(); //刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-return)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus = '0' layer.confirm('确定审核退回吗？审核后进入起始环节，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/counselorAudit',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR_search").click(); //刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_AUDIT-unpass)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.exeStatus = '-1' layer.confirm('确定审核拒绝吗？拒绝后立即终止流转，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/counselorAudit',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR_search").click(); //刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR-formlist');
var selects1=[null,null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR_SELID_COLLEGE',selects
1,function difficultApAuditCollCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
});//学院专业班级
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR',"layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFI
CULT_COUNSELOR-formlist");
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR_search").click(function(){
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR-formlist');
});
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'add':
easyutils.popupWindow(" 困 难 生 取 消 认 定
",'80%','95%','support/difficult/counselor/input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY',n
ull,null,null);
break;
case 'addFile':
var successData={MODULE_TYPE:'difficult',DATA_TYPE:'counselor'};
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 民 主 评 议 材 料 上 传
",'80%','95%','base/filerecord/counselor_file','layuiadmin-form-MFILE',successData,function
renderDoneFun(d){
$("#MFILE_LEGEND_TITLE").html("民主评议材料上传");
});
break;
case 'getAccount':
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 班 级 评 议 员 账 号
",'60%','75%','basesys/class/class_account','layuiadmin-form-MFILE',null,function
renderDoneFun(d){
});
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'audit'){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID,isView:"1"};
// easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 困 难 生 审 核
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/counselor/audit_input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_C
OUNSELOR','easyajax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
// easyutils.render(null,'layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR');
// console.log(d.SPECIAL_TYPE);
// easyutils.checkboxSetV("SPECIAL_TYPE",d.SPECIAL_TYPE);
// //初始化文件
// easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,true);
// });
easyutils.popupWindow(" 困 难 生 审 核
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/counselor/audit_input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_C
OUNSELOR','easyajax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
easyutils.val('layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_COUNSELOR',d);
easyutils.checkboxSetV("SPECIAL_TYPE",d.SPECIAL_TYPE);
easyutils.checkboxSetV("APPLY_REASON",d.APPLY_REASON);
//初始化文件
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,false);
if(d.recodeList){
layui.each(d.recodeList, function(index, item){
if(item.DATA_TYPE=='college'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(11,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}else if(item.DATA_TYPE=='counselor'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(10,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}
});
}
});
}else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID,isView:"1"};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/apply/view','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY','easyaj
ax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY');
//初始化文件
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,false);
if(d.recodeList){
layui.each(d.recodeList, function(index, item){
if(item.DATA_TYPE=='college'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(11,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}else if(item.DATA_TYPE=='counselor'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(10,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}
});
}
});
}
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
//日期控件绑定
easyutils.renderDate('layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY');
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
layer.confirm('确定在本学期对该生取消认定并提交至学院审核吗？此操作不能撤
销！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultAuditManage/counselorAdd',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
easyutils.layMes('success','提交成功！');
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_search").click();//刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_close").click(function(){
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
$("#btn_search_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY").click(function(){
var stuData = layui.$("#SEARCH_STU_DATA_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY").val();
if(stuData!=null && stuData!=''){
var data1 = {SEARCH_STU_DATA:stuData,isYd:'1'};
easyutils.reqGet('easyajax/studentInfoManage/getStuInfoMap',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
var successData=res.data;
document.getElementById('xjydTbodyId').innerHTML = "";
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_STU_NO").val("");
if(successData){
easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY",successData);
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_STU_NO").val(successData.STU_STU_NO);
if(successData.ydList){
var getTpl = document.getElementById('TPL_xjydTbodyId_init').innerHTML;
var data={ydList: successData.ydList};
layui.laytpl(getTpl).render(data, function(html){
document.getElementById('xjydTbodyId').innerHTML = html;
});
}
}
}else{
easyutils.layMes('error',res.reasonremark);
return false;
}
});
}else{
easyutils.layMes('error','请输入学号/身份证号数据！');
return false;
}
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
//日期控件绑定
easyutils.renderDate('layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY');
//监听提交
form.on('submit(LAY-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-submit)', function(data){
var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
field.SPECIAL_TYPE = easyutils.checkboxValues('SPECIAL_TYPE');
field.APPLY_REASON = easyutils.checkboxValues('APPLY_REASON');
layer.confirm('确定保存修改内容吗？此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/difficultApplyManage/saveOrUpdate',field,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_search").click();//刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});
});
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_close").click(function(){
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-formlist');
var selects1=[null,null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_SELID_COLLEGE',selects1,func
tion difficultApplyCollCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
});//学院专业班级
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY',"layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_ APPLY-formlist");
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_search").click(function(){
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_ISE").val("0");
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-formlist');
});
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'add':
easyutils.popupWindow(" 添 加
",'80%','95%','support/difficult/maintain/input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY',nu
ll,null,null);
break;
case 'stu_import':
var successData = {YEAR_NUM:new Date().getFullYear()}
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 困 难 生 名 单 导 入
",'70%','95%','support/difficult/maintain/stu_import','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APP
LY',successData,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
break;
case 'stubank_import':
var successData = null;
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 学 生 银 行 卡 导 入
",'70%','95%','stu/stuinfo/stubank_import','layuiadmin-form-STUDENT_INFO',successData,functio
n renderDoneFun(d){
});
break;
case 'batchdel':
var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id)
,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
if(checkData.length === 0){
return layer.msg('请选择数据');
}
var checkUids="",isCon=true;
layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){
checkUids+=item.APPLY_UID+",";
if(item.AUDIT_STATUS!='0' && item.AUDIT_STATUS!='-100'){
layer.msg('所选择数据包括不可删除的数据，请核实之后再进行删除！');
isCon=false;
}
});
if(isCon){
layer.confirm('确定删除吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
var data1 = {applyUid:checkUids};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultApplyManage/delete',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
});
}
break;
case 'batchAudit':
var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id)
,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
if(checkData.length === 0){
return layer.msg('请选择数据');
}
var checkUids="" ;
var checkNames = [],checkNos=[];
layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){
checkUids+=item.APPLY_UID+",";
checkNames.push(item.STU_STU_NAME);
checkNos.push(item.STU_NO);
});
var data1 = {checkNames:checkNames,checkNos:checkNos};
easyutils.popupDataWindow(" 困 难 生 名 单 批 量 提 交
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/audit/bat_input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLYAU
DIT',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_UIDS").val(checkUids);
});
break;
case 'stu_export':
layer.confirm("确定导出全部数据吗？数据过大时，请使用查询条件进行筛选过滤！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_ISE").val("1");
var
formatjson=easytable.queryWhereFun('layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY-formlist');
var dataP =
'conditions='+formatjson.conditions+'&otherConditions='+formatjson.otherConditions;
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/difficultApplyManage/query',"困难生名
单信息.xlsx",dataP);
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_ISE").val("0");
layer.close(index);
});
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'del'){
layer.confirm("确定删除数据吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3,
title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultApplyManage/delete',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑 修 改
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/maintain/input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY','ea
syajax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
easyutils.val('layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY',d);
easyutils.checkboxSetV("SPECIAL_TYPE",d.SPECIAL_TYPE);
easyutils.checkboxSetV("APPLY_REASON",d.APPLY_REASON);
//初始化文件
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,false);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'exp'){
var formData="applyUid="+data.APPLY_UID;
layer.confirm("确定导出"+data.STU_NO+"学生的困难生申请表吗？确认请点确定！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/difficultStuManage/expPdf',data.ST
U_NO+"_困难生申请表.docx",formData);
layer.close(index);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID,isView:"1"};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/apply/view','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY','easyaj
ax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY');
//初始化文件
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,false);
if(d.recodeList){
layui.each(d.recodeList, function(index, item){
if(item.DATA_TYPE=='college'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(11,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}else if(item.DATA_TYPE=='counselor'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(10,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}
});
}
});
}
});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','laytpl','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,form = layui.form
,laytpl = layui.laytpl ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
//初始化上传控件界面
easyUpload.initClickFileUploadHtml(0,function successFun(res){
var data={num:0,title:'困难生名单上传'};
layui.laytpl(res.innerHTML).render(data, function(html){
document.getElementById('uploadKnsStuFileId0').innerHTML = html;
});
});
//初始化上传控件
easyUpload.initClickFileUpload(0,'easyfile/difficultApplyManage/importExcel',function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#down_mes_0").html(res.resultinfo);
$("#imp_retfilepath_0").val(res.retfilepath);
$("#resultinfoId_0").show();
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
//导出结果下载
$("#downResButton0").click(function(){
var f = $("#imp_retfilepath_0").val();
if(f!=null && f!=''){
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downResult?fileName=' +f,'impknsmd_result');
}else{
easyutils.layMes('error',"下载文件不存在！");
}
});
$("#downButton").click(function(){
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downTemplate?fileNam
e=support/imp_knsmd.xlsx','imp_knsmd');
});
form.on('select(filter-DIFF-SETUP_UID)', function(data){
layui.$("#U_ONE_PARAM0").val(layui.$("#id-DIFF-SETUP_UID").val());
});
});

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','easyUpload'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils
,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY-formlist');
var selects1=[null,null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY_SELID_COLLEGE',selects1,fu
nction difficultApplyCollCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
});//学院专业班级
var selectsO=[null,null,null];
layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY_SELID_OCOLLEGE',selectsO,f
unction difficultApplyOCollCodeFun(o,d){
layui.$("#Q_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY_SELVALUE_OCOLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
});//学院专业班级
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY',"layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICUL
T_QAPPLY-formlist");
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY_search").click(function(){
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY_ISE").val("0");
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY-formlist');
});
$("#btn_SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'stu_export':
layer.confirm("确定导出全部数据吗？数据过大时，请使用查询条件进行筛选过滤！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY_ISE").val("1");
var
formatjson=easytable.queryWhereFun('layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY-formlist');
var dataP =
'conditions='+formatjson.conditions+'&otherConditions='+formatjson.otherConditions;
easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/difficultApplyManage/query',"困难生名
单信息.xlsx",dataP);
$("#SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY_ISE").val("0");
layer.close(index);
});
break;
case 'stu_school':
var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id)
,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 学 生 在 校 业 务 查 看
",'90%','95%','stu/school/list','layuiadmin-form-STUSCHOOL-formlist',null,null,function
renderDoneFun(d){
if(checkData.length > 0){
layui.$("#STUSCHOOL_STU_NO").val(checkData[0].STU_NO);
layui.$("#STUSCHOOL_THIS_LI_ONE").click();
}
});
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_QAPPLY)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {applyUid:data.APPLY_UID,isView:"1"};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'90%','95%','support/difficult/apply/view','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY','easyaj
ax/difficultStuManage/getApplyMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY');
//初始化文件
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(0,'difficult',d.APPLY_UID,false);
if(d.recodeList){
layui.each(d.recodeList, function(index, item){
if(item.DATA_TYPE=='college'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(11,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}else if(item.DATA_TYPE=='counselor'){
easyUpload.initAllFilesData(10,'modulerecord',item.RECORD_UID,false);
}
});
}
});
}
});
});
</script>

elem: '#difficult-setup-input-laydate'
,type: 'date' ,range: '~' });

successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_setupUid_search").click();//刷新
$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
}
});
});

$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
});
});

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP-formlist');
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP',"layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT _SETUP-formlist");
$("#btn_setupUid_search").click(function(){
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP-formlist');
});
$("#btn_setupUid_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'add':
easyutils.popupWindow(" 添 加
",'50%','65%','support/difficult/setup/input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP',null,n
ull,null);
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'del'){
layer.confirm("确定删除数据吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {setupUid:data.SETUP_UID,dataStatus:'-1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultSetupManage/updateStatus',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_setupUid_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {setupUid:data.SETUP_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑
",'50%','65%','support/difficult/setup/input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP','easy
ajax/difficultSetupManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
} else if(obj.event === 'down'){
layer.confirm("确定关闭该申请通道？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {setupUid:data.SETUP_UID,dataStatus:'0'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultSetupManage/updateStatus',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_setupUid_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'publish'){
layer.confirm("确定启用开通该申请通道？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {setupUid:data.SETUP_UID,dataStatus:'1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultSetupManage/updateStatus',data1,function
successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_setupUid_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
var data1 = {setupUid:data.SETUP_UID};
easyutils.popupViewWindow(" 查 看
",'50%','65%','support/difficult/setup/view','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP','easya
jax/difficultSetupManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
}
});
});
</script><style>
.layui-upload-img{width: 92px; height: 92px; margin: 0 10px 10px 0;}
</style>
<div class="layui-form layui-form-pane"
lay-filter="layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP" >
<fieldset class="layui-elem-field ">
<legend style="color:#393D49;">困难生开通详情信息</legend>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils'], function(){
var $ = layui.$
,table=layui.table
,easytable = layui.easytable
,form = layui.form
,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE-formlist');
var
tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE',"layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_T
YPE-formlist");
$("#btn_DifficultTypeUid_search").click(function(){
easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE-formlist');
});
$("#btn_DifficultTypeUid_reset").click(function(){
easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE-formlist');
form.render(null, 'layadmin-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE-formlist');
});
//头工具栏事件
table.on('toolbar(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE)', function(obj){
switch(obj.event){
case 'add':
//easyutils.popupWindow(" 添 加
",'60%','75%','support/difficult/type/input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE',null,null, null);
break;
};
});
//监听行工具事件
table.on('tool(easy-table-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE)', function(obj){
var data = obj.data;
if(obj.event === 'del'){
layer.confirm("确定删除数据吗？数据删除后将不能恢复，此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {typeUid:data.TYPE_UID,dataStatus:'-1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultTypeManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_DifficultTypeUid_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
} else if(obj.event === 'edit'){
var data1 = {typeUid:data.TYPE_UID};
easyutils.popupWindow(" 编 辑
",'60%','75%','support/difficult/type/input','layuiadmin-form-SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE','easyaja
x/difficultTypeManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
});
} else if(obj.event === 'down'){
layer.confirm("确定注销该信息？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {typeUid:data.TYPE_UID,dataStatus:'0'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultTypeManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_DifficultTypeUid_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
});
} else if(obj.event === 'publish'){
layer.confirm("确定启用该信息？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'}, function(index){
var data1 = {typeUid:data.TYPE_UID,dataStatus:'1'};
easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/difficultTypeManage/updateStatus',data1,function successFun(res){
if(res.success){
$("#btn_DifficultTypeUid_search").click(); //刷新
}
});
layer.close(index);
}
);
}
});
});
</script>

@Plugin(
transcode = "jobsEmployManage", transname = "勤工助学岗位雇用", author = "lcx", createDate = "2021-11-29"
)
@Transactional
public class JobsEmployManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
String isE="0";//是否导出
String jobsSelvalue=null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("JOBS_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
jobsSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("isE".equals(c.getName())) {
isE = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(jobsSelvalue,null);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("PLAN_UID",arrCode[0],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("DEP_UID",arrCode[1],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("JOB_UID",arrCode[2],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.dep.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
roleSql = " COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND
CODE_TYPE='"+RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey()+"') ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("JOB_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_JOBTYPE",true));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE",true));
formats.put("SALARY_UNIT", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_UNIT", "SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT",true));
formats.put("EMPLOY_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("EMPLOY_STATUS", "SYS_WORK_EMPLOY_STATUS"));
// formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("CREATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("CREATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("EMPLOY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("EMPLOY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("LEAVE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("LEAVE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
if(Validate.isEmpty(isE)|| "0".equals(isE)){
formats.put("CREATE_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("CREATE_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));//
}
pager.formatsMap(formats);
//数据导出不进行分页处理
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
pager.setPageSize(-1);
pager.setPageNo(-1);
}
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT T.EMPLOY_UID, T.JOB_UID, T.STU_NO, T.STU_TELEPHONE, T.EMPLOY_DATE, T.LEAVE_DATE, T.EMPLOY_STATUS, T.EMPLOY_REMARK, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE");
sqlBuild.append(" , T.CREATE_UID, T.CREATE_DATE, JI.JOB_NAME, JI.COLLEGE_CODE, JI.SALARY_AMOUNT, JI.SALARY_UNIT, JI.JOB_TYPE, JC.COLLEGE_NAME ,JD.PLAN_TYPE, JD.DEP_UID, JP.PLAN_NAME,JP.PLAN_UID ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
sqlBuild.append(" ,CASE WHEN KNS.KNS_NUM > 0 THEN '是' ELSE '否' END SFKNS
");
}
sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI ON JI.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID
LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE JC ON JC.COLLEGE_CODE = JI.COLLEGE_CODE ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP JD ON JD.DEP_UID=JI.DEP_UID
LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN JP ON JP.PLAN_UID = JD.PLAN_UID ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN (SELECT COUNT(A.STU_NO) AS
KNS_NUM,A.STU_NO FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' GROUP BY A.STU_NO) KNS ON KNS.STU_NO = T.STU_NO ");
}
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.EMPLOY_STATUS!='-1' ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString() , arrayList.toArray());
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
List<HashMap> statisticsList = pager.getDataSource();
exportData(statisticsList, surestream);
}else {
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
}
return true;
}
/**
* 数据导出
* */
public boolean exportData(List<HashMap> statisticsList,ESurestream surestream){
try {
if(statisticsList!=null&&statisticsList.size()>0){
String[] headers={"用工部门/学院","岗位名称","岗位计划","计划类别","岗
位类别","学号","姓名","所在学院"
,"是否困难生","联系电话","报酬标准" ,"是否在岗"};
String[]
column={"COLLEGE_NAME","JOB_NAME","PLAN_NAME","PLAN_TYPE","JOB_TYPE","STU_NO","S
TU_STU_NAME","STU_COLLEGE_NAME", "SFKNS","STU_TELEPHONE","SALARY_AMOUNT","EMPLOY_STATUS_SV"};
String title=" 岗 位 雇 佣 信 息
_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+ ".xlsx";
ExportExcel<HashMap> exp = new ExportExcel<HashMap>();
exp.writeExcel(title, headers, statisticsList, "yyyy-MM-dd", surestream.response(), column);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String employUid = surestream.getString("employUid");
String isView = surestream.getString("isView");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(employUid, "【ID】不能为空");
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.*, JI.JOB_NAME, JI.SALARY_AMOUNT, JI.SALARY_UNIT, JI.JOB_TYPE, JC.COLLEGE_NAME, JI.DEP_UID, D.PLAN_UID
");
if("1".equals(isView)) {
sqlBuild.append(" ,P.PLAN_NAME,P.YEAR_NUM,P.PLAN_TYPE , CASE WHEN
K.KNS_NUM > 0 THEN '是' ELSE '否' END SFKNS ");
}
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI ON JI.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID
LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE JC ON JC.COLLEGE_CODE = JI.COLLEGE_CODE ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D ON D.DEP_UID=JI.DEP_UID ");
if("1".equals(isView)) {
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P ON
P.PLAN_UID=D.PLAN_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN (SELECT COUNT(A.APPLY_UID) AS
KNS_NUM,A.STU_NO FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' GROUP BY A.STU_NO) K ON K.STU_NO=T.STU_NO ");
}
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.EMPLOY_UID =? ");
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("JOB_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_JOBTYPE"));
formats.put("SALARY_UNIT", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_UNIT", "SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT"));
formats.put("EMPLOY_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("EMPLOY_STATUS", "SYS_WORK_EMPLOY_STATUS"));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX"));//性别代码
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK"));
formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("EMPLOY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("EMPLOY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("LEAVE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("LEAVE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE"));
formats.put("CREATE_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("CREATE_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));
formats.put("CREATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("CREATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
HashMap employMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, employUid);
surestream.put("data", employMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String employUid = surestream.getString("EMPLOY_UID");//
String stuNo = surestream.getString("STU_NO");//学号
// Date employDate = surestream.getDate("EMPLOY_DATE");//雇用日期
// Date leaveDate = surestream.getDate("LEAVE_DATE");//离岗日期
String bankName = surestream.getString("BANK_NAME");
String bankCode = surestream.getString("BANK_CODE");//银行账号
String setupSelvalue = surestream.getString("SETUP_SELVALUE");
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(setupSelvalue,null);
if(arrCode ==null || arrCode.length==0) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位信息 ID】不能为空");
}
String jobUid = arrCode[2];//岗位 id
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(jobUid, "【岗位 id】不能为空");
StudentInfo studentInfo = this.get(StudentInfo.class, stuNo);
if(studentInfo==null || Validate.isEmpty(studentInfo.getStuNo())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【学生信息】不存在");
}
WorkstudyJobsInfo info = this.get(WorkstudyJobsInfo.class, jobUid);
if (info == null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位信息】不存在");
}
if(JobsValidateUtils.jobEmployIsEx(getSession(), stuNo, employUid, info.getJobUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, " 【 "+stuNo+" 】 同 学 已 经 在
"+info.getJobName()+"岗位下被录用了！");
}
if(JobsValidateUtils.vaildateNum(getSession(), info, employUid)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位需求人数】已满足！");
}
try{
WorkstudyJobsEmploy employ = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(employUid)) {
employ = this.get(WorkstudyJobsEmploy.class, employUid);
}
//填充值
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(employ)&&!Validate.isEmpty(employ.getEmployUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), employ);
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(employ.getEmployStatus())) {
employ.setEmployStatus("1");
}
employ.setJobUid(info.getJobUid());
employ.setStuNo(studentInfo.getStuNo());
employ.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
employ.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
employ.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
employ.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
employ.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(employ);
} else {
employ = new WorkstudyJobsEmploy();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), employ);
employUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudyemployuid");
employ.setJobUid(info.getJobUid());
employ.setStuNo(studentInfo.getStuNo());
employ.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
employ.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
employ.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
employ.setEmployUid(employUid);
employ.setEmployStatus("1");
employ.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
employ.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
employ.setCreateDate(nowDate);
employ.setCreateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(employ);
}
//更新
studentInfo.setTelNum(employ.getStuTelephone());//电话号码
if(!Validate.isEmpty(bankCode)) {
studentInfo.setBankCode(bankCode);//银行账号
studentInfo.setBankName(bankName);
}
this.update(studentInfo);
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 状态修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean updateStatus(ESurestream surestream) {
String employUids = surestream.getString("employUids");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(employUids, "【ID】不能为空");
if (Validate.isEmpty(dataStatus)) {
dataStatus="0";
}
String leaveDateStr = surestream.getString("LEAVE_DATE");
String employRemark = surestream.getString("EMPLOY_REMARK");
Date leaveDate = null;
if("0".equals(dataStatus)) {
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(leaveDateStr, "【离岗日期】不能为空");
leaveDate = DateUtil.strToDate(leaveDateStr);
}
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, employUids.split(","));
String optUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
Date nowDate = DateSource.getTradedate();
for(String id:uidList){
if(Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
continue;
}
WorkstudyJobsEmploy employ = this.get(WorkstudyJobsEmploy.class, id);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(employ)&&!Validate.isEmpty(employ.getEmployUid())){
employ.setEmployStatus(dataStatus);
if("0".equals(dataStatus)) {
employ.setLeaveDate(leaveDate);
}
if("1".equals(dataStatus)) {
employ.setEmployDate(nowDate);
employ.setLeaveDate(null);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(employRemark)) {
if(!Validate.isEmpty(employ.getEmployRemark())) {
employ.setEmployRemark(employ.getEmployRemark()+"//"+employRemark);
}else {
employ.setEmployRemark(employRemark);
}
}
employ.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
employ.setUpdateUid(optUid);
this.update(employ);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【勤工助学岗位雇用】不存在");
}
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "设置成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 批量删除
* id 以逗号,拼接
* **/
@Route
public boolean delete(ESurestream surestream) {
String employUid = surestream.getString("employUid");
try{
if (!Validate.isEmpty(employUid)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, employUid.split(","));
String optUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
for(String id:uidList){
//判断为空
if(!Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
this.update("UPDATE WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY SET
EMPLOY_STATUS=?, UPDATE_UID=? ,UPDATE_DATE=SYSDATE WHERE EMPLOY_UID=? AND
EMPLOY_STATUS = ? ", DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,optUid,id,"0");
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
//@composite
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "删除成功");
//@output
return true;
}
/**
* 名单导入
* */
@Route
public boolean importExcel(ESurestream surestream) {
HttpServletRequest request=surestream.request();
// HttpServletResponse response=ResponseUtils.getResponse(surestream);
// if (!ServletFileUpload.isMultipartContent(request)) {
// throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897, "Request is not multipart, please
'multipart/form-data' enctype for your form" );
// }
try{
MultipartHttpServletRequest fileRequest = (MultipartHttpServletRequest)request;
for (Iterator<?> it = fileRequest.getFileNames(); it.hasNext();) {
String key = (String) it.next();
MultipartFile multipartFile = fileRequest.getFile(key);
String
filesuffix=UEditorConfigUitl.getFileSuffix(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename());//获取上传文件的
后缀名
if(!".xlsx".equals(filesuffix.toLowerCase())){
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897,"[非.xlsx]类型文件不允许上传");
}
InputStream fileIS = multipartFile.getInputStream();
String excelname = multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().substring(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().indexOf("."));
//得到部署路径
// String rootPath =
SingletonService.getRealPath().replace("/",System.getProperty("file.separator")).replace("\\", System.getProperty("file.separator"));
// excel 列结构
List<ExcelColumn> excelColumns = new ArrayList<ExcelColumn>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(0, "COLLEGE_NAME", "用工部门/学院
"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(1, "JOB_NAME", "岗位名称"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(2, "PLAN_NAME", "岗位计划"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(3, "XH", "学号"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(4, "XM", "姓名"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(5, "YHZH", "中国银行帐号"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(6, "YHZHKHH", "银行开户行"));
ExcelHead head = new ExcelHead();
head.setRowCount(1); // 头所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
List<HashMap> stuList=null;
try {
stuList = ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().importToObjectList(head,
multipartFile.getInputStream());
} catch (Exception e) {
throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897,"导入岗位雇用信息失败" );
}
String stuNo = null;//学号
String stuName = null;//姓名
String collegeName = null;//
String jobName = null;//
String planName = null;//
String yhzh=null,yhzhkhh=null;
int countAdd = 0 ; //新增条数
//int countUpdate = 0;//更新条数
int failcnt = 0;//导入失败计数
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String remark = "";
for(HashMap stuMap : stuList){
remark = "";
int errcnt = 0;
//学号
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XH"))){
stuNo = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XH").trim());
}else{
remark +="学号不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//姓名
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XM"))){
stuName = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XM").trim());
}else{
remark +="姓名不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//用工部门/学院
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("COLLEGE_NAME"))){
collegeName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("COLLEGE_NAME").trim());
}else{
remark +="用工部门/学院不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//岗位名称
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("JOB_NAME"))){
jobName = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("JOB_NAME").trim());
}else{
remark +="岗位名称不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//计划名称
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("PLAN_NAME"))){
planName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("PLAN_NAME").trim());
}else{
remark +="计划名称不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//中国银行卡号
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("YHZH"))){
yhzh = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("YHZH").trim());
}else{
remark +="中国银行卡号不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//开户行
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("YHZHKHH"))){
yhzhkhh = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("YHZHKHH").trim());
yhzhkhh = CacheHolderDicTree.getCodeByName("SYS_DM_BANK",yhzhkhh);
if(Validate.isEmpty(yhzhkhh)) {
remark +="开户行字典数据不存在！";
errcnt++;
}
}else{
remark +="开户行不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
HashMap jobMap = null;
HashMap planMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT PLAN_UID,PLAN_TYPE
FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P WHERE P.PLAN_NAME=? AND P.PLAN_STATUS='1' ", planName);
if(planMap != null) {
HashMap depMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT
D.DEP_UID,D.COLLEGE_CODE FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C
ON C.COLLEGE_CODE = D.COLLEGE_CODE WHERE D.PLAN_UID=? AND C.COLLEGE_NAME=?
AND D.DATA_STATUS=? ", planMap.getString("PLAN_UID"),collegeName,"1");
if(depMap!=null) {
jobMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT
JI.JOB_UID,JI.COLLEGE_CODE FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI WHERE JI.JOB_NAME=? AND
JI.DEP_UID=? AND JI.JOB_STATUS = ? ", jobName, depMap.getString("DEP_UID"),"1");
if(jobMap!=null
&& !Validate.isEmpty(jobMap.getString("JOB_UID"))) {
if(this.existSQL("SELECT EMPLOY_UID FROM
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY P WHERE P.JOB_UID=? AND P.STU_NO=? AND
P.EMPLOY_STATUS!='-1' ", jobMap.getString("JOB_UID"), stuNo)) {
remark +="【" + stuNo + "】 学号的学生已经在【"+
jobName +"】岗位上.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="【" + collegeName + "】 部门/学院的【"+
jobName +"】岗位信息不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="【" + planName + "】计划中该部门或学院的信息
不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="【" + planName + "】计划的信息不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
// if(!this.existSQL("SELECT PLAN_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P
WHERE P.PLAN_NAME=? AND P.PLAN_STATUS='1' ", planName)) {
// remark +="【" + planName + "】计划的信息不存在或未启用.";
// errcnt++;
// }
//效验学号和姓名是否一致
StudentInfo studentInfo = this.get(StudentInfo.class, stuNo);
if(studentInfo!=null) {
if(!stuName.equals(studentInfo.getStuName())) {
remark +="学号【" + stuNo + "】和姓名【"+ stuName +"】对
应的学生不存在.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="学号【" + stuNo + "】的学生信息不存在.";
errcnt++;
}
if(jobMap==null) {
remark +="【" + collegeName + "】 部门/学院的【"+ jobName +"】
岗位信息不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
//没错就进行保存操作
if(errcnt==0) {
try{
WorkstudyJobsEmploy employ = new WorkstudyJobsEmploy();
employ.setEmployUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudyemployuid"));
// employ.setEmployDate(employDate);
// employ.setLeaveDate(leaveDate);
employ.setEmployRemark("导入数据");
employ.setEmployStatus("1");
employ.setJobUid(jobMap.getString("JOB_UID"));
employ.setStuNo(stuNo);
employ.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
employ.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
employ.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
employ.setStuTelephone(studentInfo.getTelNum());
employ.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
employ.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
employ.setCreateDate(nowDate);
employ.setCreateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(employ);
//更新学生银行卡信息
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yhzh)){
studentInfo.setBankName(yhzhkhh);
studentInfo.setBankCode(yhzh);
this.update(studentInfo);
}
remark = "学号[" + stuNo + "]导入成功.";
countAdd++;
}catch (Exception e) {
failcnt++;
}
}else {
failcnt++;
}
stuMap.put("IMPREMARK", remark);
}
String rootPath = Configurations.instance().getString("easy.upload.file.path").replace("/",System.getProperty("file.s
eparator"));
//生成处理结果文件
String zdypath = DicConst.IMPWORKSTUDY_PATH+File.separator;
String excelpath = rootPath + zdypath;;
File fDbfpath =new File(excelpath);
//如果文件夹不存在则创建
if (!fDbfpath.exists() && !fDbfpath.isDirectory()){
Logs.log().info( "[" + excelpath + "]不存在,创建" );
fDbfpath .mkdir();
}
String wdbffilename = DicConst.IMPWORKSTUDY_PATH+"_GWGY_" +
DateSource.getTradedate(CFrame.DatePattern5 ) + excelname;
String wdbffilepath = excelpath + wdbffilename;
String cdbffilepath = zdypath + wdbffilename;
File outputFile = new File(wdbffilepath);
// 需要特殊转换的单元
//Map<String, Map> headMap = new java.util.HashMap<String, Map>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(excelColumns.size(), "IMPREMARK", "导
入提示备注"));
head.setRowCount(1); // 模板中头部所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().exportExcelFile(head, fileIS, outputFile, stuList);
//返回数据
surestream.put("resultinfo", " 导 入 岗 位 雇 用 信 息 处 理 结 果 , 成 功 [" +
countAdd +"]条,失败["+ failcnt +"]条请下载处理结果文件" );
surestream.put("retfilename", wdbffilename);//处理结果文件名
surestream.put("retfilepath", cdbffilepath);//处理结果文件存放路径
}
} catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "导入操作成功");
//@output
return true;
}
}
package com.easy.modules.workstudy;
import java.math.BigDecimal;

@Plugin(
transcode = "jobsInfoManage", transname = "职位信息", author = "lcx", createDate = "2021-11-21"
)
@Transactional
public class JobsInfoManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
String isE="0";//是否导出
String jobsSelvalue=null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("JOBS_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
jobsSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("isE".equals(c.getName())) {
isE = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(jobsSelvalue,null);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("PLAN_UID",arrCode[0],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("DEP_UID",arrCode[1],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.dep.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
roleSql = " COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND
CODE_TYPE='"+RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey()+"') ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
// Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("DATA_STATUS",DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,Condition.noteq,new
JoinCondition("AND"));
// arrayList.add(otherCondition);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("JOB_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE",true));
formats.put("JOB_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_JOBTYPE",true));
formats.put("SALARY_UNIT", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_UNIT", "SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT",true));
formats.put("IS_LIMIT_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("IS_LIMIT_NUM", "SYS_WHETHER"));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
if(Validate.isEmpty(isE)|| "0".equals(isE)){
formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("UPDATE_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));//
}
pager.formatsMap(formats);
//数据导出不进行分页处理
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
pager.setPageSize(-1);
pager.setPageNo(-1);
}
String sql = "SELECT T.* FROM (SELECT T.JOB_UID, T.JOB_NAME, T.COLLEGE_CODE, T.DEP_UID, T.NEED_NUM, T.JOB_TYPE, T.SALARY_AMOUNT, T.SALARY_UNIT, T.IS_LIMIT_NUM, T.JOB_STATUS, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_TIME " + " , C.COLLEGE_NAME,D.PLAN_UID ,P.PLAN_NAME,P.YEAR_NUM,P.PLAN_TYPE" + " ,(SELECT COUNT(E.EMPLOY_UID) FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY E
WHERE E.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID AND E.EMPLOY_STATUS='1' ) AS ZGRS" + " ,(SELECT COUNT(E.EMPLOY_UID) FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY E
WHERE E.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID AND E.EMPLOY_STATUS='0' ) AS LGRS " + " ,(SELECT SUM(S.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT) FROM
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY S WHERE S.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID AND S.SALARY_STATUS='2' ) AS YJSJE
" + " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO T LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D
ON D.DEP_UID = T.DEP_UID " + " LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P ON P.PLAN_UID = D.PLAN_UID " + " LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON C.COLLEGE_CODE = T.COLLEGE_CODE
WHERE T.JOB_STATUS!='-1' ) T ";
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sql, arrayList.toArray());
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
List<HashMap> statisticsList = pager.getDataSource();
exportData(statisticsList, surestream);
}else {
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
}
return true;
}
/**
* 数据导出
* */
public boolean exportData(List<HashMap> statisticsList,ESurestream surestream){
try {
if(statisticsList!=null&&statisticsList.size()>0){
String[] headers={"用工部门/学院","岗位名称","岗位计划","计划类别","岗
位类别","计划人数","在岗人数","离岗人数","已结算金额","薪资金额","薪资标准","操作人"," 操作时间"};
String[]
column={"COLLEGE_NAME","JOB_NAME","PLAN_NAME","PLAN_TYPE","JOB_TYPE","NEED_NUM
","ZGRS","LGRS","YJSJE","SALARY_AMOUNT","SALARY_UNIT","UPDATE_UID","UPDATE_TIME"};
String title="岗位信息_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+
".xlsx";
ExportExcel<HashMap> exp = new ExportExcel<HashMap>();
exp.writeExcel(title, headers, statisticsList, "yyyy-MM-dd", surestream.response(), column);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String jobUid = surestream.getString("jobUid");
String isView = surestream.getString("isView");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(jobUid, "【ID】不能为空");
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("JOB_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("JOB_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_JOBTYPE"));
formats.put("SALARY_UNIT", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_UNIT", "SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT"));
formats.put("IS_LIMIT_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("IS_LIMIT_NUM", "SYS_WHETHER"));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("UPDATE_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));//
String sql = " SELECT T.*, P.PLAN_UID, P.PLAN_NAME, P.YEAR_NUM,C.COLLEGE_NAME,J.YJSJE,J.COUNT_IDS," + " ( SELECT COUNT(E.EMPLOY_UID) FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY E
WHERE E.EMPLOY_STATUS='1' AND E.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID ) AS EMPLOY_NUM, " + " ( SELECT COUNT(E.EMPLOY_UID) FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY E
WHERE E.EMPLOY_STATUS='0' AND E.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID ) AS UNEMPLOY_NUM " + " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO T LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D
ON D.DEP_UID = T.DEP_UID " + " LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P ON P.PLAN_UID = D.PLAN_UID " + " LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON C.COLLEGE_CODE = D.COLLEGE_CODE" + " LEFT JOIN (SELECT SUM(JS.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT) AS
YJSJE,JS.JOB_UID,COUNT(JS.SALARY_UID) AS COUNT_IDS FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY JS
WHERE JS.SALARY_STATUS !='0' GROUP BY JS.JOB_UID) J ON J.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID " + " WHERE T.JOB_UID = ? ";
HashMap infoMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sql, formats, jobUid);
if("1".equals(isView) && infoMap!=null) {
formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("EMPLOY_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("EMPLOY_STATUS", "SYS_WORK_EMPLOY_STATUS",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR",
"SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX"));//性别代码
formats.put("EMPLOY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("EMPLOY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("LEAVE_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("LEAVE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* , CASE WHEN
K.KNS_NUM > 0 THEN '是' ELSE '否' END SFKNS ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN (SELECT COUNT(A.APPLY_UID) AS
KNS_NUM,A.STU_NO FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' GROUP BY A.STU_NO) K ON K.STU_NO=T.STU_NO ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.JOB_UID =? AND T.EMPLOY_STATUS!='-1' ");
try {
List<HashMap> employList = this.jdbcQueryByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, jobUid);
infoMap.put("employList", employList);
} catch (SQLException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
surestream.put("data", infoMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if(!AccountPowerUtils.isRole(getSession(), optUid, RoleUidEnum.role_workstudy.getKey())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "您没有操作岗位信息修改或新增的权限！");
}
String jobUid = surestream.getString("JOB_UID");//
String jobName = surestream.getString("JOB_NAME");//职位(岗位)名称
String salaryAmount = surestream.getString("SALARY_AMOUNT");
String setupSelvalue = surestream.getString("SETUP_SELVALUE");
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(setupSelvalue,null);
if(arrCode ==null || arrCode.length==0) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位计划】不能为空");
}
String depUid = arrCode[1];//岗位计划部门 id
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(depUid, "【岗位计划部门】不能为空");
WorkstudyJobsDep dep = this.get(WorkstudyJobsDep.class, depUid);
if(dep==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位计划部门信息】不存在");
}
if(JobsValidateUtils.jobNameIsEx(getSession(), jobName, jobUid, dep.getDepUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位名称】已存在");
}
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(salaryAmount, "【薪资金额】不能为空");
if(new BigDecimal(salaryAmount).compareTo(new BigDecimal("999999.99")) > 0){
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【薪资金额】请在限制在 100 万以内");
}
try{
WorkstudyJobsInfo info = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(jobUid)) {
info = this.get(WorkstudyJobsInfo.class, jobUid);
}
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(info)&&!Validate.isEmpty(info.getJobUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), info);
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(info.getJobStatus())) {
info.setJobStatus("1");
}
info.setDepUid(dep.getDepUid());
info.setCollegeCode(dep.getCollegeCode());
info.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
info.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(info);
} else {
info = new WorkstudyJobsInfo();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), info);
jobUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudyinfouid");
info.setJobUid(jobUid);
info.setDepUid(dep.getDepUid());
info.setCollegeCode(dep.getCollegeCode());
info.setJobStatus("1");
info.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
info.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(info);
}
CacheHolderString.remData(CacheHolderString.DIC_LIST_JOBSINFO);
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 状态修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean updateStatus(ESurestream surestream) {
String jobUid = surestream.getString("jobUid");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(jobUid, "【ID】不能为空");
if (Validate.isEmpty(dataStatus)) {
dataStatus="0";
}
WorkstudyJobsInfo info = this.get(WorkstudyJobsInfo.class, jobUid);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(info)&&!Validate.isEmpty(info.getJobUid())){
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(dataStatus)) {
if(this.existSQL("SELECT D.JOB_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY D
WHERE D.JOB_UID=? ", info.getJobUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位信息】已被使用，不能删
除");
}
}
info.setJobStatus(dataStatus);
info.setUpdateTime(DateSource.getTradedate());
info.setUpdateUid(Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream));
this.update(info);
CacheHolderString.remData(CacheHolderString.DIC_LIST_JOBSINFO);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位信息】不存在");
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "设置成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 获取岗位信息数据
* */
@Route
public boolean getJobsInfoList(ESurestream surestream){
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
// String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
@SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
List<HashMap> dicList= null;//(List<HashMap>)
CacheHolderString.getValue(CacheHolderString.DIC_LIST_JOBSINFO);
if(dicList==null) {
dicList = JobsDataUtils.getJobsInfoList(this.getSession(), roleType ,optUid);
}
surestream.put("data", dicList);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"成功");
return true;
}
}
