@Plugin(
transcode = "jobsPlanManage", transname = "勤工助学岗位计划", author = "lcx", createDate = "2021-11-21"
)
@Transactional
public class JobsPlanManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("PLAN_STATUS",DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,Condition.noteq,new
JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("PLAN_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE"));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("UPDATE_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));//
pager.formatsMap(formats);
String sql = "SELECT T.PLAN_UID, T.PLAN_NAME, T.YEAR_NUM, T.PLAN_TYPE, T.PLAN_STATUS, T.PLAN_REMARK, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE FROM
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN T ";
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sql, arrayList.toArray());
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String planUid = surestream.getString("planUid");
String isView = surestream.getString("isView");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(planUid, "【ID】不能为空");
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("PLAN_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE"));
HashMap planMap = this.queryForMapByFormat("SELECT T.* FROM
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN T WHERE T.PLAN_UID =? ", formats, planUid);
if("1".equals(isView) && planMap!=null) {
formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("DATA_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("DATA_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE"));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
String sql = "SELECT T.*, C.COLLEGE_NAME, P.PLAN_NAME, P.YEAR_NUM, JS.SETTLE_AMOUNTS " + " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP T LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN
P ON P.PLAN_UID=T.PLAN_UID LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON
C.COLLEGE_CODE=T.COLLEGE_CODE " + " LEFT JOIN ( SELECT SUM(JS.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT) AS
SETTLE_AMOUNTS,JI.DEP_UID " + " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY JS LEFT JOIN
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI ON JI.JOB_UID=JS.JOB_UID " + " WHERE JS.SALARY_STATUS='2' GROUP BY JI.DEP_UID ) JS ON
JS.DEP_UID=T.DEP_UID "+ " WHERE T.PLAN_UID=? ORDER BY C.COLLEGE_NAME DESC ";
try {
List<HashMap> depList = this.jdbcQueryByFormat(sql, formats, planUid);
planMap.put("depList", depList);
} catch (SQLException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
surestream.put("data", planMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String planUid = surestream.getString("PLAN_UID");//
String yearNum = surestream.getString("YEAR_NUM");
String planType = surestream.getString("PLAN_TYPE");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(yearNum, "【年份】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(planType, "【类型】不能为空");
if(JobsValidateUtils.planIsEx(getSession(), yearNum, planType, planUid)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【相同年份和类型的岗位计划】已存在，
不能重复添加！");
}
try{
WorkstudyJobsPlan plan = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(planUid)) {
plan = this.get(WorkstudyJobsPlan.class, planUid);
}
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(plan)&&!Validate.isEmpty(plan.getPlanUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), plan);
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(plan.getPlanStatus())) {
plan.setPlanStatus("1");
}
plan.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
plan.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(plan);
} else {
plan = new WorkstudyJobsPlan();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), plan);
planUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudyplanuid");
plan.setPlanUid(planUid);
plan.setPlanStatus("1");
plan.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
plan.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(plan);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 状态修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean updateStatus(ESurestream surestream) {
String planUid = surestream.getString("planUid");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(planUid, "【ID】不能为空");
if (Validate.isEmpty(dataStatus)) {
dataStatus="0";
}
WorkstudyJobsPlan plan = this.get(WorkstudyJobsPlan.class, planUid);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(plan)&&!Validate.isEmpty(plan.getPlanUid())){
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(dataStatus)) {
if(this.existSQL("SELECT PLAN_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D WHERE
D.PLAN_UID=? AND D.DATA_STATUS!='-1' ", plan.getPlanUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位计划】已被使用，不能删
除");
}
}
plan.setPlanStatus(dataStatus);
plan.setUpdateDate(DateSource.getTradedate());
plan.setUpdateUid(Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream));
this.update(plan);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位计划信息】不存在");
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "设置成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean queryDep(ESurestream surestream) {
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("DATA_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("DATA_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
String sql = "SELECT T.* FROM (SELECT JS.SETTLE_AMOUNTS,T.DEP_UID, T.PLAN_UID, T.COLLEGE_CODE, T.JOB_NUMS, T.PLAN_TYPE, T.ALL_AMOUNTS, T.DATA_STATUS, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_TIME,C.COLLEGE_NAME " + " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP T LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON
C.COLLEGE_CODE=T.COLLEGE_CODE" + " LEFT JOIN ( SELECT SUM(JS.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT) AS
SETTLE_AMOUNTS,JI.DEP_UID " + " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY JS LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO
JI ON JI.JOB_UID=JS.JOB_UID " + " WHERE JS.SALARY_STATUS='2' GROUP BY JI.DEP_UID ) JS ON
JS.DEP_UID=T.DEP_UID " + " WHERE T.DATA_STATUS!='-1' ) T ";
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sql, arrayList.toArray());
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}

HH:mm:ss"));
String sql = "SELECT T.*, C.COLLEGE_NAME, P.PLAN_NAME, P.YEAR_NUM " + " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP T LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P
ON P.PLAN_UID=T.PLAN_UID LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON
C.COLLEGE_CODE=T.COLLEGE_CODE WHERE T.DEP_UID=? ";

/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdateDep(ESurestream surestream) {
String depUid = surestream.getString("DEP_UID");//
String planUid = surestream.getString("PLAN_UID");//
WorkstudyJobsPlan plan = this.get(WorkstudyJobsPlan.class, planUid);
try{
WorkstudyJobsDep dep = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(depUid)) {
dep = this.get(WorkstudyJobsDep.class, depUid);
}
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(dep)&&!Validate.isEmpty(dep.getDepUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), dep);
dep.setPlanType(plan.getPlanType());
dep.setPlanUid(plan.getPlanUid());
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(dep.getDataStatus())) {
dep.setDataStatus("1");
}
dep.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
dep.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(dep);
} else {
dep = new WorkstudyJobsDep();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), dep);
depUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudydepuid");
dep.setDepUid(depUid);
dep.setPlanUid(plan.getPlanUid());
dep.setPlanType(plan.getPlanType());
dep.setDataStatus("1");
dep.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
dep.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(dep);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 状态修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean updateDepStatus(ESurestream surestream) {
String depUid = surestream.getString("depUid");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(depUid, "【ID】不能为空");
if (Validate.isEmpty(dataStatus)) {
dataStatus="0";
}
WorkstudyJobsDep dep = this.get(WorkstudyJobsDep.class, depUid);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(dep)&&!Validate.isEmpty(dep.getDepUid())){
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(dataStatus)) {
if(this.existSQL("SELECT JOB_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO D WHERE
D.DEP_UID=? AND D.JOB_STATUS!='-1' ", dep.getDepUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位计划部门】已被使用，不
能删除");
}
}
dep.setDataStatus(dataStatus);
dep.setUpdateTime(DateSource.getTradedate());
dep.setUpdateUid(Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream));
this.update(dep);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【职位计划部门信息】不存在");
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "设置成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 获取岗位计划及岗位部门学院数据
* */
@Route
public boolean getJobsPlanList(ESurestream surestream){
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
@SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
List<HashMap> dicList = null;//(List<HashMap>)
CacheHolderString.getValue(CacheHolderString.DIC_LIST_JOBSPLAN);
if(dicList==null) {
dicList = JobsDataUtils.getJobsPlanList(this.getSession(), roleType ,optUid);
}
surestream.put("data", dicList);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"成功");
return true;
}
//审核流程复制
@Route
public boolean copyPlan(ESurestream surestream) {
String copyUid = surestream.getString("COPY_PLAN_UID");
String planName = surestream.getString("PLAN_NAME");//
String yearNum = surestream.getString("YEAR_NUM");
String planRemark = surestream.getString("PLAN_REMARK");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(copyUid, "【被复制计划的 ID】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(planName, "【新计划名称】不能为空");
WorkstudyJobsPlan plan = this.get(WorkstudyJobsPlan.class, copyUid);
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(plan)&&!Validate.isEmpty(plan.getPlanUid())){
WorkstudyJobsPlan newPlan = new WorkstudyJobsPlan();
newPlan.setPlanUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudyplanuid"));
newPlan.setPlanName(planName);
newPlan.setPlanRemark(planRemark);
newPlan.setPlanType(plan.getPlanType());
newPlan.setYearNum(yearNum);
newPlan.setPlanStatus("1");
newPlan.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
newPlan.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
List<WorkstudyJobsDep> depList = this.findMultiple(WorkstudyJobsDep.class, DBCondition.form("dataStatus","1"), DBCondition.form("planUid",plan.getPlanUid()));
for(WorkstudyJobsDep dep:depList) {
WorkstudyJobsDep newDep = new WorkstudyJobsDep();
BeanUtils.copyProperties(dep, newDep);
newDep.setPlanUid(newPlan.getPlanUid());
newDep.setDepUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudydepuid"));
newDep.setAllAmounts(null);
// newDep.setJobNums(null);
newDep.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
newDep.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
// newDep.setDataStatus("1");
List<WorkstudyJobsInfo> infoList = this.findMultiple(WorkstudyJobsInfo.class, DBCondition.form("jobStatus","1"), DBCondition.form("depUid",dep.getDepUid()));
if(infoList!=null) {
for(WorkstudyJobsInfo info:infoList) {
WorkstudyJobsInfo newInfo = new WorkstudyJobsInfo();
BeanUtils.copyProperties(info, newInfo);
newInfo.setDepUid(newDep.getDepUid());
newInfo.setJobUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudyinfouid"));
newInfo.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
newInfo.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
// newInfo.setJobStatus("1");
List<WorkstudyJobsEmploy> employList =
this.findMultiple(WorkstudyJobsEmploy.class, Restrictions.ne("employStatus", "-1"), DBCondition.form("jobUid",info.getJobUid()));
if(employList!=null && employList.size()>0) {
for(WorkstudyJobsEmploy employI:employList) {
WorkstudyJobsEmploy newEmploy = new
WorkstudyJobsEmploy();
BeanUtils.copyProperties(employI, newEmploy);
newEmploy.setEmployUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudyjobuid"));
newEmploy.setJobUid(newInfo.getJobUid());
newEmploy.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
newEmploy.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
// newEmploy.setEmployStatus("1");
this.save(newEmploy);
}
}
this.save(newInfo);
}
}
this.save(newDep);
}
this.save(newPlan);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【被复制的计划信息】不存在");
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "复制操作成功");
return true;
}
}

@Plugin(
transcode = "jobsSalaryManage", transname = "勤工助学_岗位薪资结算", author = "lcx", createDate = "2021-11-29"
)
@Transactional
public class JobsSalaryManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
String isE="0";//是否导出
String isET = "0";
String jobsSelvalue=null;
String yearMonth = null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("JOBS_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
jobsSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("YEAR_MONTH".equals(c.getName())) {
yearMonth = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("isE".equals(c.getName())) {
isE = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("isET".equals(c.getName())) {
isET = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
String[] yearMonthCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(yearMonth,"-");
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(jobsSelvalue,null);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("PLAN_UID",arrCode[0],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("DEP_UID",arrCode[1],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("JOB_UID",arrCode[2],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.dep.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
roleSql = " COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND
CODE_TYPE='"+RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey()+"') ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("JOB_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_JOBTYPE",true));
formats.put("PLAN_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("PLAN_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_PLANTYPE",true));
formats.put("SALARY_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_STATUS", "SYS_WORK_SALARY_STATUS"));
formats.put("SALARY_UNIT", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_UNIT", "SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT",true));
formats.put("MONTH_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("MONTH_NUM", "SYS_MONTH_NUM"));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("END_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("SUBMIT_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("SUBMIT_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
if(Validate.isEmpty(isE)|| "0".equals(isE)){
formats.put("SUBMIT_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("SUBMIT_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));//
formats.put("SETTLEMENT_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("SETTLEMENT_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));//
}
formats.put("SETTLEMENT_TIME", new
FormatDate2Str("SETTLEMENT_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK",true));//开户行
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
//数据导出不进行分页处理
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
pager.setPageSize(-1);
pager.setPageNo(-1);
}
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT T.SALARY_UID, T.JOB_UID, T.STU_NO, T.YEAR_NUM, T.MONTH_NUM, T.BEGIN_DATE, T.END_DATE, T.SALARY_AMOUNT, T.SALARY_UNIT, T.SALARY_TIMES, T.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT, T.SALARY_STATUS, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_TIME, T.SUBMIT_UID, T.SUBMIT_TIME, T.SETTLEMENT_UID, T.SETTLEMENT_TIME");
sqlBuild.append(" ,JI.JOB_NAME, JI.COLLEGE_CODE, JI.JOB_TYPE, JC.COLLEGE_NAME, D.DEP_UID,D.PLAN_UID ,D.PLAN_TYPE,JP.PLAN_NAME ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
sqlBuild.append(" ,CASE WHEN KNS.KNS_NUM > 0 THEN '是' ELSE '否' END SFKNS
");
}
sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI ON JI.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID
LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE JC ON JC.COLLEGE_CODE = JI.COLLEGE_CODE ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D ON D.DEP_UID =JI.DEP_UID
LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN JP ON JP.PLAN_UID = D.PLAN_UID");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN (SELECT COUNT(A.STU_NO) AS
KNS_NUM,A.STU_NO FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' GROUP BY A.STU_NO) KNS ON KNS.STU_NO = T.STU_NO ");
}
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.SALARY_STATUS!='-1' ");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yearMonthCode[1])) {
String ye = yearMonthCode[0].trim();
String mon = yearMonthCode[1].replaceAll("^(0+)", "").trim();
sqlBuild.append(" AND
TO_DATE(T.YEAR_NUM||'-'||T.MONTH_NUM,'YYYY-MM') >=
TO_DATE('"+ye+"-"+mon+"','YYYY-MM') ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yearMonthCode[3])) {
String ye = yearMonthCode[2].trim();
String mon = yearMonthCode[3].replaceAll("^(0+)", "").trim();
sqlBuild.append(" AND TO_DATE(T.YEAR_NUM||'-'||T.MONTH_NUM,'YYYY-MM')
<= TO_DATE('"+ye+"-"+mon+"','YYYY-MM') ");
}
sqlBuild.append(" ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
List<HashMap> statisticsList = pager.getDataSource();
if(statisticsList!=null && statisticsList.size()>0 && !Validate.isEmpty(isET) &&
"1".equals(isET)) {
HashMap onemap = statisticsList.get(0);
BigDecimal totalB = BigDecimal.ZERO;
for(HashMap smap:statisticsList) {
smap.put("QZQR_TEMP", "");
onemap.getString("COLLEGE_NAME");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(smap.getString("SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT"))) {
totalB=totalB.add(new
BigDecimal(smap.getString("SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT")));
}
}
//拼凑文档参数
Map<String, Object> dataMap = new java.util.HashMap<String, Object>();
// dataMap 对应的是模板中 {字段名}格式
dataMap.put("TITLE", onemap.getString("COLLEGE_NAME")+onemap.getString("YEAR_NUM")+" 年
"+onemap.getString("MONTH_NUM_SV"));//标题
dataMap.put("TOTAL_AMOUNT", totalB.toString());//合计总额
try {
String filePath =
SingletonService.getRealPath()+"template//workstudy//exp_khb.xlsx";
TemplateExcelUtil.templateExcelExport(surestream.response(),dataMap.get("TITLE")+" 勤 工
助学考核表.xlsx",filePath,dataMap,statisticsList);
} catch (IOException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
}else {
exportData(statisticsList, surestream);
}
}else {
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
}
return true;
}
/**
* 数据导出
* */
public boolean exportData(List<HashMap> statisticsList,ESurestream surestream){
try {
if(statisticsList!=null&&statisticsList.size()>0){
// String[] headers={"学号","姓名","开户行","银行卡号","是否困难生","年"," 总金额"};
// String[]
column={"STU_NO","STU_STU_NAME","STU_BANK_NAME","STU_BANK_CODE","SFKNS","YEAR_ NUM","SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT"};
String[] headers={"学号","姓名","用工部门/学院","岗位名称","开户行","银
行卡号","是否困难生","年","月" ,"总金额"};
String[]
column={"STU_NO","STU_STU_NAME","COLLEGE_NAME","JOB_NAME","STU_BANK_NAME","ST
U_BANK_CODE","SFKNS","YEAR_NUM","MONTH_NUM_SV","SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT"};
String title=" 岗 位 薪 资 结 算 单
_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+ ".xlsx";
ExportExcel<HashMap> exp = new ExportExcel<HashMap>();
exp.writeExcel(title, headers, statisticsList, "yyyy-MM-dd", surestream.response(), column);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getInitMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String stuNo = surestream.getString("stuNo");
String jobUid = surestream.getString("jobUid");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学号】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(jobUid, "【岗位 ID】不能为空");
HashMap stuMap = StuDataUtils.getStuMapByNo(getSession(), stuNo);
if(stuMap==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【学生信息】不存在");
}
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("JOB_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("JOB_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_JOBTYPE"));
formats.put("SALARY_UNIT", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_UNIT", "SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT"));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss"));
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK",true));//开户行
String sql = " SELECT T.*, P.PLAN_UID, P.PLAN_NAME, P.YEAR_NUM,C.COLLEGE_NAME " + " FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO T LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D
ON D.DEP_UID = T.DEP_UID " + " LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P ON P.PLAN_UID = D.PLAN_UID " + " LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON C.COLLEGE_CODE = D.COLLEGE_CODE
WHERE T.JOB_UID = ? ";
HashMap infoMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sql, formats, jobUid);
if(infoMap==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位信息】不存在");
}
stuMap.putAll(infoMap);
stuMap.put("STU_NO", stuNo);
surestream.put("data", stuMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"获取成功");
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String salaryUid = surestream.getString("salaryUid");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(salaryUid, "【ID】不能为空");
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("JOB_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("JOB_TYPE", new FormatDic2Str("JOB_TYPE", "SYS_WORK_JOBTYPE"));
formats.put("SALARY_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_STATUS", "SYS_WORK_SALARY_STATUS"));
formats.put("SALARY_UNIT", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_UNIT", "SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT"));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss"));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX"));//性别代码
formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("END_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK"));//开户行
formats.put("MONTH_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("MONTH_NUM", "SYS_MONTH_NUM"));
formats.put("SUBMIT_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("SUBMIT_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("SETTLEMENT_TIME", new
FormatDate2Str("SETTLEMENT_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("SUBMIT_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("SUBMIT_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));
formats.put("SETTLEMENT_UID", new
FormatAccountId2Name("SETTLEMENT_UID",null,this.getSession(),true));
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.*, P.PLAN_UID, P.PLAN_NAME, P.YEAR_NUM, C.COLLEGE_NAME,JI.JOB_NAME,JI.SALARY_AMOUNT,JI.SALARY_UNIT,JI.JOB_TYPE
");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY T LEFT JOIN
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI ON JI.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D ON D.DEP_UID = JI.DEP_UID
LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P ON P.PLAN_UID = D.PLAN_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON C.COLLEGE_CODE =
D.COLLEGE_CODE");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.SALARY_UID =? ");
HashMap salaryMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, salaryUid);
surestream.put("data", salaryMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String salaryUid = surestream.getString("SALARY_UID");//
String jobUid = surestream.getString("JOB_UID");//岗位信息 ID
String stuNo = surestream.getString("STU_NO");//学号
Double salaryTimes = surestream.getDouble("SALARY_TIMES");//劳作时长(结算时长)
Double salaryAllAmount = surestream.getDouble("SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT");//劳作总
金额
String yearNum = surestream.getString("YEAR_NUM");//年份
String monthNum = surestream.getString("MONTH_NUM");//月份
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(jobUid, "【岗位 ID】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(yearNum, "【年份】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(monthNum, "【月份】不能为空");
StudentInfo studentInfo = this.get(StudentInfo.class, stuNo);
if(studentInfo==null || Validate.isEmpty(studentInfo.getStuNo())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【学生信息】不存在");
}
WorkstudyJobsInfo jobInfo = this.get(WorkstudyJobsInfo.class, jobUid);
if (jobInfo==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位信息】不存在");
}
//判断是否在岗位上
if(!this.existSQL("SELECT EMPLOY_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY P WHERE
P.JOB_UID=? AND P.STU_NO=? AND P.EMPLOY_STATUS='1' ", jobUid, stuNo)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【" + stuNo + "】 学号的学生不在【"+
jobInfo.getJobName() +"】岗位上.");
}
WorkstudyJobsDep dep = this.get(WorkstudyJobsDep.class, jobInfo.getDepUid());
if (dep==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位对应计划部门信息】不存在");
}
WorkstudyJobsPlan plan = this.get(WorkstudyJobsPlan.class, dep.getPlanUid());
if (plan==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位对应的计划】不存在");
}
if(!plan.getYearNum().equals(yearNum)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位对应计划所属年份】和【工资条的
年份】不一致，请核对") ;
}
if(this.existSQL("SELECT P.SALARY_UID FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY P WHERE
P.JOB_UID=? AND P.STU_NO=? AND P.YEAR_NUM=? AND P.MONTH_NUM=? AND
P.SALARY_STATUS!='-1' ",
jobUid,stuNo,yearNum,monthNum)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, " 【 " + stuNo + " 】 学 号 的 学 生 【 "+
jobInfo.getJobName() +"】岗位【"+ yearNum +"】年【"+ monthNum +"】月薪资条已存在.");
}
Double salaryAllAmountJs = jobInfo.getSalaryAmount()*salaryTimes;
BigDecimal c1 = new BigDecimal(salaryAllAmount);
BigDecimal c2 = new BigDecimal(salaryAllAmountJs);
if(c1.compareTo(c2) !=0) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【页面计算的总金额】与【后台计算的总
金额】不一致！请核实！");
}
//1 学院， 2 部门 , 如果是学院才判断
if("1".equals(dep.getPlanType())) {
BaseSysCollege baseSysCollege = this.get(BaseSysCollege.class, dep.getCollegeCode());
if (baseSysCollege == null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【学院信息】不存在");
}
String jsSql = "SELECT COUNT(T.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT) AS
SALARY_AMOUNTS,D.DEP_UID,D.ALL_AMOUNTS AS PLAN_AMOUNTS " +
" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY T LEFT JOIN
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI ON JI.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID " +
" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D ON D.DEP_UID =JI.DEP_UID " +
" WHERE T.JOB_UID =? AND (T.SALARY_STATUS=1 OR
T.SALARY_STATUS=2) " +
" GROUP BY D.DEP_UID,D.ALL_AMOUNTS ";
//查询岗位计划机构的结算情况
HashMap jsMap = super.queryForMap(jsSql, jobInfo.getJobUid());
//计划机构的总金额
BigDecimal planAmountsB = BigDecimal.ZERO;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(dep.getAllAmounts())){
planAmountsB = new BigDecimal(dep.getAllAmounts());
}
//已用金额
BigDecimal salaryAmountsB = BigDecimal.ZERO;
if(jsMap!=null && !Validate.isEmpty(jsMap.getString("SALARY_AMOUNTS"))){
salaryAmountsB = new BigDecimal(jsMap.getString("SALARY_AMOUNTS"));
}
// //计划机构的总金额
// Double planAmounts = 0.0D;;
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(jsMap.getString("PLAN_AMOUNTS"))) {
// planAmounts = Double.valueOf(jsMap.getString("PLAN_AMOUNTS"));
// }else {
// throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897,baseSysCollege.getCollegeName()+ "【岗
位计划】的预算不存在");
// }
// //已用金额
// Double salaryAmounts = 0.0D;
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(jsMap.getString("SALARY_AMOUNTS"))) {
// salaryAmounts = Double.valueOf(jsMap.getString("SALARY_AMOUNTS"));
// }
// BigDecimal planAmountsB = new BigDecimal(planAmounts.toString());
// BigDecimal salaryAmountsB = new BigDecimal(salaryAmounts.toString());
// BigDecimal syje = b1.subtract(b2);//剩余金额
// if(syje < salaryAllAmount){
// String mes ="【" + baseSysCollege.getCollegeName() + "】 学院的可用的计
划金额，不足以制此工资，学院的计划金额为【"+ planAmounts +"】元,学院已经使用【"+
salaryAmounts +"】元,剩余金额为【"+ syje +"】元,此条工资总的劳作金额为【"+ salaryAllAmount
+"】元";
// throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, mes);
// }
BigDecimal syje = planAmountsB.subtract(salaryAmountsB);//剩余金额
if(syje.compareTo(c2)==-1){
String mes ="【" + baseSysCollege.getCollegeName() + "】 学院的可用的计
划金额，不足以制此工资，学院的计划金额为【"+ planAmountsB.doubleValue() +"】元,学院
已经使用【"+ salaryAmountsB.doubleValue() +"】元,剩余金额为【"+ syje +"】元,此条工资总
的劳作金额为【"+ salaryAllAmount +"】元";
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, mes);
}
}
try{
WorkstudyJobsSalary salary = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(salaryUid)) {
salary = this.get(WorkstudyJobsSalary.class, salaryUid);
}
//填充值
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(salary)&&!Validate.isEmpty(salary.getSalaryUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), salary);
if(Validate.isEmpty(salary.getSalaryStatus())) {
salary.setSalaryStatus("1");
}
salary.setSalaryAmount(jobInfo.getSalaryAmount());
salary.setSalaryUnit(jobInfo.getSalaryUnit());
salary.setStuNo(studentInfo.getStuNo());
salary.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
salary.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
salary.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
salary.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
salary.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(salary);
} else {
salary = new WorkstudyJobsSalary();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), salary);
salaryUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudysalaryuid");
salary.setSalaryUid(salaryUid);
salary.setStuNo(studentInfo.getStuNo());
salary.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
salary.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
salary.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
salary.setSalaryAmount(jobInfo.getSalaryAmount());
salary.setSalaryUnit(jobInfo.getSalaryUnit());
salary.setSalaryStatus("1");//0 草稿 1 待结算 2 已结算
salary.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
salary.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
salary.setSubmitUid(optAccountUid);
salary.setSubmitTime(nowDate);
this.save(salary);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 状态修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean updateStatus(ESurestream surestream) {
String salaryUid = surestream.getString("salaryUid");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(salaryUid, "【ID】不能为空");
if (Validate.isEmpty(dataStatus)) {
dataStatus="0";
}
WorkstudyJobsSalary salary = this.get(WorkstudyJobsSalary.class, salaryUid);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(salary)&&!Validate.isEmpty(salary.getSalaryUid())){
salary.setSalaryStatus(dataStatus);
salary.setUpdateTime(DateSource.getTradedate());
salary.setUpdateUid(Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream));
this.update(salary);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【岗位薪资结算信息】不存在");
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "设置成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 批量结算
* **/
@Route
public boolean batchSettle(ESurestream surestream) {
String salaryUids = surestream.getString("salaryUids");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(salaryUids, "【ID】不能为空");
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, salaryUids.split(","));
String optUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
Date nowDate = DateSource.getTradedate();
for(String id:uidList){
if(Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
continue;
}
WorkstudyJobsSalary salary = this.get(WorkstudyJobsSalary.class, id);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(salary)&&!Validate.isEmpty(salary.getSalaryUid()) &&
"1".equals(salary.getSalaryStatus())){
salary.setSalaryStatus("2");
salary.setSettlementTime(nowDate);
salary.setSettlementUid(optUid);
salary.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
salary.setUpdateUid(optUid);
this.update(salary);
}
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "设置成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 批量删除
* id 以逗号,拼接
* **/
@Route
public boolean delete(ESurestream surestream) {
String salaryUid = surestream.getString("salaryUid");
try{
if (!Validate.isEmpty(salaryUid)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, salaryUid.split(","));
String optUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
for(String id:uidList){
//判断为空
if(!Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
this.update("UPDATE WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY SET
SALARY_STATUS=?, UPDATE_UID=? ,UPDATE_TIME=SYSDATE WHERE SALARY_UID=? AND
SALARY_STATUS!=? ", DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,optUid,id,"2");
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
//@composite
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "删除成功");
//@output
return true;
}
/**
* 名单导入
* */
@Route
public boolean importExcel(ESurestream surestream) {
HttpServletRequest request=surestream.request();
// HttpServletResponse response=ResponseUtils.getResponse(surestream);
// if (!ServletFileUpload.isMultipartContent(request)) {
// throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897, "Request is not multipart, please
'multipart/form-data' enctype for your form" );
// }
String yearNum = surestream.getString("oneParam");
String monthNum = surestream.getString("twoParam");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(yearNum, "【年份】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(monthNum, "【月份】不能为空");
Calendar calendar = Calendar.getInstance();
int current_year = calendar.get(Calendar.YEAR);
if(Integer.valueOf(yearNum) != current_year ){
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "年份必须为当前年份");
}
try{
MultipartHttpServletRequest fileRequest = (MultipartHttpServletRequest)request;
for (Iterator<?> it = fileRequest.getFileNames(); it.hasNext();) {
String key = (String) it.next();
MultipartFile multipartFile = fileRequest.getFile(key);
String
filesuffix=UEditorConfigUitl.getFileSuffix(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename());//获取上传文件的
后缀名
if(!".xlsx".equals(filesuffix.toLowerCase())){
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897,"[非.xlsx]类型文件不允许上传");
}
InputStream fileIS = multipartFile.getInputStream();
String excelname = multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().substring(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().indexOf("."));
//得到部署路径
// String rootPath =
SingletonService.getRealPath().replace("/",System.getProperty("file.separator")).replace("\\", System.getProperty("file.separator"));
// excel 列结构
List<ExcelColumn> excelColumns = new ArrayList<ExcelColumn>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(0, "COLLEGE_NAME", "用工部门/学院
"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(1, "JOB_NAME", "岗位名称"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(2, "PLAN_NAME", "岗位计划"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(3, "XH", "学号"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(4, "XM", "姓名"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(5, "UNIT_NAME", "报酬标准"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(6, "SALARY_TIMES", "劳作时长"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(7, "ALL_AMOUNT", "劳作总金额"));
ExcelHead head = new ExcelHead();
head.setRowCount(1); // 头所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
List<HashMap> stuList=null;
try {
stuList = ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().importToObjectList(head, multipartFile.getInputStream());
} catch (Exception e) {
throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897,"导入岗位雇用信息失败" );
}
String stuNo = null;//学号
String stuName = null;//姓名
String collegeName = null;//
String jobName = null;//
String planName = null;//
String allAmount = null;//
String jobUid = null;
int countAdd = 0 ; //新增条数
int failcnt = 0;//导入失败计数
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String remark = "";
for(HashMap stuMap : stuList){
BigDecimal salaryTimes = null;//
remark = "";
int errcnt = 0;
//学号
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XH"))){
stuNo = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XH").trim());
}else{
stuMap.put("IMPREMARK", "学号不能为空");
errcnt++;
continue;
}
//姓名
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XM"))){
stuName = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XM").trim());
}else{
stuMap.put("IMPREMARK", "姓名不能为空");
errcnt++;
continue;
}
//用工部门/学院
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("COLLEGE_NAME"))){
collegeName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("COLLEGE_NAME").trim());
}else{
remark +="用工部门/学院不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//岗位名称
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("JOB_NAME"))){
jobName = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("JOB_NAME").trim());
}else{
remark +="岗位名称不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//计划名称
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("PLAN_NAME"))){
planName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("PLAN_NAME").trim());
}else{
remark +="计划名称不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//报酬标准
// if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("UNIT_NAME"))){
// String unitName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("UNIT_NAME").trim());
// unitCode = CacheHolderDicTree.getCodeByName("SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT", unitName);
// }else{
// remark +="报酬标准不能为空！";
// errcnt++;
// }
//劳作时长
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("SALARY_TIMES"))){
String salaryTimesStr =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("SALARY_TIMES").trim());
if( !StringUtil.isNumeric(salaryTimesStr) ){
remark +="劳作时长请直接输入数字！";
errcnt++;
}
if(Double.valueOf(salaryTimesStr)<=0){
remark +="只能导入劳作时长大于[0]的学生工资信息！";
errcnt++;
}
salaryTimes = new BigDecimal(salaryTimesStr);;
}else{
remark +="劳作时长不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//劳作总金额
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("ALL_AMOUNT"))){
allAmount =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("ALL_AMOUNT").trim());
}else{
remark +="劳作总金额不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
HashMap planMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT PLAN_UID,PLAN_TYPE
FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P WHERE P.PLAN_NAME=? AND P.YEAR_NUM=? AND
P.PLAN_STATUS='1' ", planName,yearNum);
//1 学院， 2 部门 , 如果是学院才判断
String planType = null;
if(planMap != null) {
planType = planMap.getString("PLAN_TYPE");
}else {
remark +="【"+ yearNum +"】的【" + planName + "】计划的信息
不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
//效验学号和姓名是否一致
HashMap stuValidateMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT
STU_NO,COLLEGE_CODE,SPECIALTY_CODE,CLASS_CODE,TEL_NUM FROM STUDENT_INFO WHERE
STU_NO = ? AND STU_NAME=? ", stuNo,stuName);
if(stuValidateMap==null) {
remark +="学号【" + stuNo + "】和姓名【"+ stuName +"】对应的
学生不存在.";
errcnt++;
}
HashMap depPlanMap = this.queryForMap("select
D.DEP_UID,D.COLLEGE_CODE,D.ALL_AMOUNTS from WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D LEFT JOIN
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_PLAN P ON P.PLAN_UID=D.PLAN_UID " +
" LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON C.COLLEGE_CODE = D.COLLEGE_CODE WHERE P.YEAR_NUM=? AND C.COLLEGE_NAME=? AND D.DATA_STATUS=? ", yearNum, collegeName,"1");
String salaryAmountStr = null;
String unitCode = null;
String allAmounts = null;//预算
if(depPlanMap!=null) {
String collegeUid = depPlanMap.getString("COLLEGE_CODE");
String depUid = depPlanMap.getString("DEP_UID");
allAmounts = depPlanMap.getString("ALL_AMOUNTS");//学院预算
金额
HashMap jobMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT
JI.JOB_UID,JI.COLLEGE_CODE,JI.SALARY_AMOUNT,JI.SALARY_UNIT FROM
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI WHERE JI.JOB_NAME=? AND JI.DEP_UID=? AND JI.COLLEGE_CODE=?
AND JI.JOB_STATUS != '-1' ", jobName, depUid, collegeUid);
if(jobMap!=null && !Validate.isEmpty(jobMap.getString("JOB_UID")))
{
jobUid = jobMap.getString("JOB_UID");
unitCode = jobMap.getString("SALARY_UNIT");//薪资单位(1
月 2 天 3 小时)
salaryAmountStr = jobMap.getString("SALARY_AMOUNT");//
薪资金额（元）
if (Validate.isEmpty(unitCode)){
remark +="对应岗位信息中的报酬标准单位为空！";
errcnt++;
}
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("UNIT_NAME"))){
String unitName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("UNIT_NAME").trim());
unitCode = CacheHolderDicTree.getCodeByName("SYS_WORK_SALARYUNIT", unitName);
}else{
remark +="报酬标准不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
if (Validate.isEmpty(salaryAmountStr)){
remark +="对应岗位信息中的报酬标准金额为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//判断是否在岗位上
if(!this.existSQL("SELECT EMPLOY_UID FROM
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_EMPLOY P WHERE P.JOB_UID=? AND P.STU_NO=? AND P.EMPLOY_STATUS='1' ", jobUid, stuNo)) {
remark +=【" " + stuNo + "】学号的学生不在【"+ jobName
+"】岗位上.";
errcnt++;
}
if(this.existSQL("SELECT P.SALARY_UID FROM
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY P WHERE P.JOB_UID=? AND P.STU_NO=? AND P.YEAR_NUM=? AND
P.MONTH_NUM=? AND P.SALARY_STATUS!='-1' ", jobUid,stuNo,yearNum,monthNum)) {
remark +="【" + stuNo + "】学号的学生【"+ jobName +"】
岗位【"+ yearNum +"】年【"+ monthNum +"】月薪资条已存在.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="【" + collegeName + "】 部门/学院的【"+ yearNum
+"】岗位计划中【"+ jobName +"】岗位信息不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="【" + collegeName + "】 部门/学院的【"+ yearNum +"】
岗位计划中不存在或未启用.";
errcnt++;
}
BigDecimal c2 = BigDecimal.ZERO;
BigDecimal salaryAllAmountB = BigDecimal.ZERO;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(salaryAmountStr) && !Validate.isEmpty(salaryTimes)
&& !Validate.isEmpty(allAmount)) {
salaryAllAmountB = new BigDecimal(salaryAmountStr);
BigDecimal c1 = salaryAllAmountB.multiply(salaryTimes);
c2 = new BigDecimal(allAmount);
if(c1.compareTo(c2) !=0) {
remark +="【劳作总金额】与【后台计算的总金额】不一致！
请核实！";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="【后台计算的总金额】所需参数不完整！请核实！";
errcnt++;
}
if(planType!=null && "1".equals(planType)) {
String jsSql = "SELECT COUNT(T.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT) AS
SALARY_AMOUNTS,D.DEP_UID,D.ALL_AMOUNTS AS PLAN_AMOUNTS " +
" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY T LEFT JOIN
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO JI ON JI.JOB_UID=T.JOB_UID " +
" LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D ON D.DEP_UID
=JI.DEP_UID " +
" WHERE T.JOB_UID =? AND (T.SALARY_STATUS=1 OR
T.SALARY_STATUS=2) " +
" GROUP BY D.DEP_UID,D.ALL_AMOUNTS ";
//查询岗位计划机构的结算情况
HashMap jsMap = super.queryForMap(jsSql, jobUid);
//计划机构的总金额
BigDecimal planAmountsB = BigDecimal.ZERO;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(allAmounts)){//学院预算金额
planAmountsB = new BigDecimal(allAmounts);
}else {
remark +="【学院计划预算】为空！请核实！";
errcnt++;
}
//已用金额
BigDecimal salaryAmountsB = BigDecimal.ZERO;
if(jsMap!=null
&& !Validate.isEmpty(jsMap.getString("SALARY_AMOUNTS"))){
salaryAmountsB = new
BigDecimal(jsMap.getString("SALARY_AMOUNTS"));
}
BigDecimal syje = planAmountsB.subtract(salaryAmountsB);//剩余
金额
if(syje.compareTo(c2)==-1){
remark +="【" + collegeName + "】 可用的计划金额，不足以
制此工资，学院的计划金额为【"+ planAmountsB.doubleValue() +"】元,学院已经使用【"+
salaryAmountsB.doubleValue() +"】元,剩余金额为【"+ syje +"】元,此条工资总的劳作金额为【"+
c2.doubleValue() +"】元";
errcnt++;
}
}
//没错就进行保存操作
if(errcnt==0) {
try{
WorkstudyJobsSalary salary = new WorkstudyJobsSalary();
salary.setSalaryUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("workstudysalaryuid"));
salary.setJobUid(jobUid);
salary.setStuNo(stuNo);
salary.setStuCollegeCode(stuValidateMap.getString("COLLEGE_CODE"));
salary.setStuSpecialtyCode(stuValidateMap.getString("SPECIALTY_CODE"));
salary.setStuClassCode(stuValidateMap.getString("CLASS_CODE"));
salary.setYearNum(yearNum);
salary.setMonthNum(monthNum);
// salary.setBeginDate(beginDate);
// salary.setEndDate(endDate);
salary.setSalaryAmount(salaryAllAmountB.doubleValue());
salary.setSalaryUnit(unitCode);
salary.setSalaryTimes(salaryTimes.doubleValue());
salary.setSalaryAllAmount(c2.doubleValue());
salary.setSalaryStatus("1");//待结算
salary.setSalaryRemark(null);
salary.setSubmitUid(optAccountUid);
salary.setSubmitTime(nowDate);
// salary.setSettlementUid(optAccountUid);
// salary.setSettlementTime(nowDate);
salary.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
salary.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(salary);
remark = "学号[" + stuNo + "]导入成功.";
countAdd++;
}catch (Exception e) {
failcnt++;
}
}else {
failcnt++;
}
stuMap.put("IMPREMARK", remark);
}
String rootPath = Configurations.instance().getString("easy.upload.file.path").replace("/",System.getProperty("file.s
eparator"));
//生成处理结果文件
String zdypath = DicConst.IMPWORKSTUDY_PATH+File.separator;
String excelpath = rootPath + zdypath;;
File fDbfpath =new File(excelpath);
//如果文件夹不存在则创建
if (!fDbfpath.exists() && !fDbfpath.isDirectory()){
Logs.log().info( "[" + excelpath + "]不存在,创建" );
fDbfpath .mkdir();
}
String wdbffilename = DicConst.IMPWORKSTUDY_PATH+"_GWXZ_" +
DateSource.getTradedate(CFrame.DatePattern5 ) + excelname;
String wdbffilepath = excelpath + wdbffilename;
String cdbffilepath = zdypath + wdbffilename;
File outputFile = new File(wdbffilepath);
// 需要特殊转换的单元
//Map<String, Map> headMap = new java.util.HashMap<String, Map>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(excelColumns.size(), "IMPREMARK", "导
入提示备注"));
head.setRowCount(1); // 模板中头部所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().exportExcelFile(head, fileIS, outputFile, stuList);
//返回数据
surestream.put("resultinfo", " 导 入 岗 位 薪 资 信 息 处 理 结 果 , 成 功 [" +
countAdd +"]条,失败["+ failcnt +"]条请下载处理结果文件" );
surestream.put("retfilename", wdbffilename);//处理结果文件名
surestream.put("retfilepath", cdbffilepath);//处理结果文件存放路径
}
} catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "导入操作成功");
//@output
return true;
}
}
package com.easy.modules.workstudy;
import java.io.IOException;

@Plugin(
transcode = "jobStuManage", transname = "勤工助学_学生薪资报表", author = "lcx", createDate = "2023-03-14"
)
@Transactional
public class JobStuManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream>{
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean queryAll(ESurestream surestream) {
String isE="0";//是否导出
String yearMonth = null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("isE".equals(c.getName())) {
isE = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("YEAR_MONTH".equals(c.getName())) {
yearMonth = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
String[] yearMonthCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(yearMonth,"-");
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " AND I.COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.dep.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
roleSql = " AND I.COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND
CODE_TYPE='"+RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey()+"') ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
// Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
// arrayList.add(collCondition);
// }
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
arrayList.add(new OrderBy("SALARY_STATUS",OrderBy.desc));
arrayList.add(new OrderBy("YEAR_NUM",OrderBy.desc));
arrayList.add(new OrderBy("ALL_GWS", OrderBy.desc));
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SALARY_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_STATUS", "SYS_WORK_SALARY_STATUS"));
formats.put("MONTH_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("MONTH_NUM", "SYS_MONTH_NUM"));
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK",true));//开户行
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX",true));//性别代码
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
//数据导出不进行分页处理
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
pager.setPageSize(-1);
pager.setPageNo(-1);
}
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT T.STU_NO, T.SALARY_STATUS,T.ALL_GWS,T.YEAR_NUM,T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE,T.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE,T.STU_ CLASS_CODE, ");
sqlBuild.append(" T.ALL_AMOUNT, COUNT_QGZX_STU_YF(T.STU_NO, T.YEAR_NUM) AS
MON_NUM, CASE WHEN KNS.KNS_NUM > 0 THEN '是' ELSE '否' END SFKNS ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM (SELECT S.STU_NO, S.YEAR_NUM,S.SALARY_STATUS,COUNT(S.SALARY_UID) AS ALL_GWS, SUM(S.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT) AS ALL_AMOUNT ");
sqlBuild.append(" ,S.STU_COLLEGE_CODE,S.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE,S.STU_CLASS_CODE
");
// sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY S WHERE 1=1 ");
sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY S LEFT JOIN
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO I ON I.JOB_UID=S.JOB_UID WHERE 1=1 ");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yearMonthCode[1])) {
String ye = yearMonthCode[0].trim();
String mon = yearMonthCode[1].replaceAll("^(0+)", "").trim();
sqlBuild.append(" AND
TO_DATE(S.YEAR_NUM||'-'||S.MONTH_NUM,'YYYY-MM') >=
TO_DATE('"+ye+"-"+mon+"','YYYY-MM') ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yearMonthCode[3])) {
String ye = yearMonthCode[2].trim();
String mon = yearMonthCode[3].replaceAll("^(0+)", "").trim();
sqlBuild.append(" AND TO_DATE(S.YEAR_NUM||'-'||S.MONTH_NUM,'YYYY-MM')
<= TO_DATE('"+ye+"-"+mon+"','YYYY-MM') ");
}
//数据权限控制
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
sqlBuild.append(roleSql);
}
sqlBuild.append(" GROUP BY S.SALARY_STATUS, S.STU_NO, S.YEAR_NUM ,S.STU_COLLEGE_CODE,S.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE,S.STU_CLASS_CODE) T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN (SELECT COUNT(A.STU_NO) AS KNS_NUM,A.STU_NO
FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' GROUP BY A.STU_NO) KNS
ON KNS.STU_NO = T.STU_NO ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE 1=1 ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
List<HashMap> statisticsList = pager.getDataSource();
exportData(statisticsList, surestream);
}else {
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
}
return true;
}
/**
* 数据导出
* */
public boolean exportData(List<HashMap> statisticsList,ESurestream surestream){
try {
if(statisticsList!=null&&statisticsList.size()>0){
String[] headers={"学号","姓名","性别","开户行","银行卡号","是否困难生
","年份","岗位数","月份数","总金额","总金额","状态","学院","班级"};
String[]
column={"STU_NO","STU_STU_NAME","STU_SEX_CODE","STU_BANK_NAME","STU_BANK_CODE
","SFKNS","YEAR_NUM","ALL_GWS","MON_NUM","ALL_AMOUNT","SALARY_STATUS_SV","STU_ COLLEGE_NAME","STU_CLASS_NAME"};
String title=" 学 生 薪 资 报 表
_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+ ".xlsx";
ExportExcel<HashMap> exp = new ExportExcel<HashMap>();
exp.writeExcel(title, headers, statisticsList, "yyyy-MM-dd", surestream.response(), column);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
return true;
}
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean queryStu(ESurestream surestream) {
String isE="0";//是否导出
String yearMonth = null;
String jobsSelvalue=null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("isE".equals(c.getName())) {
isE = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("YEAR_MONTH".equals(c.getName())) {
yearMonth = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("JOBS_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
jobsSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
String[] yearMonthCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(yearMonth,"-");
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(jobsSelvalue,null);
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " AND I.COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.dep.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
roleSql = " AND I.COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND
CODE_TYPE='"+RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey()+"') ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
arrayList.add(new OrderBy("SALARY_STATUS",OrderBy.desc));
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SALARY_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("SALARY_STATUS", "SYS_WORK_SALARY_STATUS"));
// formats.put("MONTH_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("MONTH_NUM", "SYS_MONTH_NUM"));
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK",true));//开户行
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX",true));//性别代码
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
//数据导出不进行分页处理
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
pager.setPageSize(-1);
pager.setPageNo(-1);
}
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT ROWNUM, T.STU_NO, T.SALARY_STATUS,T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE,T.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE,T.STU_CLASS_CODE, ");
sqlBuild.append(" T.ALL_AMOUNT AS
SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT,T.JOB_UIDS,T.SALARY_UIDS, CASE WHEN KNS.KNS_NUM > 0 THEN ' 是 ' ELSE '否' END SFKNS ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM (SELECT
S.STU_NO,S.SALARY_STATUS,S.STU_COLLEGE_CODE,S.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE,S.STU_CLASS_CODE, SUM(S.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT) AS ALL_AMOUNT ");
sqlBuild.append(" ,Listagg(S.JOB_UID,',') AS JOB_UIDS ,Listagg(S.SALARY_UID,',') as
SALARY_UIDS ");
sqlBuild.append(" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY S LEFT JOIN
WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO I ON I.JOB_UID=S.JOB_UID LEFT JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_DEP D ON
D.DEP_UID=I.DEP_UID WHERE 1=1 ");
String dateStr = "";
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yearMonthCode[0])) {
String ye = yearMonthCode[0].trim();
//sqlBuild.append(" AND S.YEAR_NUM >="+ye+"");
dateStr = dateStr+ye+"年";
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yearMonthCode[1])) {
String ye = yearMonthCode[0].trim();
String mon = yearMonthCode[1].replaceAll("^(0+)", "").trim();
//sqlBuild.append(" AND S.MONTH_NUM >= "+mon+" ");
sqlBuild.append(" AND
TO_DATE(S.YEAR_NUM||'-'||S.MONTH_NUM,'YYYY-MM') >=
TO_DATE('"+ye+"-"+mon+"','YYYY-MM') ");
dateStr = dateStr+mon+"月";
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yearMonthCode[2])) {
String ye = yearMonthCode[2].trim();
//sqlBuild.append(" AND S.YEAR_NUM <="+ye+" ");
dateStr = dateStr+"-"+ye+"年";
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(yearMonthCode[3])) {
String ye = yearMonthCode[2].trim();
String mon = yearMonthCode[3].replaceAll("^(0+)", "").trim();
//Integer mon = Integer.valueOf(yearMonthCode[3]);
//sqlBuild.append(" AND S.MONTH_NUM <= "+mon+" ");
sqlBuild.append(" AND TO_DATE(S.YEAR_NUM||'-'||S.MONTH_NUM,'YYYY-MM')
<= TO_DATE('"+ye+"-"+mon+"','YYYY-MM') ");
dateStr = dateStr+mon+"月";
}
//数据权限控制
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
sqlBuild.append(roleSql);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND D.PLAN_UID ='"+arrCode[0]+"'");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND I.DEP_UID ='"+arrCode[1]+"'");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND S.JOB_UID ='"+arrCode[2]+"'");
}
sqlBuild.append(" GROUP BY S.SALARY_STATUS, S.STU_NO, S.STU_COLLEGE_CODE, S.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE, S.STU_CLASS_CODE) T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN (SELECT COUNT(A.STU_NO) AS KNS_NUM,A.STU_NO
FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' GROUP BY A.STU_NO) KNS
ON KNS.STU_NO = T.STU_NO ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE 1=1 ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
List<HashMap> statisticsList = pager.getDataSource();
BigDecimal totalB = BigDecimal.ZERO;
if(statisticsList!=null && statisticsList.size()>0) {
for(int i=0;i<statisticsList.size();i++ ) {
HashMap smap = statisticsList.get(i);
String stuNo = smap.getString("STU_NO");
String salaryUids = smap.getString("SALARY_UIDS");
String sql = " SELECT S.JOB_UID,I.JOB_NAME,C.COLLEGE_NAME, SUM(S.SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT) AS ALL_AMOUNT " +
" FROM WORKSTUDY_JOBS_SALARY S " +
" left JOIN WORKSTUDY_JOBS_INFO I ON S.JOB_UID=I.JOB_UID" +
" LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_COLLEGE C ON C.COLLEGE_CODE =
I.COLLEGE_CODE" +
" WHERE S.STU_NO=? AND S.SALARY_UID IN ("+salaryUids+")" +
" GROUP BY S.JOB_UID,I.JOB_NAME,C.COLLEGE_NAME ";
List<HashMap> ssList = this.sqlQuery(sql, stuNo);
StringBuilder jobReamrk = new StringBuilder();
String jobReamrkStr = "";
if(ssList!=null && ssList.size()>0) {
jobReamrk.setLength(0);
int xh = 1;
for(HashMap ssmap : ssList) {
String cName = ssmap.getString("COLLEGE_NAME");
String jName = ssmap.getString("JOB_NAME");
String sAmount = ssmap.getString("ALL_AMOUNT");
jobReamrk.append(","+xh+" 、 "+cName+" 【 "+jName+" 】：
"+sAmount+"元");
}
if(jobReamrk!=null && jobReamrk.length()>1) {
jobReamrkStr = jobReamrk.substring(1);
}
}
smap.put("JOB_REAMRK", jobReamrkStr);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(smap.getString("SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT"))) {
totalB=totalB.add(new
BigDecimal(smap.getString("SALARY_ALL_AMOUNT")));
}
smap.put("ROWNUM", i+1);
}
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
//拼凑文档参数
Map<String, Object> dataMap = new java.util.HashMap<String, Object>();
// dataMap 对应的是模板中 {字段名}格式
String title = "";
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
WorkstudyJobsDep dep = this.get(WorkstudyJobsDep.class, arrCode[1]);
if(dep!=null && dep.getCollegeCode()!=null) {
BaseSysCollege baseSysCollege = this.get(BaseSysCollege.class, dep.getCollegeCode());
if(baseSysCollege!=null) {
title=title+baseSysCollege.getCollegeName();
}
}
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(dateStr)) {
title="("+dateStr+")"+title;
}
dataMap.put("TITLE", title) ;//标题
dataMap.put("TOTAL_AMOUNT", totalB.toString());//合计总额
try {
String filePath =
SingletonService.getRealPath()+"template//workstudy//exp_hzkhb.xlsx";
TemplateExcelUtil.templateExcelExport(surestream.response(),dataMap.get("TITLE")+" 勤 工
助学汇总考核表.xlsx",filePath,dataMap,statisticsList);
} catch (IOException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
}else {
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
}
return true;
}
}
package com.easy.modules.syn;
import java.io.File;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.egi.ISessionFactory;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.egi.IStatus;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.facade.AppContext;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.stereotype.Plugin;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.stereotype.Priority;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.util.FileUtilsExt;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.constant.CFrame;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.util.Logs;
@Plugin(
transcode = "jdbcMsdataSession", transname = "数据对接会话工厂管理", author = "lcx", createDate = "2023-02-08", singleton = true, priority = Priority.low1
)
public class JdbcMsdataSession implements IStatus{
public final static String JDBC_MSDATA="jdbc-msdata"; //ms_data
//数据对接同步学生信息 学籍、年级(复学后年级会变化)、毕业日期、学院、班级、
专业
public boolean start() {
try{
File file = FileUtilsExt.getFile("classpath:jdbc-msdata.properties");
if(file.exists()){
ISessionFactory buildSessionFactory = AppContext.buildSessionFactory(CFrame.hibernate,file );
AppContext.regSessionFactory(JDBC_MSDATA, buildSessionFactory );
}
}
catch ( Exception e )
{
Logs.log( ).error( "数据对接会话工厂管理", e );
}
return true;
}
public boolean stop() {
return true;
}
}

package com.easy.modules.syn;
import java.util.Date;
import java.util.List;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.constant.CCurrent;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.egi.ISession;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.egi.ISessionFactory;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.exception.RException;

import com.easy.asgi.footstone.stereotype.Plugin;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.stereotype.Transactional;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.stereotype.method.Route;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.util.HashMap;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.ega.genericity.AbstractSessionComponent;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.facade.AppContext;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.struct.pojo.QResultSet;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.util.DateSource;

@Plugin(
transcode = "synWelManage", transname = "迎新数据同步", author = "lcx", createDate = "2022-08-08"
)
@Transactional
public class SynWelManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream>{
@Override
@Autowired("jdbc-welcome")
public void setDbfactory(ISessionFactory sessionFactory ){
this.sessionFactory = sessionFactory;
}
@Autowired(JdbcWelcomeSession.JDBC_JWELCOME+CCurrent.dbsession)
public void setDbfactorydbsession( ISession session ){
super.setDbfactorydbsession( session );
}
/**
* 同步迎新学生信息数据
* **/
@Route
public boolean synStu(ESurestream surestream ) {
String optAccountName=Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
if(!"administrator".equals(optAccountName)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【"+optAccountName+"】您没有操作权限！
");
}
String yearNum = surestream.getString("YEAR_NUM");
if (!Validate.isEmpty(yearNum)) {
int currentPage = 1;// 当前页数
int pageSize = 1000;// 每页显示数
int totalPages = 0 ;//分页
ISession dSession = AppContext.getSession(AppContext.defaultKey);
try{
DBOperate.delete(dSession, " DELETE FROM DORM_STUDENT_INFO WHERE
GRADE_CODE=? ", yearNum);
}catch(Exception e) {
ExceptionStackTrace.print( e );
}finally{
dSession.flush();
DBUtil.closeSession(dSession);
}
QResultSet qresultset = new QResultSet();
qresultset.setPageNo(currentPage);
qresultset.setPageSize(pageSize);
String selectAform ="SELECT T.* FROM WEL_STUDENT_INFO T WHERE
T.GRADE_CODE = '"+yearNum+"' AND T.REGISTER_STATUS='1' ORDER BY
T.COLLEGE_CODE,T.CLASS_CODE,T.STUDENT_NO ";
qresultset = this.sqlConditionQuery(qresultset,selectAform, null, null);
List<HashMap> stuList=null;
Date nowTime = DateSource.getTradedate();
if(!Validate.isEmpty(qresultset)&&!Validate.isEmpty(qresultset.getDataSource())) {
stuList=qresultset.getDataSource();
ISession chiSession = AppContext.getSession(AppContext.defaultKey);
try{
for(HashMap stumap:stuList) {
saveStu(chiSession, stumap, nowTime);
}
}catch(Exception e) {
ExceptionStackTrace.print( e );
}finally{
chiSession.flush();
DBUtil.closeSession(chiSession );
}
int totalRows = (int)qresultset.getTotalItems();
if ((totalRows % pageSize) == 0) {
totalPages = totalRows / pageSize;
} else {
totalPages = totalRows / pageSize + 1;
}
for (int i = 2 ; i < totalPages + 1; i++) {
qresultset.setPageNo(i);
qresultset.setPageSize(pageSize);
qresultset = this.sqlConditionQuery(qresultset,selectAform, null, null);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(qresultset)&&!Validate.isEmpty(qresultset.getDataSource())) {
stuList=qresultset.getDataSource();
chiSession = AppContext.getSession(AppContext.defaultKey);
try{
for(HashMap stumap:stuList) {
saveStu(chiSession, stumap, nowTime);
}
}catch(Exception e) {
ExceptionStackTrace.print( e );
}finally{
chiSession.flush();
DBUtil.closeSession(chiSession );
}
}
}
}
System.out.println(" 学 生 数 据 同 步 成 功
====================================");
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "成功");
//@output
return true;
}
private void saveStu(ISession dsession,HashMap stuMap,Date nowTime) {
try{
if(!DBOperate.existSQL(dsession,"SELECT COUNT(1) FROM STUDENT_INFO WHERE
STU_NO=? ", stuMap.getString("STU_NO"))) {
StudentInfo stuInfo = new StudentInfo();
this.hashMap2Obj(stuMap, stuInfo);
stuInfo.setPyccCode(stuMap.getString("LEVEL_CODE"));
stuInfo.setXuezCode(stuMap.getString("XUEZHI_CODE"));
stuInfo.setCardType("1");//身份证
stuInfo.setExamNo(stuMap.getString("EXAMINEER_UID"));
stuInfo.setMiddleSchool(stuMap.getString("MIDDLE_SCHOOL_NAME"));
stuInfo.setUpdateTime(nowTime);
stuInfo.setEnrollmentStatus("1");
stuInfo.setDataStatus("1");
DBOperate.save(dsession, stuInfo);
StudentInfoExt infoExt = new StudentInfoExt();
this.hashMap2Obj(stuMap, infoExt);
infoExt.setStuNoExt(stuInfo.getStuNo());
infoExt.setHomePost(stuMap.getString("POSTNO_NUM"));
infoExt.setPhotoPath(stuMap.getString("PHOTO_PATH"));
DBOperate.save(dsession, infoExt);
saveOrUpdateAccount(dsession, stuInfo, nowTime);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
}
public void saveOrUpdateAccount( ISession dsession,StudentInfo stuInfo,Date nowTime)
{
if(!DBOperate.existSQL(dsession,"SELECT COUNT(1) FROM BASE_ACCOUNT WHERE
ACCOUNT_NAME=? ", stuInfo.getStuNo())) {
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
BaseAccount bAccount=new BaseAccount();
bAccount.setAccountUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("accountid"));
bAccount.setAccountName(stuInfo.getStuNo());
bAccount.setAccountNickname(stuInfo.getStuName());
bAccount.setAccountType(AccountTypeEnum.type_2.getKey());
bAccount.setAccountInfoUid(bAccount.getAccountUid());
bAccount.setDataStatus("1");
bAccount.setAccountPw(MD5.md5Password(DicConst.DEFAULT_PASSWORD));
bAccount.setLoginCount(0);
bAccount.setErrorCount(0);
bAccount.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
bAccount.setUpdateUid(null);
bAccount.setCreateTime(nowDate);
bAccount.setCreateUid(null);
this.save(bAccount);
BaseAccountInfo accountInfo=new BaseAccountInfo();
accountInfo.setInfoUid(bAccount.getAccountUid());
accountInfo.setCellPhone(null);
accountInfo.setCollegeUid(stuInfo.getCollegeCode());
accountInfo.setEmail(null);
accountInfo.setRealName(bAccount.getAccountNickname());
accountInfo.setRegTime(bAccount.getCreateTime());
accountInfo.setSex(stuInfo.getSexCode());
accountInfo.setUpdateTime(nowDate);
accountInfo.setUpdateUid(null);
this.save(accountInfo);
//学生角色
String sql="INSERT INTO BASE_ACCOUNT_ROLE(AR_UID, ROLE_UID, ACCOUNT_UID) values ("+DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("accountRoleId")+",?,?)";
this.update(sql,RoleUidEnum.role_student.getKey(),bAccount.getAccountUid());
}
}
/**
* 同步迎新系统班级及专业信息数据
* **/
@Route
public boolean synClass(ESurestream surestream ) {
String optAccountName=Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
if(!"administrator".equals(optAccountName)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【"+optAccountName+"】您没有操作权限！
");
}
String yearNum = surestream.getString("YEAR_NUM");
String likeStr = yearNum.substring(2, 4);//相同年匹配参数
if (!Validate.isEmpty(yearNum)) {
List<HashMap> welClassList = this.sqlQuery(" SELECT T.* FROM BASE_SYS_CLASS T
WHERE T.CLASS_CODE LIKE ? ", likeStr+"%");
if(welClassList!=null) {
ISession chiSession = AppContext.getSession(AppContext.defaultKey);
try{
for(HashMap cmap:welClassList) {
String classCode = cmap.getString("CLASS_CODE");
String className = cmap.getString("CLASS_NAME");
String specialtyCode = cmap.getString("SPECIALTY_CODE");
String collegeCode = cmap.getString("COLLEGE_CODE");
saveClass( chiSession, classCode, className, specialtyCode, collegeCode, yearNum);
}
}catch(Exception e) {
ExceptionStackTrace.print( e );
}finally{
chiSession.flush();
DBUtil.closeSession(chiSession );
}
}
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "成功");
//@output
return true;
}
private void saveClass(ISession chiSession,String classCode,String className,String
specialtyCode,String collegeCode,String gradeCode) {
BaseSysClass baseSysClass = DBOperate.get(chiSession,BaseSysClass.class, classCode);
if(baseSysClass==null) {
baseSysClass = new BaseSysClass();
baseSysClass.setClassCode(classCode);
}
baseSysClass.setClassName(className);
baseSysClass.setCollegeCode(collegeCode);
baseSysClass.setDataStatus("1");
baseSysClass.setGradeCode(gradeCode);
baseSysClass.setSpecialtyCode(specialtyCode);
DBOperate.merge(chiSession,baseSysClass);
saveSpecialty( chiSession, specialtyCode, collegeCode);
}
private void saveSpecialty(ISession chiSession,String specialtyCode,String collegeCode) {
BaseSysSpecialty baseSysSpecialty = DBOperate.get(chiSession,BaseSysSpecialty.class,
specialtyCode);
if (baseSysSpecialty==null) {
String welSpecialtyName = this.queryForString("SELECT SPECIALTY_NAME FROM
BASE_SYS_SPECIALTY WHERE SPECIALTY_CODE=?", specialtyCode);
if(Validate.isEmpty(welSpecialtyName)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【"+specialtyCode+"】对应的专业代码
不存在！");
}
baseSysSpecialty = new BaseSysSpecialty();
baseSysSpecialty.setDataStatus("1");
//baseSysSpecialty.setGbSpecialtyCode(gbSpecialtyCode);
baseSysSpecialty.setSpecialtyCode(specialtyCode);
baseSysSpecialty.setSpecialtyName(welSpecialtyName);
DBOperate.save(chiSession,baseSysSpecialty);
}
}
}
