@Plugin(
transcode = "difficultApplyManage", transname = "困难生信息", author = "lcx", createDate = "2021-11-19"
)
@Transactional
public class DifficultApplyManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
String collegeSelvalue=null,ocollegeSelvalue=null;
String isE="0";//是否导出
String isRepeat = null,schoolYear=null,termNum=null,auditStatus=null;
String dicType = null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("COLLEGE_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
collegeSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("OCOLLEGE_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
ocollegeSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("isE".equals(c.getName())) {
isE = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("IS_REPEAT".equals(c.getName())) {
isRepeat = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("SCHOOL_YEAR".equals(c.getName())) {
schoolYear = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("TERM_NUM".equals(c.getName())) {
termNum = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID".equals(c.getName())) {
dicType = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("AUDIT_STATUS".equals(c.getName())) {
auditStatus = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(collegeSelvalue,null);
String[] arrCodeO = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(ocollegeSelvalue,null);
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
//学年
if(!Validate.isEmpty(schoolYear)) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("SCHOOL_YEAR",schoolYear,Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
//学期
if(!Validate.isEmpty(termNum)) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("TERM_NUM",termNum,Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
// Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_COLLEGE_CODE",arrCode[0],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
// arrayList.add(otherCondition);
// }
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
// Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_SPECIALTY_CODE",arrCode[1],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
// arrayList.add(otherCondition);
// }
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
// Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_CLASS_CODE",arrCode[2],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
// arrayList.add(otherCondition);
// }
//困难类型
if(!Validate.isEmpty(dicType)) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID",dicType,Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
//导出时排除取消认定的数据
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE) && Validate.isEmpty(dicType)){
// Condition otherCondition = new Condition("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID", DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey(), Condition.noteq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
// arrayList.add(otherCondition);
// Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue("
(DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID !='"+DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey()+"' OR DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID IS NULL ) "));
// arrayList.add(collCondition);
// }
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.counselor.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_CLASS_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.student.getKey().equals(roleType)){
roleSql = " STU_NO = '"+optAccount+"' ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "无权限进行操作");
return true;
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
// isRepeat:1 学年去重 2 学期去重
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isRepeat) && !Validate.isEmpty(schoolYear)) {
if("1".equals(isRepeat)) {//学年去重
Condition otherCondition = new Condition("RW", isRepeat, Condition.eq,new
JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}else if("2".equals(isRepeat) && !Validate.isEmpty(termNum)) {//春季去重 主要
查询 秋季不是困难生 春季是困难生的人员
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(" STU_NO NOT
IN (SELECT A.STU_NO FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE
A.SCHOOL_YEAR='"+schoolYear+"' AND A.TERM_NUM!='"+termNum+"' AND
A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' ) "));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
}
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("AUDIT_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("AUDIT_STATUS", "AUDIT_AUDIT_STATUS"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM",true));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM",true));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX",true));//性别代码
//formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("APPLY_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("APPLY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("CONFIRM_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("CONFIRM_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
formats.put("CONFIRM_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("CONFIRM_DATE","yyyyMMdd",true));
}
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK",true));//开户行
//数据导出不进行分页处理
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
formats.put("APPLY_REASON", new FormatDic2Str("APPLY_REASON", "SYS_DIFF_APPLY_REASON"));//申请原由
pager.setPageSize(-1);
pager.setPageNo(-1);
}
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT T.APPLY_UID, T.STU_NO, T.SETUP_UID, T.SCHOOL_YEAR, T.TERM_NUM, T.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID, T.APPLY_DATE, T.CONFIRM_DATE, T.APPLY_REASON, T.OTHER_REASON,T.APPLY_REMARK, T.AUDIT_STATUS, T.AUDIT_SORT_NO, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE ");
sqlBuild.append(" ,T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE,T.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE,T.STU_CLASS_CODE,S.SET
UP_NAME, DT.TYPE_NAME, DT.STANDARD_AMOUNT ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isRepeat) && !Validate.isEmpty(schoolYear)) {
sqlBuild.append(" ,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY T.STU_NO ORDER BY
T.SCHOOL_YEAR DESC,T.TERM_NUM DESC,T.CONFIRM_DATE DESC)
RW,I.COLLEGE_CODE,I.SPECIALTY_CODE,I.CLASS_CODE ");
}
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY T LEFT JOIN STUDENT_INFO I
ON I.STU_NO=T.STU_NO ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP S ON
S.SETUP_UID=T.SETUP_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE DT ON
DT.TYPE_UID=T.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.AUDIT_STATUS!='-1' ");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isRepeat) && !Validate.isEmpty(schoolYear)) {
if("1".equals(isRepeat)) {//学年去重
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.SCHOOL_YEAR='"+schoolYear+"' AND
T.AUDIT_STATUS!='0' AND T.AUDIT_STATUS!='-100' AND (T.AUDIT_STATUS='100' OR
T.AUDIT_STATUS='30' )");
}
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND I.COLLEGE_CODE='"+arrCode[0]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND I.SPECIALTY_CODE='"+arrCode[1]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND I.CLASS_CODE='"+arrCode[2]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCodeO[0])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE='"+arrCodeO[0]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCodeO[1])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE='"+arrCodeO[1]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCodeO[2])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_CLASS_CODE='"+arrCodeO[2]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(auditStatus)) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.AUDIT_STATUS='"+auditStatus+"' ");
}
sqlBuild.append(" ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
List<HashMap> statisticsList = pager.getDataSource();
boolean isCance = false;
if(statisticsList!=null) {
if(!Validate.isEmpty(dicType) &&
DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey().equals(dicType)) {
statisticsList = getDiffStu(statisticsList, schoolYear);
isCance = true;
}else {
StringBuilder reasonStrB = new StringBuilder();
for(HashMap tmap:statisticsList) {
if(Validate.isEmpty(tmap.get("STU_BANK_ANAME"))) {
tmap.put("STU_BANK_ANAME", tmap.get("STU_STU_NAME"));
}
reasonStrB.setLength(0);
String dtype = tmap.getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID");
String reasonStr = "";
if(!Validate.isEmpty(dtype) &&
DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey().equals(dtype)) {
reasonStr = tmap.getString("APPLY_REMARK");//取消认定的
原因 取 APPLY_REMARK 字段值
}else {
String otReason = tmap.getString("OTHER_REASON");
String apReason = tmap.getString("APPLY_REASON_SV");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(apReason)) {
reasonStrB.append("，").append(apReason);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(otReason)) {
reasonStrB.append("，").append(otReason);
}
if(reasonStrB!=null && reasonStrB.length()>1) {
reasonStr = reasonStrB.substring(1);
}
}
tmap.put("APPLY_REASON_SV", reasonStr);
tmap.put("CARD_NUM_TYPE", "居民身份证");
}
}
}
exportData(statisticsList, surestream, isCance);
}else {
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
}
return true;
}
/**
* 数据导出
* */
public boolean exportData(List<HashMap> statisticsList,ESurestream surestream,boolean
isCance){
try {
if(statisticsList!=null&&statisticsList.size()>0){
if(isCance) {
String[] headers={"学号","学院","班级","姓名","身份证件类型","身份
证码","取消困难类别","原认定时间","取消时间","取消原因","是否退役士兵学生","认定批次
","认定学年","认定学期","银行账号","银行卡户名","开户行","批次","状态"};
String[]
column={"STU_NO","STU_COLLEGE_NAME","STU_CLASS_NAME","STU_STU_NAME","CARD_NU
M_TYPE","STU_CARD_NUM","TYPE_NAME","OLD_CONFIRM_DATE","CONFIRM_DATE","APPLY_R
EASON_SV","","SETUP_NAME","SCHOOL_YEAR","TERM_NUM"
,"STU_BANK_CODE","STU_BANK_ANAME","STU_BANK_NAME","SETUP_NAME","AUDIT_STA
TUS_SV"};
String title=" 困 难 生 取 消 名 单
_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+ ".xlsx";
ExportExcel<HashMap> exp = new ExportExcel<HashMap>();
exp.writeExcel(title, headers, statisticsList, "yyyy-MM-dd", surestream.response(), column);
}else {
String[] headers={"学号","学院","班级","姓名","身份证件类型","身份
证码","认定困难类别","认定时间","认定原因","是否退役士兵学生","认定批次","认定学年"," 认定学期","银行账号","银行卡户名","开户行","批次","状态"};
String[]
column={"STU_NO","STU_COLLEGE_NAME","STU_CLASS_NAME","STU_STU_NAME","CARD_NU
M_TYPE","STU_CARD_NUM","TYPE_NAME","CONFIRM_DATE","APPLY_REASON_SV","","SETUP_ NAME","SCHOOL_YEAR","TERM_NUM"
,"STU_BANK_CODE","STU_BANK_ANAME","STU_BANK_NAME","SETUP_NAME","AUDIT_STA
TUS_SV"};
String title=" 困 难 生 名 单
_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+ ".xlsx";
ExportExcel<HashMap> exp = new ExportExcel<HashMap>();
exp.writeExcel(title, headers, statisticsList, "yyyy-MM-dd", surestream.response(), column);
}
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
return true;
}
//对取消认定的数据 导出时加入 前一次的困难生认定日期
private List<HashMap> getDiffStu(List<HashMap> statisticsList,String schoolYear) {
if(Validate.isEmpty(schoolYear)) {
return statisticsList;
}
StringBuilder applyUidStr = new StringBuilder();
StringBuilder stuUidStr = new StringBuilder();
//StringBuilder reasonStrB = new StringBuilder();
for(HashMap tmap:statisticsList) {
if(Validate.isEmpty(tmap.get("STU_BANK_ANAME"))) {
tmap.put("STU_BANK_ANAME", tmap.get("STU_STU_NAME"));
}
// reasonStrB.setLength(0);
// String otReason = tmap.getString("OTHER_REASON");
// String apReason = tmap.getString("APPLY_REASON_SV");
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(apReason)) {
// reasonStrB.append("，").append(apReason);
// }
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(otReason)) {
// reasonStrB.append("，").append(otReason);
// }
// String reasonStr = "";
// if(reasonStrB!=null && reasonStrB.length()>1) {
// reasonStr = reasonStrB.substring(1);
// }
tmap.put("APPLY_REASON_SV", tmap.getString("APPLY_REMARK"));
tmap.put("CARD_NUM_TYPE", "居民身份证");
applyUidStr.append(",").append("'"+tmap.getString("APPLY_UID")+"'");
stuUidStr.append(",").append("'"+tmap.getString("STU_NO")+"'");
}
String applyUids = applyUidStr.substring(1);
String stuUids = stuUidStr.substring(1);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("CONFIRM_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("CONFIRM_DATE","yyyyMMdd",true));
String sql = " SELECT A.APPLY_UID, A.STU_NO, A.SETUP_UID, A.SCHOOL_YEAR, A.TERM_NUM, A.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID,A.CONFIRM_DATE FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A " + " WHERE A.SCHOOL_YEAR=? AND A.STU_NO IN ("+stuUids+") AND
A.APPLY_UID NOT IN ("+applyUids+") AND A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' ORDER BY A.SCHOOL_YEAR
DESC, A.TERM_NUM DESC ";
List<HashMap> diffList = null;
try {
diffList = this.jdbcQueryByFormat(sql, formats, schoolYear);
} catch (SQLException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
HashMap difTemMap = new HashMap();
if(diffList!=null) {
for(HashMap dimap:diffList) {
String stuTemp = dimap.getString("STU_NO");
if(!difTemMap.containsKey(stuTemp)) {
difTemMap.put(stuTemp, dimap.getString("CONFIRM_DATE"));
}
}
//加入 认定日期
for(HashMap tmap:statisticsList) {
String stuTemp = tmap.getString("STU_NO");
tmap.put("OLD_CONFIRM_DATE", difTemMap.getString(stuTemp));
}
}
return statisticsList;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
*@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String applyUid = surestream.getString("applyUid");
String isView = surestream.getString("isView","0");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(applyUid, "【ID】不能为空");
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("AUDIT_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("AUDIT_STATUS", "AUDIT_AUDIT_STATUS"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX"));//性别代码
formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("APPLY_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("APPLY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("CONFIRM_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("CONFIRM_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss"));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("END_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.*, S.SETUP_NAME, DT.TYPE_NAME,S.BEGIN_DATE,S.END_DATE ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP S ON
S.SETUP_UID=T.SETUP_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE DT ON
DT.TYPE_UID=T.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID ");

if(applyMap!=null && "1".equals(isView)) {
applyMap.put("auditExeList", AuditDataUtils.getAuditExeList(this.getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey(), applyMap.getString("APPLY_UID"),true));
String stuNo = applyMap.getString("STU_NO");
sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.*, S.SETUP_NAME,S.BEGIN_DATE,S.END_DATE ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP S ON
S.SETUP_UID=T.SETUP_UID ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.STU_NO = ? AND T.AUDIT_STATUS =? ORDER BY
T.SCHOOL_YEAR DESC ");
try {
List<HashMap> hisList = this.jdbcQueryByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, stuNo, AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_pass.getKey());
applyMap.put("hisList", hisList);
} catch (SQLException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
surestream.put("data", applyMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
} **/
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String applyUid = surestream.getString("APPLY_UID");//
String stuNo = surestream.getString("STU_NO");//学号
String setupUid = surestream.getString("SETUP_UID");//困难生开通设置 ID
//String difficultTypeUid = surestream.getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID");// 困 难 类 型
ID(一般困难，困难，特别困难)
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(applyUid, "【困难生信息 ID】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【困难生开通设置 ID】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
SupportDifficultApply apply = this.get(SupportDifficultApply.class, applyUid);
if(apply==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生信息】不存在");
}
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
Typecast.hashMap2obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), apply);
apply.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
apply.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(apply);
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}

/**
* 批量删除
* id 以逗号,拼接
* **/
@Route
public boolean delete(ESurestream surestream) {
String applyUid = surestream.getString("applyUid");
if (!Validate.isEmpty(applyUid)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, applyUid.split(","));
String optUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
for(String id:uidList){
//判断为空
if(!Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
this.update("UPDATE SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY SET AUDIT_STATUS=?, UPDATE_UID=? ,UPDATE_DATE=SYSDATE WHERE APPLY_UID=?", DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,optUid,id);
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
//@composite
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "删除成功");
//@output
return true;
}
/**
* 名单导入
* */
@Route
public boolean importExcel(ESurestream surestream) {
HttpServletRequest request=surestream.request();
// HttpServletResponse response=ResponseUtils.getResponse(surestream);
// if (!ServletFileUpload.isMultipartContent(request)) {
// throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897, "Request is not multipart, please
'multipart/form-data' enctype for your form" );
// }
String setupUid = surestream.getString("oneParam");//开通设置 ID
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【困难生开通设置 ID】不能为空");
SupportDifficultSetup setup = this.get(SupportDifficultSetup.class, setupUid);
if(setup==null || Validate.isEmpty(setup.getSetupUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【设置信息】不存在");
}
if(!"1".equals(setup.getSetupStatus())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生申请】未开放，请联系管理员启
用该开通设置");
}
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
if(!DateUtil.isEffectiveDate(nowDate, setup.getBeginDate(), setup.getEndDate())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生申请】未开放，请在有效时间内
进行数据导入");
}
HashMap typeMap = new HashMap();
List<SupportDifficultType> typeList = this.findMultiple(SupportDifficultType.class, DBCondition.form("dataStatus", "1"));
if(typeList!=null) {
for(SupportDifficultType tymap:typeList) {
typeMap.put(tymap.getTypeName(), tymap.getTypeUid());
}
}else {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生类型档次】信息不存在");
}
try{
MultipartHttpServletRequest fileRequest = (MultipartHttpServletRequest)request;
for (Iterator<?> it = fileRequest.getFileNames(); it.hasNext();) {
String key = (String) it.next();
MultipartFile multipartFile = fileRequest.getFile(key);
String
filesuffix=UEditorConfigUitl.getFileSuffix(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename());//获取上传文件的
后缀名
if(!".xlsx".equals(filesuffix.toLowerCase())){
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897,"[非.xlsx]类型文件不允许上传");
}
InputStream fileIS = multipartFile.getInputStream();
String excelname = multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().substring(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().indexOf("."));
//得到部署路径
// String rootPath =
SingletonService.getRealPath().replace("/",System.getProperty("file.separator")).replace("\\", System.getProperty("file.separator"));
// excel 列结构
List<ExcelColumn> excelColumns = new ArrayList<ExcelColumn>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(0, "XH", "学号"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(1, "XM", "姓名"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(2, "DIFFICULT_TYPE", "困难生档次"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(3, "APPLY_REASON", "认定原因"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(4, "CONFIRM_DATE", "认定时间"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(5, "APPLY_REMARK", "备注"));
ExcelHead head = new ExcelHead();
head.setRowCount(1); // 头所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
List<HashMap> stuList=null;
try {
stuList = ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().importToObjectList(head, multipartFile.getInputStream());
} catch (Exception e) {
throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897,"导入困难生名单数据失败" );
}
String stuNo = null;//学号
String stuName = null;//姓名
String difficultType = null;//困难生档次
String applyReason = null;//认定原因
String confirmDate = null;//认定时间
String applyRemark = null;//备注
int countAdd = 0 ; //新增条数
//int countUpdate = 0;//更新条数
int failcnt = 0;//导入失败计数
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String remark = "";
for(HashMap stuMap : stuList){
remark = "";
int errcnt = 0;
//学号
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XH"))){
stuNo = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XH").trim());
}else{
remark +="学号不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//姓名
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XM"))){
stuName = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XM").trim());
}else{
remark +="姓名不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//困难生档次
String typeName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE").trim());
if( Validate.isEmpty(typeName) ){
remark+= "导入失败,困难生档次不能为空.";
}else{
difficultType = typeMap.getString(typeName);
if(Validate.isEmpty(difficultType)){
remark+= "导入失败,困难生档次【" + typeName + "】对应的
代码信息不存在.";
}
}
//认定时间
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("CONFIRM_DATE"))){
confirmDate =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("CONFIRM_DATE").trim());
}else{
remark +="认定时间不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//认定原因
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("APPLY_REASON"))){
applyReason =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("APPLY_REASON").trim());
}else{
remark +="认定原因不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//效验学号和姓名是否一致
HashMap stuValidateMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT
STU_NO,COLLEGE_CODE,SPECIALTY_CODE,CLASS_CODE FROM STUDENT_INFO WHERE STU_NO
= ? AND STU_NAME=? ", stuNo,stuName);
if(stuValidateMap==null) {
remark +="学号【" + stuNo + "】和姓名【"+ stuName +"】对应的
学生不存在.";
errcnt++;
}
//同一学年、学号是否重复导入
if(DifficultValidateUtils.difficultIsApply(this.getSession(), stuNo, null, setup.getSchoolYear(), setup.getTermNum())) {
remark+= "导入失败,学号【" + stuNo + "】对应的学生已导入困难
生名单.";
errcnt++;
}
//没错就进行保存操作
if(errcnt==0) {
try{
SupportDifficultApply apply = new SupportDifficultApply();
apply.setApplyUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("supportdifficultapplyuid"));
apply.setAuditStatus(AuditStageStatusEnum.two_wait.getKey());
apply.setApplyDate(nowDate);
apply.setApplyReason(applyReason);
apply.setApplyRemark(applyRemark);
apply.setConfirmDate(DateUtil.strToDate(confirmDate));
apply.setDifficultTypeUid(difficultType);
apply.setSetupUid(setupUid);
apply.setStuCollegeCode(stuValidateMap.getString("COLLEGE_CODE"));
apply.setStuSpecialtyCode(stuValidateMap.getString("SPECIALTY_CODE"));
apply.setStuClassCode(stuValidateMap.getString("CLASS_CODE"));
apply.setStuNo(stuNo);
apply.setSchoolYear(setup.getSchoolYear());
apply.setTermNum(setup.getTermNum());
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey());
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(),auditFlowUId, apply.getApplyUid(), 1, "0", "修改提交", nowDate, optAccountUid, optAccount);
apply.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
apply.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
apply.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
apply.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(apply);
remark = "学号[" + stuNo + "]导入成功.";
countAdd++;
}catch (Exception e) {
failcnt++;
}
}else {
failcnt++;
}
stuMap.put("IMPREMARK", remark);
}
String rootPath = Configurations.instance().getString("easy.upload.file.path").replace("/",System.getProperty("file.s
eparator"));
//生成处理结果文件
String zdypath = DicConst.IMPSUPPORT_PATH+File.separator;
String excelpath = rootPath + zdypath;
File fDbfpath =new File(excelpath);
//如果文件夹不存在则创建
if (!fDbfpath.exists() && !fDbfpath.isDirectory()){
Logs.log().info( "[" + excelpath + "]不存在,创建" );
fDbfpath .mkdir();
}
String wdbffilename = DicConst.IMPSUPPORT_PATH+"_KNS_" +
DateSource.getTradedate(CFrame.DatePattern5 ) + excelname;
String wdbffilepath = excelpath + wdbffilename;
String cdbffilepath = zdypath + wdbffilename;
File outputFile = new File(wdbffilepath);
// 需要特殊转换的单元
//Map<String, Map> headMap = new java.util.HashMap<String, Map>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(excelColumns.size(), "IMPREMARK", "导
入提示备注"));
head.setRowCount(1); // 模板中头部所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().exportExcelFile(head, fileIS, outputFile, stuList);
//返回数据
surestream.put("resultinfo", "导入困难生名单处理结果,成功[" + countAdd
+"]条,失败["+ failcnt +"]条请下载处理结果文件" );
surestream.put("retfilename", wdbffilename);//处理结果文件名
surestream.put("retfilepath", cdbffilepath);//处理结果文件存放路径
}
} catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "导入操作成功");
//@output
return true;
}
}
package com.easy.modules.support;
import java.util.ArrayList;

@Plugin(
transcode = "difficultAuditManage", transname = "困难生信息审核", author = "lcx", createDate = "2021-12-5"
)
@Transactional
public class DifficultAuditManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream>{
/**
* 审核列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean queryAudit(ESurestream surestream) {
String collegeSelvalue=null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("COLLEGE_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
collegeSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(collegeSelvalue,null);
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_COLLEGE_CODE",arrCode[0],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_SPECIALTY_CODE",arrCode[1],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_CLASS_CODE",arrCode[2],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.counselor.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_CLASS_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.student.getKey().equals(roleType)){
roleSql = " STU_NO = '"+optAccount+"' ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "无权限进行操作");
return true;
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey());
AuditDataUtils.putAuditSql(arrayList, optUid, auditFlowUId);
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("AUDIT_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("AUDIT_STATUS", "AUDIT_AUDIT_STATUS"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM",true));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM",true));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX",true));//性别代码
formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("APPLY_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("APPLY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("CONFIRM_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("CONFIRM_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK",true));//开户行
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT T.APPLY_UID, T.STU_NO, T.SETUP_UID, T.SCHOOL_YEAR, T.TERM_NUM, T.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID, T.APPLY_DATE,
T.CONFIRM_DATE, T.APPLY_REASON, T.APPLY_REMARK, T.AUDIT_STATUS, T.AUDIT_SORT_NO, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE");
sqlBuild.append(" ,T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE,T.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE,T.STU_CLASS_CODE,S.SET
UP_NAME, DT.TYPE_NAME, DT.STANDARD_AMOUNT ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP S ON
S.SETUP_UID=T.SETUP_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE DT ON
DT.TYPE_UID=T.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.AUDIT_STATUS!='-1' ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 困难生提交或审核
* 1、验证该操作用户是否可进行该步骤
* 2、获取下步骤及步骤号
* 3、保存审核人、时间、意见
* 4、同意：继续下一步
* 5、退回: 按退回设置进行处理
* 6、拒绝：根据设置，返回
* **/
@Route
public boolean batchAudit(ESurestream surestream) {
String applyUids = surestream.getString("APPLY_UID");//
String exeStatus = surestream.getString("exeStatus");//执行状态 1 同意 0 退回 -1
拒绝
String exeRemark = surestream.getString("exeRemark","批量审核操作");//执行意见
String typeUid = surestream.getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID");
String isBat = surestream.getString("isBat","0");//是否批量审核操作
if (!Validate.isEmpty(applyUids)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, applyUids.split(","));
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
//单个审核时判定
if(!"1".equals(isBat) && uidList!=null && uidList.size()==1 &&
AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
validatorReason(surestream);
}
for(String id:uidList){
if(Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
continue;
}
SupportDifficultApply apply = this.get(SupportDifficultApply.class, id);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(apply)&&!Validate.isEmpty(apply.getApplyUid())) {
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey());
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(),auditFlowUId, apply.getApplyUid(), apply.getAuditSortNo(), exeStatus,exeRemark, nowDate, optUid, Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream));
//修改该条记录的状态及步骤号
apply.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
apply.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
if(AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_pass.getKey().equals(apply.getAuditStatus())) {
apply.setConfirmDate(nowDate);//认定日期
}
//审核文件材料随审核信息提交 注意：单个审核时才会有修改数据
if(!"1".equals(isBat) && uidList!=null && uidList.size()==1 &&
AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
apply.setDifficultTypeUid(typeUid);
apply.setApplyRemark(surestream.getString("APPLY_REMARK"));
//非取消认定类型的在学院和学生处审核时才有以下两个值
if(!DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey().equals(apply.getDifficultTypeUid()))
{
apply.setApplyReason(surestream.getString("APPLY_REASON"));
if(!Validate.isEmpty(surestream.getString("OTHER_REASON")))
{
apply.setOtherReason(surestream.getString("OTHER_REASON").trim());
}else {
apply.setOtherReason(null);
}
}
}
this.update(apply);
//审核文件材料随审核信息提交
if(AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
//更新文件的业务对象及 ID
String[]
auditfileidsStr=(String[])surestream.getArray("auditfileids[]");
BaseFileUtils.saveBaseFile(this.getSession(), auditfileidsStr, ObjTypeEnum.auditext.getKey(), returnParam.getAuditExtUid());
}
}else {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生信息】不存在");
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 困难生辅导员审核
* 1、验证该操作用户是否可进行该步骤
* 2、获取下步骤及步骤号
* 3、保存审核人、时间、意见
* 4、同意：继续下一步
* 5、退回: 按退回设置进行处理
* 6、拒绝：根据设置，返回
* **/
@Route
public boolean counselorAudit(ESurestream surestream) {
String applyUids = surestream.getString("APPLY_UID");//
String exeStatus = surestream.getString("exeStatus");//执行状态 1 同意 0 退回 -1
拒绝
String exeRemark = surestream.getString("exeRemark","批量审核操作");//执行意见
// String typeUid = surestream.getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID");
// String otherReason = surestream.getString("OTHER_REASON");
// String applyReason = surestream.getString("APPLY_REASON");
if(AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
validatorReason(surestream);
}
if (!Validate.isEmpty(applyUids)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, applyUids.split(","));
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
for(String id:uidList){
if(Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
continue;
}
SupportDifficultApply apply = this.get(SupportDifficultApply.class, id);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(apply)&&!Validate.isEmpty(apply.getApplyUid())) {
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
if(AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
Typecast.hashMap2obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), apply);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(surestream.getString("OTHER_REASON"))) {
apply.setOtherReason(surestream.getString("OTHER_REASON").trim());
}
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey());
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(),auditFlowUId, apply.getApplyUid(), apply.getAuditSortNo(), exeStatus,exeRemark, nowDate, optUid, Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream));
//修改该条记录的状态及步骤号
apply.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
apply.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
apply.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
apply.setUpdateUid(optUid);
this.update(apply);
}else {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生信息】不存在");
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 评定理由验证
* 字符长度不超过 30 个字 含标点符号
* */
private boolean validatorReason(ESurestream surestream) {
String typeUid = surestream.getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID");
String otherReason = surestream.getString("OTHER_REASON");
String applyReason = surestream.getString("APPLY_REASON");
if(Validate.isEmpty(typeUid)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【推荐档次】不能为空！");
}
if(DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey().equals(typeUid)) {
String applyRemark = surestream.getString("APPLY_REMARK");//取消认定理由
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(applyRemark, "【取消原因】不能为空");
}else{
if(Validate.isEmpty(applyReason) && Validate.isEmpty(otherReason)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【评定原由或其他原由】不能为空！");
}
StringBuilder reasonStrB = new StringBuilder();
if(!Validate.isEmpty(applyReason)){
String[] str= applyReason.split(",");
for(String str0:str){
DictionaryTreeNode node = CacheHolderDicTree.getDicByName("SYS_DIFF_APPLY_REASON", str0);
if(node!=null){
reasonStrB.append("，").append(node.getDicName());
}
}
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(otherReason)) {
// String tmpRe = otherReason;
// tmpRe = tmpRe.replaceAll("\\p{P}", "");
// if (tmpRe.length() != otherReason.length()) {
// throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【其他原由】中还有英文字符！");
// }
char[] zs = otherReason.toCharArray();
for(char tt : zs) {
if(!StringUtil.isChinese(tt)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【其他原由】中还有英文字
符！请修改【"+tt+"】");
}
}
reasonStrB.append("，").append(otherReason);
}
String reasonStr = "";
if(reasonStrB!=null && reasonStrB.length()>1) {
reasonStr = reasonStrB.substring(1);
}
if(reasonStr.length()>30) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【评定原由和其他原由】拼接后字符
长度大于 30 个字符！");
}
}
return true;
}
/**
* 辅导员添加困难生档次取消数据
* */
@Route
public boolean counselorAdd(ESurestream surestream) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("SETUP_UID");
String stuNo = surestream.getString("STU_NO");
String applyRemark = surestream.getString("APPLY_REMARK");//取消认定理由
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【开通 ID】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(applyRemark, "【取消原因】不能为空");
SupportDifficultSetup setup = this.get(SupportDifficultSetup.class, setupUid);
if(setup==null || Validate.isEmpty(setup.getSetupUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【设置信息】不存在");
}
if(!"1".equals(setup.getSetupStatus())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生申请批次】未开放，请联系管理
员启用该开通设置");
}
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
if(!DateUtil.isEffectiveDate(nowDate, setup.getBeginDate(), setup.getEndDate())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生申请批次】未开放，请在有效时
间内进行申请");
}
StudentInfo studentInfo = this.get(StudentInfo.class, stuNo);
if(studentInfo==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【学生信息】不存在");
}
SupportDifficultApply diffApply = this.findSingle(SupportDifficultApply.class, DBCondition.form("stuNo", studentInfo.getStuNo())
,DBCondition.form("schoolYear", setup.getSchoolYear()), Order.desc("termNum"));
if(diffApply==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, setup.getSchoolYear()+"年度【困难生评定】
未参与，不能进行申请调整！");
}
if(!AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_pass.getKey().equals(diffApply.getAuditStatus())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, setup.getSchoolYear()+"年度【困难生评定】
未审核通过或正在审核中，不能进行申请调整！");
}
//会出现 一个学期内刚认定通过后 又会休学等情况，需要进行认定取消操作
if(setup.getTermNum().equals(diffApply.getTermNum()) &&
DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey().equals(diffApply.getDifficultTypeUid())) {
String termName = CacheHolderDicTree.getNameByCode("SYS_TERM_NUM", diffApply.getTermNum());
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, setup.getSchoolYear()+"年度【困难生评定】
的"+termName+"学期存在取消认定操作，不能再进行取消认定操作！");
}
SupportDifficultApply apply = new SupportDifficultApply();
Typecast.hashMap2obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), apply);
apply.setApplyUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("difficultapplyuid"));
apply.setStuNo(studentInfo.getStuNo());
apply.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
apply.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
apply.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
apply.setSchoolYear(setup.getSchoolYear());
apply.setTermNum(setup.getTermNum());
apply.setSetupUid(setup.getSetupUid());
apply.setDifficultTypeUid(DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey());
apply.setApplyDate(nowDate);
apply.setApplyUseruid(optAccountUid);
apply.setApplyRemark(applyRemark);//取消原因
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(this.getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey());
if(Validate.isEmpty(auditFlowUId)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【该业务审核流程】未配置，请联系管理
员配置！");
}
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(), auditFlowUId, apply.getApplyUid(), 2, "1", "辅导员提交调整申请", nowDate, optAccountUid, optAccount);
apply.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
apply.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
apply.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
apply.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(apply);
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 按学院班级审核初始化
* **/
@Route
public boolean getBatchNum(ESurestream surestream) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("SETUP_UID");//开通批次
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【开通 ID】不能为空");
String aSelvalue = surestream.getString("BATCH_SELVALUE");//学院/专业/班级
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(aSelvalue,null);
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.counselor.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " T.STU_CLASS_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.student.getKey().equals(roleType)){
roleSql = " T.STU_NO = '"+optAccount+"' ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "您无权限进行操作！");
}
String flowUid = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey());
String auditSql = " T.AUDIT_SORT_NO IN ( SELECT P0.SORT_NO FROM
BASE_AUDIT_STAGE_PERSON P0 WHERE P0.FLOW_UID = '"+flowUid+"' AND (P0.AUDIT_PERSONS ='"+optUid+"' OR P0.AUDIT_ROLES IN (SELECT AR.ROLE_UID from BASE_ACCOUNT_ROLE AR
WHERE AR.ACCOUNT_UID ='"+optUid+"' ) )) ";
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT COUNT(T.APPLY_UID) AS
COUNT_NUM ");
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP S ON
S.SETUP_UID=T.SETUP_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE DT ON
DT.TYPE_UID=T.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.AUDIT_STATUS!='-1' AND T.AUDIT_STATUS=? ");
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.SETUP_UID='"+setupUid+"' ");
sqlBuild.append(" AND " + roleSql);
sqlBuild.append(" AND " + auditSql);
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE='"+arrCode[0]+"' ");
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_CLASS_CODE='"+arrCode[2]+"' ");
String auditStatus = AuditStageRoleEnum.getTypeTitle(roleType);//待审状态 两个
一个待学院审核 一个待学生处
HashMap countMap = this.queryForMap(sqlBuild.toString(), auditStatus);
// @output
surestream.put("data", countMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "获取成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 按学院班级审核
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveBatch(ESurestream surestream) {
String exeStatus = surestream.getString("exeStatus");//执行状态 1 同意 0 退回 -1
拒绝
String exeRemark = surestream.getString("exeRemark","批量审核操作");//执行意见
String setupUid = surestream.getString("SETUP_UID");//开通批次
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【开通 ID】不能为空");
String aSelvalue = surestream.getString("BATCH_SELVALUE");//学院/专业/班级
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(aSelvalue,null);
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
String auditStatus = AuditStageRoleEnum.getTypeTitle(roleType);//待审状态 两个
一个待学院审核 一个待学生处
List<SupportDifficultApply> applyList = this.findMultiple(SupportDifficultApply.class
, DBCondition.form("stuClassCode", arrCode[2]), DBCondition.form("stuSpecialtyCode", arrCode[1]), DBCondition.form("stuCollegeCode", arrCode[0])
, DBCondition.form("setupUid", setupUid), DBCondition.form("auditStatus", setupUid));
if(applyList!=null && applyList.size()>0) {
for(SupportDifficultApply apply:applyList) {
if (!Validate.isEmpty(apply)&&!Validate.isEmpty(apply.getApplyUid())) {
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey());
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(),auditFlowUId, apply.getApplyUid(), apply.getAuditSortNo(), exeStatus,exeRemark, nowDate, optUid, Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream));
//修改该条记录的状态及步骤号
apply.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
apply.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
if(AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_pass.getKey().equals(apply.getAuditStatus())) {
apply.setConfirmDate(nowDate);//认定日期
}
this.update(apply);
//审核文件材料随审核信息提交
if(AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
//更新文件的业务对象及 ID
String[]
auditfileidsStr=(String[])surestream.getArray("auditfileids[]");
BaseFileUtils.saveBaseFile(this.getSession(), auditfileidsStr, ObjTypeEnum.auditext.getKey(), returnParam.getAuditExtUid());
}
}
}
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "批量审核成功");
// @output
return true;
}
}

@Plugin(
transcode = "difficultSetupManage", transname = "困难生开通设置", author = "lcx", createDate = "2021-11-19"
)
@Transactional
public class DifficultSetupManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("SETUP_STATUS",DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,Condition.noteq,new
JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SETUP_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("SETUP_STATUS",
"SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM",true));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM",true));
formats.put("END_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
String sql = "SELECT T.SETUP_UID, T.SETUP_NAME, T.SCHOOL_YEAR, T.TERM_NUM, T.BEGIN_DATE, T.END_DATE, T.SETUP_STATUS, T.SETUP_REMARK, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE
FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP T ";
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sql, arrayList.toArray());
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("setupUid");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【ID】不能为空");
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SETUP_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("SETUP_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("END_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
HashMap setupMap = this.queryForMapByFormat("SELECT T.* FROM
SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP T WHERE T.SETUP_UID =? ", formats, setupUid);
if(setupMap!=null) {
String bStr = setupMap.getString("BEGIN_DATE");
String eStr = setupMap.getString("END_DATE");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(bStr) && !Validate.isEmpty(eStr)) {
setupMap.put("EDU_BEGIN_DATE", bStr+" ~ "+eStr);
}
}
surestream.put("data", setupMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("SETUP_UID");//
String eduDate = surestream.getString("EDU_BEGIN_DATE");//时间段 2020-01--01 - 2021-07-01
String[] dateData = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(eduDate,"~");
try{
SupportDifficultSetup setup = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(setupUid)) {
setup = this.get(SupportDifficultSetup.class, setupUid);
}
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(setup)&&!Validate.isEmpty(setup.getSetupUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), setup);
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(setup.getSetupStatus())) {
setup.setSetupStatus("1");
}
setup.setBeginDate(DateUtil.strToDate(dateData[0]));
setup.setEndDate(DateUtil.strToDate(dateData[1]));
setup.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
setup.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(setup);
} else {
setup = new SupportDifficultSetup();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), setup);
setupUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("supportdifficultsetupuid");
setup.setSetupUid(setupUid);
setup.setBeginDate(DateUtil.strToDate(dateData[0]));
setup.setEndDate(DateUtil.strToDate(dateData[1]));
setup.setSetupStatus("1");
setup.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
setup.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(setup);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 状态修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean updateStatus(ESurestream surestream) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("setupUid");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【ID】不能为空");
if (Validate.isEmpty(dataStatus)) {
dataStatus="0";
}
SupportDifficultSetup setup = this.get(SupportDifficultSetup.class, setupUid);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(setup)&&!Validate.isEmpty(setup.getSetupUid())){
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(dataStatus)) {
if(this.existSQL("SELECT A.SETUP_UID FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A
WHERE A.SETUP_UID=? ", setup.getSetupUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生开通设置信息】已使用，
不能删除！");
}
}
setup.setSetupStatus(dataStatus);
setup.setUpdateDate(DateSource.getTradedate());
setup.setUpdateUid(Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream));
this.update(setup);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生开通设置】不存在");
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
return true;
}
}

@Plugin(
transcode = "difficultStuManage", transname = "我的困难生信息", author = "lcx", createDate = "2022-12-15"
)
@Transactional
public class DifficultStuManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream>{
/**
* 我的困难生列表
* **/
@Route
public boolean queryApply(ESurestream surestream) {
String dataType=null;//已申请 auditData、可申请 applyData、已获得 getData、已
退回 returnData
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("DATA_TYPE".equals(c.getName())) {
dataType = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
// Long optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
arrayList = AuditDataUtils.getStuStatusArrayList(dataType, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM",true));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM",true));
if("applyData".equals(dataType)) {
formats.put("END_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
}else {
formats.put("APPLY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("APPLY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
}
pager.formatsMap(formats);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder("");
if("applyData".equals(dataType)) {
sqlBuild.append(" SELECT T.* FROM (SELECT
S.SCHOOL_YEAR,S.TERM_NUM,S.BEGIN_DATE,S.END_DATE,S.SETUP_UID,S.SETUP_NAME,A.APPL
Y_UID, A.AUDIT_STATUS ");
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP S ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A ON
A.STU_NO='"+optAccount+"' AND A.SETUP_UID=S.SETUP_UID AND A.AUDIT_STATUS!='-1' ");
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE S.SETUP_STATUS='1' ) T "); //可以加当前时间在时间段
的查询条件
}else {
sqlBuild.append(" SELECT T.* FROM (SELECT
A.APPLY_UID,A.STU_NO,A.SCHOOL_YEAR,S.TERM_NUM,A.SETUP_UID,A.APPLY_DATE,A.AUDIT_ST
ATUS,S.SETUP_NAME ");
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A LEFT JOIN
SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP S ON A.SETUP_UID=S.SETUP_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE A.STU_NO='"+optAccount+"' AND
A.AUDIT_STATUS!='-1' AND A.AUDIT_STATUS!='0' ) T ");
}
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
List<HashMap> appList = pager.getDataSource();
if(appList!=null && appList.size()>0) {
for(HashMap dMp:appList) {
dMp.put("tableType", dataType);
if("applyData".equals(dataType)) {
dMp.put("isApply", "0");
Date nowDate =DateSource.getTradedate();
Date beginDate = DateUtil.strToDate(dMp.getString("BEGIN_DATE"));
Date endDate = DateUtil.strToDate(dMp.getString("END_DATE"));
if(DateUtil.isEffectiveDate(nowDate, beginDate, endDate)) {
dMp.put("isApply", "1");
}
}
dMp.put("END_DATE", dMp.getString("BEGIN_DATE") + " ~ " +
dMp.getString("END_DATE"));
}
}
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getApplyMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("setupUid");
String applyUid = surestream.getString("applyUid");
String isView = surestream.getString("isView","0");
HashMap applyMap = null;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(applyUid)) {
applyMap = this.getApplyMap(applyUid, isView);
}else {
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("END_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【设置 ID】不能为空");
HashMap stuMap = StuDataUtils.getStuMapByNo(getSession(), optAccount);
if(stuMap==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【学生信息数据】不存在！");
}
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT
S.SCHOOL_YEAR,S.TERM_NUM,S.BEGIN_DATE,S.END_DATE,S.SETUP_UID,S.SETUP_STATUS,S.SETU
P_NAME FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP S WHERE S.SETUP_UID=? ");
applyMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, setupUid);
applyMap.putAll(stuMap);
}
surestream.put("data", applyMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 申请撤回和取消申请操作
* **/
@Route
public boolean deleteStu(ESurestream surestream) {
String applyUid = surestream.getString("applyUid");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus","0");//0 撤回成草稿，-1 取消删除
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(applyUid, "【ID】不能为空");
String stuNo = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);//学号
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
SupportDifficultApply apply = this.get(SupportDifficultApply.class, applyUid);
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(apply)&&!Validate.isEmpty(apply.getApplyUid())){
SupportDifficultSetup setup = this.get(SupportDifficultSetup.class, apply.getSetupUid());
if(!stuNo.equals(apply.getStuNo())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【非本人申请记录】不能处理");
}
if(AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_draft.getKey().equals(dataStatus)) {//撤回操作
if(!DateUtil.isEffectiveDate(nowDate, setup.getBeginDate(),
setup.getEndDate())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【该困难生申请批次】已关闭，
不能操作");
}
if(DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey().equals(apply.getDifficultTypeUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "该批次【困难生评定】已被辅导
员取消认定，不能撤回");
}
}
if(!AuditStageStatusEnum.one_return.getKey().equals(apply.getAuditStatus())
&& !AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_draft.getKey().equals(apply.getAuditStatus()) &&
AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_delete.getKey().equals(dataStatus)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生已提交申请】不能直接取消，
请先撤回");
}
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(this.getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey());
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(), auditFlowUId, apply.getApplyUid(), 1, dataStatus, " 撤 回 或 删 除 ", nowDate, Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream), optAccount);
apply.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
apply.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
apply.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
apply.setUpdateUid(Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream));
this.update(apply);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难生信息】不存在");
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
//@output
return true;
}
/**
* 学生自行修改
* 草稿修改或申请提交
* 后续，判断学生是否有资格申请
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveStuApply(ESurestream surestream) {
String applyUid = surestream.getString("APPLY_UID");//
String setupUid = surestream.getString("SETUP_UID");
String stuNo = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);//学号
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【设置 ID】不能为空");
DifficultDateUtils.saveOrUpdateApply(this.getSession(),setupUid, applyUid, stuNo, 1, surestream);
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
private HashMap getApplyMap(String applyUid,String isView) {
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("END_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX"));//性别代码
formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK"));//开户行
formats.put("IS_PROMISE", new FormatDic2Str("IS_PROMISE", "SYS_WHETHER"));
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("AUDIT_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("AUDIT_STATUS", "AUDIT_AUDIT_STATUS"));
formats.put("APPLY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("APPLY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));//申请时间
formats.put("CONFIRM_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("CONFIRM_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));//认定日期
formats.put("APPLY_REASON", new FormatDic2Str("APPLY_REASON", "SYS_DIFF_APPLY_REASON"));//
formats.put("HOUSEHOLD_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("HOUSEHOLD_CODE", "SYS_DM_HOUSEHOLDTYPE"));//户口
formats.put("BIRTHDAY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("BIRTHDAY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.*, S.SETUP_NAME,S.BEGIN_DATE,S.END_DATE ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" ,D.TYPE_NAME AS DIFFICULT_TYPE_NAME, SAN.AREA_NAME AS
NATIVE_NAME");
sqlBuild.append(" ,SI.NATIVE_CODE AS STU_NATIVE_CODE,E.HOME_TEL AS
STU_HOME_TEL,E.HOME_ADDRESS AS STU_HOME_ADDRESS,E.HOME_POST AS
STU_HOME_POST ");
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_SETUP S ON
S.SETUP_UID=T.SETUP_UID ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN STUDENT_INFO_EXT E ON E.STU_NO_EXT=T.STU_NO ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE D ON
D.TYPE_UID=T.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN BASE_SYS_AREA SAN ON
SAN.AREA_CODE=SI.NATIVE_CODE ");//籍贯
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.APPLY_UID = ? ");
HashMap applyMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, applyUid);
if(applyMap!=null) {
if("1".equals(isView)) {
applyMap.put("auditExeList", AuditDataUtils.getAuditExeList(this.getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey(), applyMap.getString("APPLY_UID"),true));
String specialType = applyMap.getString("SPECIAL_TYPE");
List<HashMap> specialList = CacheHolderDicTree.getDicListByCode("SYS_DIFF_SPECIAL_TYPE");
if(specialList!=null) {
for(HashMap smap : specialList) {
String idCode = smap.getString("ID");
if( !Validate.isEmpty(specialType) && specialType.contains(idCode))
{
smap.put("YES", "checked");
}else {
smap.put("NO", "checked");
}
}
}
applyMap.put("specialList", specialList);
//公示和评议文件
applyMap.put("recodeList",BaseFileUtils.getRecodeList(getSession(),
applyMap.getString("STU_CLASS_CODE"), applyMap.getString("STU_COLLEGE_CODE"), applyMap.getString("SCHOOL_YEAR"), applyMap.getString("TERM_NUM"), ObjTypeEnum.difficult.getKey()));
//学籍异动数据
if(!Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID")) &&
DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey().equals(applyMap.getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID"))) {
applyMap.put("ydList", StuXjDataUtils.getStuYdNo(applyMap.getString("STU_NO")));
}
}
formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("BIRTHDAY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("BIRTHDAY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("RELATION_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("RELATION_CODE", "SYS_DM_RELATION"));
formats.put("HEALTH_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("HEALTH_CODE", "SYS_DM_HEALTH"));
String sql = "SELECT
DFAMILY_UID,APPLY_UID,STU_NO,RELATION_CODE,MEMBER_NAME,BIRTHDAY_DATE,WORK_UN
IT,TITLES_NAME,INCOME_YEAR,HEALTH_CODE FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_FAMILY WHERE
APPLY_UID=? AND DATA_STATUS=? ";
try {
List<HashMap> familyList = this.jdbcQueryByFormat(sql,formats, applyUid, "1");
applyMap.put("familyList",familyList);
} catch (SQLException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
return applyMap;
}

/**
SELECT T.* FROM (
SELECT
E.EXE_UID,E.EXE_DATE,E.EXE_USER,E.EXE_USER_NAME,E.STAGE_UID,S.SORT_NO,E.EXE_REMARK, E.AUDIT_STATUS
,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY E.STAGE_UID ORDER BY S.SORT_NO ASC,E.EXE_DATE DESC)
RW
FROM BASE_AUDIT_EXE E
LEFT JOIN BASE_AUDIT_STAGE S ON E.STAGE_UID=S.STAGE_UID
WHERE E.OBJ_UID='997366520738758656' AND E.OBJ_TYPE='supportdifficult' ORDER BY S.SORT_NO ASC,E.EXE_DATE DESC) T WHERE T.RW=1
* 申请表导出
* **/
@Route
public boolean expPdf(ESurestream surestream) {
String applyUid = surestream.getString("applyUid");
HashMapapplyMap = this.getApplyMap(applyUid, "1");
if(applyMap!=null) {
//项目部署根路径
String SUB_FILE_DIR = SingletonService.getRealPath();
InputStream in = null;
try {
WordToPdfUtils wordToPdfUtils = new WordToPdfUtils(new
FileInputStream(new
File(SUB_FILE_DIR+"template/support/exp_kns.docx".replace("/",System.getProperty("file.separ
ator")))));
Map<String, Object> context = new java.util.HashMap<>();
@SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
List<HashMap> familyList = (List<HashMap>)applyMap.get("familyList");
List<StuFamilyVo> familys = new ArrayList<>();
if(familyList!=null && familyList.size()>0) {
for(HashMap tmap : familyList){
String birDateS = tmap.getString("BIRTHDAY_DATE");
String ages = "";
if(!Validate.isEmpty(birDateS)) {
Date birDate = DateUtil.strToDate(birDateS);
if(DateUtil.getAge(birDate)!=0) {
ages = String.valueOf(DateUtil.getAge(birDate));
}
}
familys.add(new
StuFamilyVo(tmap.getString("DFAMILY_UID"),tmap.getString("MEMBER_NAME"),String.valueOf(
ages),tmap.getString("RELATION_CODE_SV")
,tmap.getString("WORK_UNIT"),tmap.getString("TITLES_NAME"),tmap.getString("INCOME_
YEAR"),tmap.getString("HEALTH_CODE_SV")));
}
}else {
familys.add(new StuFamilyVo("1"," "," "," "," "," "," ", ""));
}
context.put("familys", familys);
//将需要替换的数据数据添加到上下文中
//其中 key 为 word 模板中的域名，value 是需要替换的值
context.put("SCHOOL_NAME", DicConst.DEFAULT_SCHOOLNAME);
context.put("STU_COLLEGE_NAME", applyMap.getString("STU_COLLEGE_NAME"));
context.put("STU_GRADE_CODE", applyMap.getString("STU_GRADE_CODE"));
context.put("STU_SPECIALTY_NAME", applyMap.getString("STU_SPECIALTY_NAME"));
context.put("STU_CLASS_NAME", applyMap.getString("STU_CLASS_NAME"));
context.put("STU_STU_NAME", applyMap.getString("STU_STU_NAME"));
context.put("STU_SEX_CODE_SV", applyMap.getString("STU_SEX_CODE_SV"));
context.put("BIRTHDAY_DATE", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("BIRTHDAY_DATE"))?apply
Map.getString("BIRTHDAY_DATE"):"");//出生日期
context.put("NATIVE_NAME", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("NATIVE_NAME"))?applyMa
p.getString("NATIVE_NAME"):"");//籍贯
context.put("CARD_NUM", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_CARD_NUM"))?applyMa
p.getString("STU_CARD_NUM"):"");
context.put("FAMILY_NUM", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("FAMILY_NUM"))?applyMap. getString("FAMILY_NUM"):"");//家庭人口
context.put("STU_TEL_NUM", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_TEL_NUM"))?applyM
ap.getString("STU_TEL_NUM"):"");
context.put("STU_HOME_ADDRESS", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_HOME_ADDRE
SS"))?applyMap.getString("STU_HOME_ADDRESS"):"");
context.put("STU_HOME_POST", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_HOME_POST"))?ap
plyMap.getString("STU_HOME_POST"):"");//
context.put("STU_HOME_TEL", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_HOME_TEL"))?apply
Map.getString("STU_HOME_TEL"):"");
context.put("PER_CAPITA_INCOME", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("PER_CAPITA_INCOM
E"))?applyMap.getString("PER_CAPITA_INCOME"):"");
context.put("NATURAL_DISASTER", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("NATURAL_DISASTER"))
?applyMap.getString("NATURAL_DISASTER"):"");//家庭遭受自然灾害情况
context.put("ACCIDENT_EVENT", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("ACCIDENT_EVENT"))?ap
plyMap.getString("ACCIDENT_EVENT"):"");//家庭遭受突发意外事件
context.put("DISABILITY_EVENT", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("DISABILITY_EVENT"))?a
pplyMap.getString("DISABILITY_EVENT"):"");//家庭成员因残疾、年迈而劳动能力弱情况
context.put("LOSE_JOB", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("LOSE_JOB"))?applyMap.getStrin
g("LOSE_JOB"):"");//家庭成员失业情况
context.put("DEBT_EVENT", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("DEBT_EVENT"))?applyMap.g
etString("DEBT_EVENT"):"");//家庭欠债情况
context.put("OTHER_EVENT", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("OTHER_EVENT"))?applyMa
p.getString("OTHER_EVENT"):"");//其他情况
if(!Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("IS_PROMISE")) &&
"1".equals(applyMap.getString("IS_PROMISE"))) {
context.put("PROMISE_REMARK", "本人承诺以上所填写资料真实，如
有虚假，愿承担相应责任。");//
}else {
context.put("PROMISE_REMARK", "");
}
context.put("APPLY_REASON", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("APPLY_REASON_SV"))?app
lyMap.getString("APPLY_REASON_SV"):"");//评定原由
context.put("OTHER_REASON", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("OTHER_REASON"))?apply
Map.getString("OTHER_REASON"):"");//评定其他原由
String diffType = applyMap.getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID");
context.put("DIFFICULT_TYPE_A", "□");//推荐档次
context.put("DIFFICULT_TYPE_B", "□");//推荐档次
context.put("DIFFICULT_TYPE_C", "□");//推荐档次
context.put("DIFFICULT_TYPE_D", "□");//推荐档次
if(DifficultTypeEnum.A.getKey().equals(diffType)) {
context.put("DIFFICULT_TYPE_A", "☑");//
}else if(DifficultTypeEnum.B.getKey().equals(diffType)) {
context.put("DIFFICULT_TYPE_B", "☑");//推荐档次
}else if(DifficultTypeEnum.C.getKey().equals(diffType)) {
context.put("DIFFICULT_TYPE_C", "☑");//推荐档次
}else {
//context.put("DIFFICULT_TYPE_D", "☑");//
}
@SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
List<HashMap> specialList = (List<HashMap>)applyMap.get("specialList");
if(specialList!=null) {
for(HashMap tmap : specialList){
String id = tmap.getString("ID");
String speStr = "";
if("checked".equals(tmap.getString("YES"))) {
speStr = "☑ 是 □否";
}else {
speStr = "□是 □否";
}
context.put("SPECIAL_"+id, speStr);//
}
}
//添加每个步骤的审核日期
HashMap dataMap = AuditDataUtils.getAuditDate(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportdifficult.getKey(), applyUid);
context.putAll(dataMap);
String stuNo = applyMap.getString("STU_STU_NO");
//组装数据
wordToPdfUtils.assembleMap(context);
String fileName = stuNo+"_ 困 难 生 申 请 表
_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+ ".docx";
//生成 pdf
// File outputFile = new File("D:/ok_template.pdf");
// OutputStream outputStream = new FileOutputStream(outputFile);
// wordToPdfUtils.createPdf(outputStream);
wordToPdfUtils.downWord(surestream.response(), fileName);
// wordToPdfUtils.downPdf(surestream.response(), fileName);
Logs.log( ).info("*********************"+stuNo +"的困难生申请表导出成
功" );
} catch (IOException e) {
Logs.log( ).error("困难生申请表导出，读取 Word 模板异常",e);
// logger.error("读取 Word 模板异常",e);
} catch (XDocReportException e) {
Logs.log( ).error("困难生申请表导出，模板生成失败",e);
} catch (Exception e) {
//e.printStackTrace();
}finally {
if(in!=null){
try {
in.close();
} catch (IOException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
}
}
return true;
}

package com.easy.modules.support;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Date;
import java.util.List;

import com.easy.asgi.footstone.egi.IFormatField;

import com.easy.asgi.footstone.exception.RWarn;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.stereotype.Plugin;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.stereotype.Transactional;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.stereotype.method.Route;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.util.HashMap;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.db.format.FormatDate2Str;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.ega.genericity.AbstractSessionComponent;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.struct.pojo.Condition;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.struct.pojo.JoinCondition;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.struct.pojo.QResultSet;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.util.DateSource;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.util.TryThrowable;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.util.Validate;
import com.easy.asgi.framework.util.ValidatorSupport;
import com.easy.entity.support.SupportDifficultType;
import com.easy.framework.common.Accountmgt;
import com.easy.framework.common.DcKeyGenerate;
import com.easy.framework.common.DicConst;
import com.easy.framework.format.FormatDic2Str;
import com.easy.framework.layui.LayUiTableUtils;
import com.easy.framework.standard.ESurestream;
@Plugin(
transcode = "difficultTypeManage", transname = "困难生困难类型", author = "lcx", createDate = "2021-11-19"
)
@Transactional
public class DifficultTypeManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("DATA_STATUS",DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,Condition.noteq,new
JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("DATA_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("DATA_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss"));
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
String sql = "SELECT T.TYPE_UID, T.TYPE_NAME, T.STANDARD_AMOUNT, T.DATA_STATUS, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE T ";
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sql, arrayList.toArray());
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String typeUid = surestream.getString("typeUid");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(typeUid, "【ID】不能为空");
HashMap typeMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT T.* FROM SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_TYPE T
WHERE T.TYPE_UID =? ", typeUid);
surestream.put("data", typeMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String typeUid = surestream.getString("TYPE_UID");//困难类型 ID
try{
SupportDifficultType type = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(typeUid)) {
type = this.get(SupportDifficultType.class, typeUid);
}
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(type)&&!Validate.isEmpty(type.getTypeUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), type);
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(type.getDataStatus())) {
type.setDataStatus("1");
}
type.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
type.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(type);
} else {
type = new SupportDifficultType();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), type);
typeUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("supportdifficulttypeuid");
type.setTypeUid(typeUid);
type.setDataStatus("1");
type.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
type.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(type);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 状态修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean updateStatus(ESurestream surestream) {
String typeUid = surestream.getString("typeUid");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(typeUid, "【ID】不能为空");
if (Validate.isEmpty(dataStatus)) {
dataStatus="0";
}
SupportDifficultType type = this.get(SupportDifficultType.class, typeUid);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(type)&&!Validate.isEmpty(type.getTypeUid())){
type.setDataStatus(dataStatus);
type.setUpdateDate(DateSource.getTradedate());
type.setUpdateUid(Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream));
this.update(type);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【困难类型信息】不存在");
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "设置成功");
return true;
}
}
package com.easy.modules.support;
import java.util.ArrayList;
