import com.easy.modules.stu.util.StuDataUtils;
@Plugin(
transcode = "grantApplyManage", transname = "助学金信息",
author = "lcx", createDate = "2022-12-08"
)
@Transactional
public class GrantApplyManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
String collegeSelvalue=null,ocollegeSelvalue=null;
String isE="0";//是否导出
String isRepeat = null,schoolYear=null,termNum=null,auditStatus=null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("COLLEGE_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
collegeSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("OCOLLEGE_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
ocollegeSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("isE".equals(c.getName())) {
isE = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("IS_REPEAT".equals(c.getName())) {
isRepeat = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("SCHOOL_YEAR".equals(c.getName())) {
schoolYear = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("TERM_NUM".equals(c.getName())) {
termNum = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("AUDIT_STATUS".equals(c.getName())) {
auditStatus = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(collegeSelvalue,null);
String[] arrCodeO = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(ocollegeSelvalue,null);
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
//学年
if(!Validate.isEmpty(schoolYear)) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("SCHOOL_YEAR",schoolYear,Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
//学期
if(!Validate.isEmpty(termNum)) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("TERM_NUM",termNum,Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
// Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_COLLEGE_CODE",arrCode[0],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
// arrayList.add(otherCondition);
// }
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
// Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_SPECIALTY_CODE",arrCode[1],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
// arrayList.add(otherCondition);
// }
// if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
// Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_CLASS_CODE",arrCode[2],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
// arrayList.add(otherCondition);
// }
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.counselor.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_CLASS_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.student.getKey().equals(roleType)){
roleSql = " STU_NO = '"+optAccount+"' ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "无权限进行操作");
return true;
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
// isRepeat:1 学年去重 2 学期去重
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isRepeat) && !Validate.isEmpty(schoolYear)) {
if("1".equals(isRepeat)) {//学年去重
Condition otherCondition = new Condition("RW", isRepeat, Condition.eq,new
JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}else if("2".equals(isRepeat) && !Validate.isEmpty(termNum)) {//春季去重 主要
查询 秋季不是困难生 春季是困难生的人员
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(" STU_NO NOT
IN (SELECT A.STU_NO FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY A WHERE
A.SCHOOL_YEAR='"+schoolYear+"' AND A.TERM_NUM!='"+termNum+"' AND
A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' ) "));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
}
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("AUDIT_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("AUDIT_STATUS", "AUDIT_AUDIT_STATUS"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM",true));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM",true));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX",true));//性别代码
// formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("APPLY_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("APPLY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK",true));//开户行
formats.put("STU_ENROL_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("STU_ENROL_DATE","yyyy-MM",true));
// formats.put("APPLY_REASON", new FormatDic2Str("APPLY_REASON", "SYS_GRANT_APPLY_REASON"));
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
//数据导出不进行分页处理
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
pager.setPageSize(-1);
pager.setPageNo(-1);
}
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT T.SETUP_UID, T.GRANT_UID, T.SCHOOL_YEAR, T.TERM_NUM, T.STU_NO, T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE, T.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE, T.STU_CLASS_CODE, T.GRANT_GRADE, T.SHOULD_AMOUNT, T.ACTUAL_AMOUNT, T.APPLY_REASON, T.OTHER_REASON, T.GRANT_REMARK,T.COLLEGE_BULLETIN, T.SCHOOL_BULLETIN, T.AUDIT_STATUS, T.AUDIT_SORT_NO, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE, T.APPLY_USERUID, T.APPLY_DATE ");
sqlBuild.append(" ,S.SETUP_NAME , RT.TYPE_NAME AS GRANT_GRADE_NAME ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isRepeat) && !Validate.isEmpty(schoolYear)) {
sqlBuild.append(" ,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY T.STU_NO ORDER BY
T.SCHOOL_YEAR DESC,T.TERM_NUM DESC)
RW,I.COLLEGE_CODE,I.SPECIALTY_CODE,I.CLASS_CODE ");
}
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY T LEFT JOIN STUDENT_INFO I ON
I.STU_NO=T.STU_NO ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_GRANT_SETUP S ON S.SETUP_UID=T.SETUP_UID
");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_STU_TYPE RT ON RT.TYPE_CODE =
T.GRANT_GRADE AND RT.TYPE_LEVEL='3' ");
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.AUDIT_STATUS!='-1' ");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isRepeat) && !Validate.isEmpty(schoolYear)) {
if("1".equals(isRepeat)) {//学年去重
/**
* 1、由于学生的助学金和定期困难补助只能二选一
* 2、学年去重查询 需要过滤学生春季学期由助学金换成定期困难补助
的数据
* **/
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.SCHOOL_YEAR='"+schoolYear+"' AND
(T.AUDIT_STATUS='100' OR T.AUDIT_STATUS='30' OR T.AUDIT_STATUS='20')");
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_NO NOT IN (SELECT A.STU_NO FROM
SUPPORT_SUBSIDY_APPLY A WHERE A.SCHOOL_YEAR='"+schoolYear+"' AND A.TERM_NUM='2' AND (A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' OR A.AUDIT_STATUS='30' OR T.AUDIT_STATUS='20' ) ) ");
}else {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.SCHOOL_YEAR='"+schoolYear+"' AND
(T.AUDIT_STATUS='100' OR T.AUDIT_STATUS='30' )");
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_NO NOT IN (SELECT A.STU_NO FROM
SUPPORT_SUBSIDY_APPLY A WHERE A.SCHOOL_YEAR='"+schoolYear+"' AND A.TERM_NUM='2' AND (A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' OR A.AUDIT_STATUS='30' ) ) ");
}
//困难生取消认定的要排除
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_NO NOT IN (select A.STU_NO from
SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY A WHERE A.SCHOOL_YEAR='"+schoolYear+"' AND A.TERM_NUM='2' AND A.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID='D' AND A.AUDIT_STATUS='100' )");
}
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND I.COLLEGE_CODE='"+arrCode[0]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND I.SPECIALTY_CODE='"+arrCode[1]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND I.CLASS_CODE='"+arrCode[2]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCodeO[0])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE='"+arrCodeO[0]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCodeO[1])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE='"+arrCodeO[1]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCodeO[2])) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.STU_CLASS_CODE='"+arrCodeO[2]+"' ");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(auditStatus)) {
sqlBuild.append(" AND T.AUDIT_STATUS='"+auditStatus+"' ");
}
sqlBuild.append(" ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
List<HashMap> statisticsList = pager.getDataSource();
if(statisticsList!=null) {
for(HashMap smap:statisticsList) {
if(Validate.isEmpty(smap.get("STU_BANK_ANAME"))) {
smap.put("STU_BANK_ANAME", smap.get("STU_STU_NAME"));
}
String applyReason = smap.getString("APPLY_REASON");
StringBuilder reasonStrB = new StringBuilder();
boolean isVother = false;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(applyReason)){
String[] str= applyReason.split(",");
for(String str0:str){
if("H".equals(str0)) {
isVother=true;
continue;
}
DictionaryTreeNode node = CacheHolderDicTree.getDicByName("SYS_GRANT_APPLY_REASON", str0);
if(node!=null){
reasonStrB.append("，").append(node.getDicName());
}
}
smap.put("APPLY_REASON", applyReason.replaceAll(",", "，"));
}
if(isVother) {
if(!Validate.isEmpty(smap.getString("OTHER_REASON"))) {
reasonStrB.append(" ，
").append(smap.getString("OTHER_REASON"));
}else {
if(!Validate.isEmpty(smap.getString("GRANT_REMARK"))) {
reasonStrB.append(" ，
").append(smap.getString("GRANT_REMARK").replaceAll(",", "，"));
}
}
}
String reasonStr = " ";
if(reasonStrB!=null && reasonStrB.length()>1) {
reasonStr = reasonStrB.substring(1);
}
smap.put("APPLY_REASON_SV", reasonStr);
}
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
exportData(statisticsList, surestream);
}else {
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
}
return true;
}
/**
* 数据导出
* */
public boolean exportData(List<HashMap> statisticsList,ESurestream surestream){
try {
if(statisticsList!=null&&statisticsList.size()>0){
String[] headers={"学生姓名","身份证号","学院","专业","学号","班级","性
别","民族","入学年月", "受助类别","资助标准(元/学期)","实发金额","学年","学期","开
户行","银行账号","银行卡户名","申请理由代码","申请理由","批次"};
String[]
column={"STU_STU_NAME","STU_CARD_NUM","STU_COLLEGE_NAME","STU_SPECIALTY_NAME
","STU_NO","STU_CLASS_NAME","STU_SEX_CODE","","STU_ENROL_DATE", "GRANT_GRADE_NAME","SHOULD_AMOUNT","ACTUAL_AMOUNT","SCHOOL_YEAR","TER
M_NUM","STU_BANK_NAME","STU_BANK_CODE","STU_BANK_ANAME","APPLY_REASON","APP
LY_REASON_SV","SETUP_NAME"};
String title=" 国 家 助 学 金 名 单
_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+ ".xlsx";
ExportExcel<HashMap> exp = new ExportExcel<HashMap>();
exp.writeExcel(title, headers, statisticsList, "yyyy-MM-dd", surestream.response(), column);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
return true;
}
/**
* 审核列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean queryAudit(ESurestream surestream) {
String collegeSelvalue=null;
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("COLLEGE_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
collegeSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
QResultSet pager = queryCommon( surestream, true,collegeSelvalue,DicConst.DIC_COM_NO);
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* isAudit 是否审核页调用
* */
private QResultSet queryCommon(ESurestream surestream,boolean isAudit,String
collegeSelvalue,String isE) {
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(collegeSelvalue,null);
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_COLLEGE_CODE",arrCode[0],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_SPECIALTY_CODE",arrCode[1],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_CLASS_CODE",arrCode[2],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.counselor.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_CLASS_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.student.getKey().equals(roleType)){
roleSql = " STU_NO = '"+optAccount+"' ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
return pager;
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
//获取待审核数据
if(isAudit) {
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey());
AuditDataUtils.putAuditSql(arrayList, optUid, auditFlowUId);
}
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("AUDIT_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("AUDIT_STATUS", "AUDIT_AUDIT_STATUS"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM",true));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM",true));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX",true));//性别代码
// formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("APPLY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("APPLY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK",true));//开户行
formats.put("STU_ENROL_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("STU_ENROL_DATE","yyyy-MM",true));
formats.put("APPLY_REASON", new FormatDic2Str("APPLY_REASON", "SYS_GRANT_APPLY_REASON"));
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
//数据导出不进行分页处理
if(!Validate.isEmpty(isE)&&"1".equals(isE)){
pager.setPageSize(-1);
pager.setPageNo(-1);
}
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT
T.SETUP_UID, T.GRANT_UID, T.SCHOOL_YEAR, T.TERM_NUM, T.STU_NO, T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE, T.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE, T.STU_CLASS_CODE, T.GRANT_GRADE, T.SHOULD_AMOUNT, T.ACTUAL_AMOUNT, T.APPLY_REASON, T.COLLEGE_BULLETIN, T.SCHOOL_BULLETIN, T.AUDIT_STATUS, T.AUDIT_SORT_NO, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE, T.APPLY_USERUID, T.APPLY_DATE ");
sqlBuild.append(" ,S.SETUP_NAME , RT.TYPE_NAME AS GRANT_GRADE_NAME ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_GRANT_SETUP S ON
S.SETUP_UID=T.SETUP_UID ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_STU_TYPE RT ON RT.TYPE_CODE =
T.GRANT_GRADE AND RT.TYPE_LEVEL='3' ");
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.AUDIT_STATUS!='-1' ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
return pager;
}
/**
* 助学金提交或审核
* 1、验证该操作用户是否可进行该步骤
* 2、获取下步骤及步骤号
* 3、保存审核人、时间、意见
* 4、同意：继续下一步
* 5、退回: 按退回设置进行处理
* 6、拒绝：根据设置，返回
* **/
@Route
public boolean batchAudit(ESurestream surestream) {
String grantUids = surestream.getString("GRANT_UID");//
String exeStatus = surestream.getString("exeStatus");//执行状态 1 同意 0 退回 -1
拒绝
String exeRemark = surestream.getString("exeRemark","批量审核操作");//执行意见
String isBat = surestream.getString("isBat","0");//是否批量审核操作
if (!Validate.isEmpty(grantUids)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, grantUids.split(","));
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
//单个审核时判定
if(!"1".equals(isBat) && uidList!=null && uidList.size()==1 &&
AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
validatorReason(surestream);
}
for(String id:uidList){
if(Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
continue;
}
SupportGrantApply apply = this.get(SupportGrantApply.class, id);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(apply)&&!Validate.isEmpty(apply.getGrantUid())) {
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
if(!"1".equals(isBat) && uidList!=null && uidList.size()==1 &&
AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
Typecast.hashMap2obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), apply);
}
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey());
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(),auditFlowUId, apply.getGrantUid(), apply.getAuditSortNo(), exeStatus,exeRemark, nowDate, optUid, Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream));
//修改该条记录的状态及步骤号
apply.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
apply.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
if(AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_pass.getKey().equals(apply.getAuditStatus())) {
//院系和学校公示天数填写？？？？？
// apply.setCollegeBulletin(collegeBulletin);
// apply.setSchoolBulletin(schoolBulletin);
//apply.setActualAmount(apply.getShouldAmount());
}
this.update(apply);
//审核文件材料随审核信息提交
if(AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
//更新文件的业务对象及 ID
String[]
auditfileidsStr=(String[])surestream.getArray("auditfileids[]");
BaseFileUtils.saveBaseFile(this.getSession(), auditfileidsStr, ObjTypeEnum.auditext.getKey(), returnParam.getAuditExtUid());
}
}else {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【助学金信息】不存在");
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 助学金辅导员审核
* 1、验证该操作用户是否可进行该步骤
* 2、获取下步骤及步骤号
* 3、保存审核人、时间、意见
* 4、同意：继续下一步
* 5、退回: 按退回设置进行处理
* 6、拒绝：根据设置，返回
* **/
@Route
public boolean counselorAudit(ESurestream surestream) {
String grantUids = surestream.getString("GRANT_UID");//
String exeStatus = surestream.getString("exeStatus");//执行状态 1 同意 0 退回 -1
拒绝
String exeRemark = surestream.getString("exeRemark","批量审核操作");//执行意见
if(AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
validatorReason(surestream);
}
if (!Validate.isEmpty(grantUids)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, grantUids.split(","));
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
for(String id:uidList){
if(Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
continue;
}
SupportGrantApply apply = this.get(SupportGrantApply.class, id);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(apply)&&!Validate.isEmpty(apply.getGrantUid())) {
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
if(AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
Typecast.hashMap2obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), apply);
}
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey());
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(),auditFlowUId, apply.getGrantUid(), apply.getAuditSortNo(), exeStatus,exeRemark, nowDate, optUid, Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream));
//修改该条记录的状态及步骤号
apply.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
apply.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
apply.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
apply.setUpdateUid(optUid);
this.update(apply);
}else {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【助学金信息】不存在");
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 字符长度不超过 100 个字 含标点符号
* */
private boolean validatorReason(ESurestream surestream) {
String otherReason = surestream.getString("OTHER_REASON");
String applyReason = surestream.getString("APPLY_REASON");
String grantGrade = surestream.getString("GRANT_GRADE");//
String shouldAmount = surestream.getString("SHOULD_AMOUNT");//
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(grantGrade, "【助学金等级】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(shouldAmount, "【应发金额】不能为空");
if(Validate.isEmpty(applyReason) && Validate.isEmpty(otherReason)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【评定原由】不能为空！");
}
StringBuilder reasonStrB = new StringBuilder();
boolean isVother = false;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(applyReason)){
String[] str= applyReason.split(",");
for(String str0:str){
if("H".equals(str0)) {
isVother=true;
continue;
}
DictionaryTreeNode node = CacheHolderDicTree.getDicByName("SYS_GRANT_APPLY_REASON", str0);
if(node!=null){
reasonStrB.append("，").append(node.getDicName());
}
}
}
if(isVother && Validate.isEmpty(otherReason)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【评定原由为其他】，请完善补充原由！");
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(otherReason)) {
char[] zs = otherReason.toCharArray();
for(char tt : zs) {
if((tt >= '0') && (tt <= '9')) {//数字判断
continue;
}
if(!StringUtil.isChinese(tt)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【补充原由】中还有英文字符！
请修改【"+tt+"】");
}
}
reasonStrB.append("，").append(otherReason);
}
String reasonStr = "";
if(reasonStrB!=null && reasonStrB.length()>1) {
reasonStr = reasonStrB.substring(1);
}
if(reasonStr.length()>100) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【评判原由和补充原由】拼接后字符长度
大于 100 个字符！");
}
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
*@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String grantUid = surestream.getString("grantUid");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(grantUid, "【ID】不能为空");
HashMap grantMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT T.* FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY T
WHERE T.GRANT_UID =? ", grantUid);
surestream.put("data", grantMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
} **/
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String grantUid = surestream.getString("GRANT_UID");//
String stuNo = surestream.getString("STU_NO");//学号
String setupUid = surestream.getString("SETUP_UID");//开通设置 ID
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(grantUid, "【助学金申请 ID】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【助学金开通设置 ID】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
try{
SupportGrantApply grant = this.get(SupportGrantApply.class, grantUid);
if (grant==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【助学金申请信息】不存在");
}
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(grant)&&!Validate.isEmpty(grant.getGrantUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), grant);
grant.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
grant.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(grant);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 批量删除
* id 以逗号,拼接
* **/
@Route
public boolean delete(ESurestream surestream) {
String grantUid = surestream.getString("grantUid");
try{
if (!Validate.isEmpty(grantUid)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, grantUid.split(","));
String optUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
for(String id:uidList){
//判断为空
if(!Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
this.update("UPDATE SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY SET
AUDIT_STATUS=?, UPDATE_UID=? ,UPDATE_DATE=SYSDATE WHERE GRANT_UID=?", DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,optUid,id);
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
//@composite
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "删除成功");
//@output
return true;
}
/**
* 名单导入
*@Route
public boolean importExcel(ESurestream surestream) {
HttpServletRequest request=surestream.request();
// HttpServletResponse response=ResponseUtils.getResponse(surestream);
// if (!ServletFileUpload.isMultipartContent(request)) {
// throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897, "Request is not multipart, please
'multipart/form-data' enctype for your form" );
// }
String schoolYear = surestream.getString("oneParam");//学年
String termNum = surestream.getString("twoParam");//学期
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(termNum, "【学期】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(schoolYear, "【学年】不能为空");
HashMap typeMap = new HashMap();
List<RewardStuType> stuTypeList = this.findMultiple(RewardStuType.class, DBCondition.form("typeLevel", "3"));
if(stuTypeList!=null) {
for(RewardStuType tymap:stuTypeList) {
typeMap.put("CODE_"+tymap.getTypeName(), tymap.getTypeCode());
typeMap.put("AMOUNT_"+tymap.getTypeName(), tymap.getTypeCode());
}
}else {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【国家助学金级别】信息不存在");
}
try{
MultipartHttpServletRequest fileRequest = (MultipartHttpServletRequest)request;
for (Iterator<?> it = fileRequest.getFileNames(); it.hasNext();) {
String key = (String) it.next();
MultipartFile multipartFile = fileRequest.getFile(key);
String
filesuffix=UEditorConfigUitl.getFileSuffix(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename());//获取上传文件的
后缀名
if(!".xlsx".equals(filesuffix.toLowerCase())){
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897,"[非.xlsx]类型文件不允许上传");
}
InputStream fileIS = multipartFile.getInputStream();
String excelname = multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().substring(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().indexOf("."));
//得到部署路径
// String rootPath =
SingletonService.getRealPath().replace("/",System.getProperty("file.separator")).replace("\\", System.getProperty("file.separator"));
// excel 列结构
List<ExcelColumn> excelColumns = new ArrayList<ExcelColumn>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(0, "XH", "学号"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(1, "XM", "姓名"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(2, "GRANT_GRADE", "助学金级别"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(3, "ACTUAL_AMOUNT", "实发金额"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(4, "APPLY_REASON", "申请理由"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(5, "GRANT_REMARK", "备注说明"));
ExcelHead head = new ExcelHead();
head.setRowCount(1); // 头所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
List<HashMap> stuList=null;
try {
stuList = ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().importToObjectList(head, multipartFile.getInputStream());
} catch (Exception e) {
throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897,"导入国家助学金名单数据失败" );
}
String stuNo = null;//学号
String stuName = null;//姓名
String grantGrade = null;//助学金等级(1 一等；2 二等)
Double shouldAmount = null;//应发金额
Double actualAmount = null;//实发金额
String applyReason = null;//申请理由（申请理由合集）
String grantRemark = null;//备注
int countAdd = 0 ; //新增条数
//int countUpdate = 0;//更新条数
int failcnt = 0;//导入失败计数
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String remark = "";
for(HashMap stuMap : stuList){
remark = "";
int errcnt = 0;
//学号
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XH"))){
stuNo = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XH"));
}else{
remark +="学号不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//姓名
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XM"))){
stuName = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XM"));
}else{
remark +="姓名不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
String actualAmountS =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("ACTUAL_AMOUNT"));
if( Validate.isEmpty( actualAmountS) ){
remark+= "导入失败,实发金额不能为空.";
}else{
if(!NumberUtil.isDouble(actualAmountS) ||
Double.valueOf(actualAmountS)<=0){
remark+= "导入失败,实发金额【" + actualAmountS + "】格式
不正确.";
}else{
actualAmount = Double.valueOf(actualAmountS);
}
}
//助学金级别
String grantGradeName =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("GRANT_GRADE"));
if( Validate.isEmpty(grantGradeName) ){
remark+= "导入失败,助学金级别不能为空.";
}else{
grantGrade = typeMap.getString("CODE_"+grantGradeName);
if(Validate.isEmpty(grantGrade)){
remark+= "导入失败,助学金级别【" + grantGrade + "】对应
的信息不存在.";
}
String amouStr =
typeMap.getString("AMOUNT_"+grantGradeName);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(amouStr)) {
shouldAmount = Double.valueOf(amouStr);
}else {
remark+= "导入失败,助学金级别【" + grantGrade + "】对应
的金额不存在.";
}
}
grantRemark = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("GRANT_REMARK"));
String reasonStr = stuMap.getString("APPLY_REASON").trim();
List<HashMap> reasonList = CacheHolderDicTree.getDicListByCode("SYS_STUSCHOL_APPLY_REASON");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(reasonStr)) {
List<String> reasonCodeList = new ArrayList<String>();
if(reasonList!=null) {
for(HashMap rmap:reasonList) {
reasonCodeList.add(rmap.getString("ID"));
}
}
String[] reasonArr = reasonStr.split("、");
Object[] newReasonArr = BaseDataUtils.getUniqueArr(reasonArr);
StringBuilder powerStr = new StringBuilder("");
if(newReasonArr!=null && newReasonArr.length>0){
for(int i=0;i<newReasonArr.length;i++){
String reasonCode = (String)newReasonArr[i];
if(!Validate.isEmpty(reasonCode)
&& !reasonCodeList.contains(reasonCode)){
remark+="导入失败,申请理由【"+reasonCode+"】
有误，请根据表头说明填写.";
}else if(!Validate.isEmpty(reasonCode) &&
reasonCode.equals("H")){//申请理由为 H：其他，必须填写备注说明
if(Validate.isEmpty(grantRemark)){
remark+="导入失败,申请理由为 H：其他，必
须填写备注说明.";
}
}
powerStr.append(",").append(reasonCode);
}
applyReason=powerStr.substring(1);
}
}
//效验学号和姓名是否一致
HashMap stuValidateMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT
STU_NO,COLLEGE_CODE,SPECIALTY_CODE,CLASS_CODE FROM STUDENT_INFO WHERE STU_NO
= ? AND STU_NAME=? ", stuNo,stuName);
if(stuValidateMap==null) {
remark +="学号【" + stuNo + "】和姓名【"+ stuName +"】对应的
学生不存在.";
errcnt++;
}
//同一学年、学号是否重复导入
if(ScholarshipValidateUtils.stuGrantIsApply(this.getSession(), stuNo, null,
schoolYear,termNum)) {
remark+= "导入失败,学号【" + stuNo + "】对应的学生已导入国家
助学金名单.";
errcnt++;
}
//校验助学金获得者必须是最近一个批次贫困生名单里的学生，根据
当前学年往前推俩个学期 否则导入无效
if(!DifficultValidateUtils.stuDifficultIsExist(this.getSession(), stuNo, schoolYear, termNum, 1)) {
remark+= "导入失败,学号【" + stuNo + "】不是最近一个批次贫困
生名单里的学生.";
errcnt++;
}
if(DifficultValidateUtils.subsidyIsApply(this.getSession(), stuNo, null, schoolYear, termNum)) {
remark+= "导入失败,学号【" + stuNo + "】对应的学生已申请了困
难生补助.";
errcnt++;
}
//没错就进行保存操作
if(errcnt==0) {
try{
SupportGrantApply stuGrant = new SupportGrantApply();
stuGrant.setGrantUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("supportgrantuid"));
stuGrant.setSchoolYear(schoolYear);
stuGrant.setTermNum(termNum);
stuGrant.setStuNo(stuNo);
stuGrant.setGrantGrade(grantGrade);
stuGrant.setShouldAmount(shouldAmount);
stuGrant.setActualAmount(actualAmount);
stuGrant.setApplyReason(applyReason);
stuGrant.setGrantRemark(grantRemark);
stuGrant.setStuCollegeCode(stuValidateMap.getString("COLLEGE_CODE"));
stuGrant.setStuSpecialtyCode(stuValidateMap.getString("SPECIALTY_CODE"));
stuGrant.setStuClassCode(stuValidateMap.getString("CLASS_CODE"));
//stuGrant.setAuditStatus(AuditStageStatusEnum.two_wait.getKey());//学院公示
stuGrant.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
stuGrant.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.rewardstugrant.getKey());
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(), auditFlowUId, stuGrant.getGrantUid(), 1, "0", "修改提交", nowDate, optAccountUid, optAccount);
stuGrant.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
stuGrant.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
this.save(stuGrant);
remark = "学号[" + stuNo + "]导入成功.";
countAdd++;
}catch (Exception e) {
failcnt++;
}
}else {
failcnt++;
}
stuMap.put("IMPREMARK", remark);
}
String rootPath = Configurations.instance().getString("easy.upload.file.path").replace("/",System.getProperty("file.s
eparator"));
//生成处理结果文件
String zdypath = DicConst.IMPREWARD_PATH+File.separator;
String excelpath = rootPath + zdypath;;
File fDbfpath =new File(excelpath);
//如果文件夹不存在则创建
if (!fDbfpath.exists() && !fDbfpath.isDirectory()){
Logs.log().info( "[" + excelpath + "]不存在,创建" );
fDbfpath .mkdir();
}
String wdbffilename = DicConst.IMPREWARD_PATH+"_GJZXJ_" +
DateSource.getTradedate(CFrame.DatePattern5 ) + excelname;
String wdbffilepath = excelpath + wdbffilename;
String cdbffilepath = zdypath + wdbffilename;
File outputFile = new File(wdbffilepath);
// 需要特殊转换的单元
//Map<String, Map> headMap = new java.util.HashMap<String, Map>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(excelColumns.size(), "IMPREMARK", "导
入提示备注"));
head.setRowCount(1); // 模板中头部所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().exportExcelFile(head, fileIS, outputFile, stuList);
//返回数据
surestream.put("resultinfo", "导入国家助学金名单处理结果,成功[" +
countAdd +"]条,失败["+ failcnt +"]条请下载处理结果文件" );
surestream.put("retfilename", wdbffilename);//处理结果文件名
surestream.put("retfilepath", cdbffilepath);//处理结果文件存放路径
}
} catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "导入操作成功");
//@output
return true;
} **/
}
package com.easy.modules.support;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Date;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.egi.IFormatField;
import com.easy.asgi.footstone.exception.RException;

import com.easy.asgi.footstone.stereotype.method.Route;

@Plugin(
transcode = "grantSetupManage", transname = "助学金开通设置", author = "lcx", createDate = "2022-12-08"
)
@Transactional
public class GrantSetupManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("SETUP_STATUS",DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,Condition.noteq,new
JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SETUP_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("SETUP_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM",true));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM",true));
formats.put("END_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
String sql = "SELECT T.SETUP_UID, T.SETUP_NAME, T.SCHOOL_YEAR, T.TERM_NUM, T.BEGIN_DATE, T.END_DATE, T.SETUP_STATUS, T.SETUP_REMARK, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE
FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_SETUP T ";
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sql, arrayList.toArray());
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("setupUid");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【ID】不能为空");
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SETUP_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("SETUP_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("END_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
HashMap setupMap = this.queryForMapByFormat("SELECT T.* FROM
SUPPORT_GRANT_SETUP T WHERE T.SETUP_UID =? ", formats, setupUid);
if(setupMap!=null) {
String bStr = setupMap.getString("BEGIN_DATE");
String eStr = setupMap.getString("END_DATE");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(bStr) && !Validate.isEmpty(eStr)) {
setupMap.put("EDU_BEGIN_DATE", bStr+" ~ "+eStr);
}
}
surestream.put("data", setupMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("SETUP_UID");//
String eduDate = surestream.getString("EDU_BEGIN_DATE");//时间段 2020-01--01 - 2021-07-01
String[] dateData = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(eduDate,"~");
try{
SupportGrantSetup setup = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(setupUid)) {
setup = this.get(SupportGrantSetup.class, setupUid);
}
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(setup)&&!Validate.isEmpty(setup.getSetupUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), setup);
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(setup.getSetupStatus())) {
setup.setSetupStatus("1");
}
setup.setBeginDate(DateUtil.strToDate(dateData[0]));
setup.setEndDate(DateUtil.strToDate(dateData[1]));
setup.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
setup.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(setup);
} else {
setup = new SupportGrantSetup();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), setup);
setupUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("supportgrantsetupuid");
setup.setSetupUid(setupUid);
setup.setBeginDate(DateUtil.strToDate(dateData[0]));
setup.setEndDate(DateUtil.strToDate(dateData[1]));
setup.setSetupStatus("1");
setup.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
setup.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(setup);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 状态修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean updateStatus(ESurestream surestream) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("setupUid");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【ID】不能为空");
if (Validate.isEmpty(dataStatus)) {
dataStatus="0";
}
SupportGrantSetup setup = this.get(SupportGrantSetup.class, setupUid);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(setup)&&!Validate.isEmpty(setup.getSetupUid())){
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(dataStatus)) {
if(this.existSQL("SELECT A.SETUP_UID FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY A
WHERE A.SETUP_UID=? ", setup.getSetupUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【助学金开通设置信息】已使用，
不能删除！");
}
}
setup.setSetupStatus(dataStatus);
setup.setUpdateDate(DateSource.getTradedate());
setup.setUpdateUid(Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream));
this.update(setup);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【助学金开通设置】不存在");
}
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
return true;
}
}

@Plugin(
transcode = "grantStuManage", transname = "我的助学金信息", author = "lcx", createDate = "2022-12-08"
)
@Transactional
public class GrantStuManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream>{
/**
* 我的助学金列表
* **/
@Route
public boolean queryApply(ESurestream surestream) {
String dataType=null;//已申请 auditData、可申请 applyData、已获得 getData、已
退回 returnData
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("DATA_TYPE".equals(c.getName())) {
dataType = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
QResultSet pager =LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
// Long optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
arrayList = AuditDataUtils.getStuStatusArrayList(dataType, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM",true));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM",true));
if("applyData".equals(dataType)) {
formats.put("END_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
}else {
formats.put("APPLY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("APPLY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
}
pager.formatsMap(formats);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder("");
if("applyData".equals(dataType)) {
sqlBuild.append(" SELECT T.* FROM (SELECT
S.SCHOOL_YEAR,S.TERM_NUM,S.BEGIN_DATE,S.END_DATE,S.SETUP_UID,S.SETUP_NAME,A.GRA
NT_UID, A.AUDIT_STATUS ");
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_SETUP S ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY A ON
A.STU_NO='"+optAccount+"' AND A.SETUP_UID=S.SETUP_UID AND A.AUDIT_STATUS!='-1' ");
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE S.SETUP_STATUS='1' ) T "); //可以加当前时间在时间段
的查询条件
}else {
sqlBuild.append(" SELECT T.* FROM (SELECT
A.GRANT_UID,A.STU_NO,A.SCHOOL_YEAR,S.TERM_NUM,A.SETUP_UID,A.APPLY_DATE,A.AUDIT_S
TATUS,S.SETUP_NAME ");
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY A LEFT JOIN
SUPPORT_GRANT_SETUP S ON A.SETUP_UID=S.SETUP_UID ");
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE A.STU_NO='"+optAccount+"' AND
A.AUDIT_STATUS!='-1' AND A.AUDIT_STATUS!='0' ) T ");
}
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
List<HashMap> appList = pager.getDataSource();
if(appList!=null && appList.size()>0) {
for(HashMap dMp:appList) {
dMp.put("tableType", dataType);
if("applyData".equals(dataType)) {
dMp.put("isApply", "0");
Date nowDate =DateSource.getTradedate();
Date beginDate = DateUtil.strToDate(dMp.getString("BEGIN_DATE"));
Date endDate = DateUtil.strToDate(dMp.getString("END_DATE"));
if(DateUtil.isEffectiveDate(nowDate, beginDate, endDate)) {
dMp.put("isApply", "1");
}
}
dMp.put("END_DATE", dMp.getString("BEGIN_DATE") + " ~ " +
dMp.getString("END_DATE"));
}
}
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getApplyMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("setupUid");
String grantUid = surestream.getString("grantUid");
String isView = surestream.getString("isView","0");
HashMap applyMap = null;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(grantUid)) {
applyMap = this.getApplyMap(grantUid, isView);
}else {
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("END_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【设置 ID】不能为空");
HashMap stuMap = StuDataUtils.getStuMapByNo(getSession(), optAccount);
if(stuMap==null) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【学生信息数据】不存在！");
}
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT
S.SCHOOL_YEAR,S.TERM_NUM,S.BEGIN_DATE,S.END_DATE,S.SETUP_UID,S.SETUP_STATUS,S.SETU
P_NAME FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_SETUP S WHERE S.SETUP_UID=? ");
applyMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, setupUid);
applyMap.putAll(stuMap);
HashMap diffMap = DifficultDateUtils.getDiffMap(this.getSession(), optAccount, applyMap.getString("SCHOOL_YEAR"),true);
if(diffMap!=null) {
String diffType=diffMap.getString("D_DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID");
if(DifficultTypeEnum.D.getKey().equals(diffType)){
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, applyMap.getString("SCHOOL_YEAR_SV")+" 学 年 度 "+applyMap.getString("TERM_NUM_SV")+" 【困难生评定】中已被取消认定，不能申请国家助学金！");
}
}else {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, applyMap.getString("SCHOOL_YEAR_SV")+" 学 年 度 "+applyMap.getString("TERM_NUM_SV")+" 【困难生评定】未参与或未审核通过，不能申请国家助学金！");
}
applyMap.putAll(diffMap);
}
surestream.put("data", applyMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 申请撤回和取消申请操作
* **/
@Route
public boolean deleteStu(ESurestream surestream) {
String grantUid = surestream.getString("grantUid");
String dataStatus=surestream.getString("dataStatus","0");//0 撤回成草稿，-1 取消删除
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(grantUid, "【ID】不能为空");
String stuNo = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);//学号
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
SupportGrantApply apply = this.get(SupportGrantApply.class, grantUid);
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(apply)&&!Validate.isEmpty(apply.getGrantUid())){
SupportGrantSetup setup = this.get(SupportGrantSetup.class, apply.getSetupUid());
if(!stuNo.equals(apply.getStuNo())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【非本人申请记录】不能处理");
}
if(AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_draft.getKey().equals(dataStatus)) {//撤回操作
if(!DateUtil.isEffectiveDate(nowDate, setup.getBeginDate(), setup.getEndDate())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【该助学金申请批次】已关闭，
不能操作");
}
}
if(!AuditStageStatusEnum.one_return.getKey().equals(apply.getAuditStatus())
&& !AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_draft.getKey().equals(apply.getAuditStatus()) &&
AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_delete.getKey().equals(dataStatus)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【助学金申请已提交申请】不能直接
取消，请先撤回");
}
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(this.getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey());
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(), auditFlowUId, apply.getGrantUid(), 1, dataStatus,
" 撤 回 或 删 除 ", nowDate, Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream), optAccount);
apply.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
apply.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
apply.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
apply.setUpdateUid(Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream));
this.update(apply);
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【助学金申请信息】不存在");
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
//@output
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveStuApply(ESurestream surestream) {
String setupUid = surestream.getString("SETUP_UID");
String exeStatus = surestream.getString("exeStatus");//执行状态 1提交 0保存草稿
String stuNo = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);//学号
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(setupUid, "【设置 ID】不能为空");
String grantUid = surestream.getString("GRANT_UID");//
String applyRemark =surestream.getString("APPLY_REMARK");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(applyRemark, "【申请理由】不能为空");
SupportGrantSetup setup = this.get(SupportGrantSetup.class, setupUid);
if(setup==null || Validate.isEmpty(setup.getSetupUid())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【设置信息】不存在");
}
if(!"1".equals(setup.getSetupStatus())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【助学金申请批次】未开放，请联系管理
员启用该开通设置");
}
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
if(!DateUtil.isEffectiveDate(nowDate, setup.getBeginDate(), setup.getEndDate())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【助学金申请批次】未开放，请在有效时
间内进行申请");
}
StudentInfo studentInfo = this.get(StudentInfo.class, stuNo);
if(studentInfo==null || Validate.isEmpty(studentInfo.getStuNo())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【学生信息】不存在");
}
ReturnDataVo reVo = DifficultValidateUtils.validateDiff(this.getSession(), stuNo, setup.getSchoolYear(),null, ObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey(), "国家助学金");
if(reVo.isResult()) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, reVo.getRemark());
}
//批次在春季学期，但认定信息在秋季学期，不需要重修申请！
if(TermNumEnum.t2.getKey().equals(setup.getTermNum())) {
if(TermNumEnum.t1.getKey().equals(reVo.getTermNum())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, " 【 "+stuNo+" 】 在
【"+setup.getSchoolYear()+"】学年没有调整困难生档次，不需要提交该批次国家助学金申请
");
}
/**
* 1、是否每个学期都有困难生认定记录，且两次认定的困难档次是一致的
* 2、若是：则判断上学期是否申请过助学金，若没有则不能申请助学金
* 会不会出现 两次评定为困难生且未变动档次 但是上学期 没
有获得助学金也没有获得定时困难补助 这种情况 下学期 也不能申请？？？？？
* */
List<HashMap> difList = this.sqlQuery("SELECT
T.APPLY_UID,T.STU_NO,T.SCHOOL_YEAR,T.DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID FROM
SUPPORT_DIFFICULT_APPLY T WHERE T.STU_NO=? AND T.AUDIT_STATUS=? "
, studentInfo.getStuNo(),AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_pass.getKey());
if(difList!=null && difList.size()>1) {//两条则表示有变动记录
String dType0 = difList.get(0).getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID");
String dType1 = difList.get(1).getString("DIFFICULT_TYPE_UID");
if(dType0.equals(dType1)) {
if(!DifficultValidateUtils.grantIsApply(this.getSession(), stuNo, grantUid, setup.getSchoolYear(), TermNumEnum.t1.getKey()) &&
DifficultValidateUtils.subsidyIsApply(this.getSession(), stuNo, null, setup.getSchoolYear(), TermNumEnum.t1.getKey())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, " 【 "+stuNo+" 】 在
【"+setup.getSchoolYear()+"】学年有困难生档次变动且上学期已获得定期困难补助，该批次
不能申请国家助学金，只能申请定时困难补助");
}
}
}
}
if(DifficultValidateUtils.grantIsApply(this.getSession(), stuNo, grantUid, setup.getSchoolYear(), setup.getTermNum())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【"+stuNo+"】已申请该批次助学金，,不能
重复申请");
}
//国家助学金与定期困难补助不可兼得，如出现同一人已导入助学金名单，则该同
学导入无效
if(DifficultValidateUtils.subsidyIsApply(this.getSession(), stuNo, null, setup.getSchoolYear(), setup.getTermNum())) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, " 【 "+stuNo+" 】 已 申 请
【"+setup.getSchoolYear()+"】年度的定期困难补助，不能再申请国家助学金");
}
try{
SupportGrantApply grant = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(grantUid)) {
grant = this.get(SupportGrantApply.class, grantUid);
}
if (!Validate.isEmpty(grant)&&!Validate.isEmpty(grant.getGrantUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), grant);
grant.setAuditStatus(AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_draft.getKey());
if(!Validate.isEmpty(exeStatus) &&
AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
if(Validate.isEmpty(grant.getApplyUseruid())) {
grant.setApplyDate(nowDate);
grant.setApplyUseruid(optAccountUid);
}
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(this.getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey());
if(Validate.isEmpty(auditFlowUId)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【该业务审核流程】未配置，
请联系管理员配置！");
}
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(), auditFlowUId, grant.getGrantUid(), 1, exeStatus, "修改提交申请", nowDate, optAccountUid, optAccount);
grant.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
grant.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
}
if(Validate.isEmpty(grant.getStuClassCode())) {
grant.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
grant.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
grant.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
}
grant.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
grant.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(grant);
} else {
grant = new SupportGrantApply();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), grant);
grantUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("supportgrantuid");
grant.setGrantUid(grantUid);
grant.setAuditStatus(AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_draft.getKey());
if(!Validate.isEmpty(exeStatus) &&
AuditStatusEnum.pass_status.getKey().equals(exeStatus)) {
if(Validate.isEmpty(grant.getApplyUseruid())) {
grant.setApplyDate(nowDate);
grant.setApplyUseruid(optAccountUid);
}
//处理审核逻辑
String auditFlowUId = AuditDataUtils.getAuditFlowUid(this.getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey());
if(Validate.isEmpty(auditFlowUId)) {
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【该业务审核流程】未配置，
请联系管理员配置！");
}
AuditReturnParamEntity returnParam= AuditDataUtils.saveAuditExe(this.getSession(), auditFlowUId, grant.getGrantUid(), 1, exeStatus, "直接提交申请", nowDate, optAccountUid, optAccount);
grant.setAuditStatus(returnParam.getReturnStatus());
grant.setAuditSortNo(returnParam.getReturnSortNo());
}
grant.setStuNo(studentInfo.getStuNo());
grant.setStuCollegeCode(studentInfo.getCollegeCode());
grant.setStuSpecialtyCode(studentInfo.getSpecialtyCode());
grant.setStuClassCode(studentInfo.getClassCode());
grant.setSchoolYear(setup.getSchoolYear());
grant.setTermNum(setup.getTermNum());
grant.setSetupUid(setup.getSetupUid());
grant.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
grant.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(grant);
}
//更新文件的业务对象及 ID
String[] attrfileidsStr=(String[])surestream.getArray("attrfileids[]");
BaseFileUtils.saveBaseFile(this.getSession(), attrfileidsStr, ObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey(), grant.getGrantUid());
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
private HashMap getApplyMap(String grantUid,String isView) {
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("BEGIN_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("BEGIN_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("END_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("END_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX"));//性别代码
formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK"));//开户行
formats.put("UPDATE_TIME", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_TIME","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss"));
formats.put("AUDIT_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("AUDIT_STATUS", "AUDIT_AUDIT_STATUS"));
formats.put("APPLY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("APPLY_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));//申请时间
formats.put("APPLY_REASON", new FormatDic2Str("APPLY_REASON", "SYS_GRANT_APPLY_REASON"));//
formats.put("STU_NATION_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_NATION_CODE", "SYS_DM_NATION"));//民族代码
formats.put("BIRTHDAY_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("BIRTHDAY_DATE","yyyy-MM",true));//出生年月
formats.put("STU_ENROL_DATE", new
FormatDate2Str("STU_ENROL_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd",true));//入学日期
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.*, S.SETUP_NAME,S.BEGIN_DATE,S.END_DATE, RT.TYPE_NAME AS
GRANT_GRADE_NAME,E.HOME_TEL AS STU_HOME_TEL,E.HOME_ADDRESS AS
STU_HOME_ADDRESS,E.HOME_POST AS STU_HOME_POST ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY T ");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_GRANT_SETUP S ON S.SETUP_UID=T.SETUP_UID
");
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN SUPPORT_STU_TYPE RT ON RT.TYPE_CODE =
T.GRANT_GRADE AND RT.TYPE_LEVEL='3' ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN STUDENT_INFO_EXT E ON E.STU_NO_EXT=T.STU_NO ");
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.GRANT_UID = ? ");
HashMap applyMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, grantUid);
if(applyMap!=null) {
if("1".equals(isView)) {
//审核记录
applyMap.put("auditExeList", AuditDataUtils.getAuditExeList(this.getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey(), applyMap.getString("GRANT_UID"),true));
//公式材料和评议材料
applyMap.put("recodeList",BaseFileUtils.getRecodeList(getSession(), applyMap.getString("STU_CLASS_CODE"), applyMap.getString("STU_COLLEGE_CODE"), applyMap.getString("SCHOOL_YEAR"), applyMap.getString("TERM_NUM"), ObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey()));
}
HashMap diffMap = DifficultDateUtils.getDiffMap(this.getSession(), applyMap.getString("STU_NO"), applyMap.getString("SCHOOL_YEAR"),true);
applyMap.putAll(diffMap);
String applyReason = applyMap.getString("APPLY_REASON");
StringBuilder reasonStrB = new StringBuilder();
boolean isVother = false;
if(!Validate.isEmpty(applyReason)){
String[] str= applyReason.split(",");
for(String str0:str){
if("H".equals(str0)) {
isVother=true;
continue;
}
DictionaryTreeNode node = CacheHolderDicTree.getDicByName("SYS_GRANT_APPLY_REASON", str0);
if(node!=null){
reasonStrB.append("，").append(node.getDicName());
}
}
}
if(isVother) {
reasonStrB.append("，").append(applyMap.getString("OTHER_REASON"));
}
String reasonStr = "";
if(reasonStrB!=null && reasonStrB.length()>1) {
reasonStr = reasonStrB.substring(1);
}
applyMap.put("APPLY_REASON_SV", reasonStr);
}
return applyMap;
}
/**
* 申请表导出
* **/
@Route
public boolean expPdf(ESurestream surestream) {
String grantUid = surestream.getString("grantUid");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(grantUid, "【助学金 ID】不能为空");
HashMapapplyMap = this.getApplyMap(grantUid, "1");
if(applyMap!=null) {
//项目部署根路径
String SUB_FILE_DIR = SingletonService.getRealPath();
InputStream in = null;
try {
WordToPdfUtils wordToPdfUtils = new WordToPdfUtils(new
FileInputStream(new
File(SUB_FILE_DIR+"template/support/exp_grant.docx".replace("/",System.getProperty("file.sep
arator")))));
Map<String, Object> context = new java.util.HashMap<>();
@SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
List<HashMap> familyList = (List<HashMap>)applyMap.get("familyList");
List<StuFamilyVo> familys = new ArrayList<>();
if(familyList!=null && familyList.size()>0) {
for(HashMap tmap : familyList){
String birDateS = tmap.getString("BIRTHDAY_DATE");
String ages = "";
if(!Validate.isEmpty(birDateS)) {
Date birDate = DateUtil.strToDate(birDateS);
if(DateUtil.getAge(birDate)!=0) {
ages = String.valueOf(DateUtil.getAge(birDate));
}
}
familys.add(new
StuFamilyVo(tmap.getString("DFAMILY_UID"),tmap.getString("MEMBER_NAME"),String.valueOf(
ages),tmap.getString("RELATION_CODE_SV")
,tmap.getString("WORK_UNIT"),tmap.getString("TITLES_NAME"),tmap.getString("INCOME_
YEAR"),tmap.getString("HEALTH_CODE_SV")));
}
}else {
familys.add(new StuFamilyVo("1"," "," "," "," "," "," ", ""));
}
context.put("familys", familys);
//将需要替换的数据数据添加到上下文中
//其中 key 为 word 模板中的域名，value 是需要替换的值
context.put("SCHOOL_NAME", DicConst.DEFAULT_SCHOOLNAME);
context.put("STU_COLLEGE_NAME", applyMap.getString("STU_COLLEGE_NAME"));
context.put("STU_SPECIALTY_NAME", applyMap.getString("STU_SPECIALTY_NAME"));
context.put("STU_CLASS_NAME", applyMap.getString("STU_CLASS_NAME"));
context.put("STU_STU_NAME", applyMap.getString("STU_STU_NAME"));
context.put("STU_SEX_CODE_SV", applyMap.getString("STU_SEX_CODE_SV"));
context.put("BIRTHDAY_DATE", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("BIRTHDAY_DATE"))?apply
Map.getString("BIRTHDAY_DATE"):"");//出生日期
context.put("STU_NATION_CODE_SV", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_NATION_COD
E_SV"))?applyMap.getString("STU_NATION_CODE_SV"):"");
context.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE_SV", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_POLITICAL_ CODE_SV"))?applyMap.getString("STU_POLITICAL_CODE_SV"):"");
context.put("STU_ENROL_DATE", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_ENROL_DATE"))?a
pplyMap.getString("STU_ENROL_DATE"):"");//入学日期
context.put("STU_NO", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_NO"))?applyMap.getString(" STU_NO"):"");
context.put("STU_GRADE_CODE", applyMap.getString("STU_GRADE_CODE"));
context.put("STU_CARD_NUM", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_CARD_NUM"))?appl
yMap.getString("STU_CARD_NUM"):"");
context.put("STU_TEL_NUM", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_TEL_NUM"))?applyM
ap.getString("STU_TEL_NUM"):"");
context.put("FAMILY_NUM", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("D_FAMILY_NUM"))?applyM
ap.getString("D_FAMILY_NUM"):"");//家庭人口
context.put("ALL_INCOME_MONTH", "");
context.put("PER_INCOME_MONTH", "");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("D_FAMILY_NUM"))
&& !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("D_PER_CAPITA_INCOME"))) {
String fNum = applyMap.getString("D_FAMILY_NUM");//家庭人口
String fIncome = applyMap.getString("D_PER_CAPITA_INCOME");//人均
年收入
BigDecimal monNumB = new BigDecimal("12");
BigDecimal fNumB = new BigDecimal(fNum);
BigDecimal fIncomeB = new BigDecimal(fIncome);
BigDecimal perMonth =
fIncomeB.divide(monNumB,BigDecimal.ROUND_HALF_UP);
BigDecimal fMonth = perMonth.multiply(fNumB);
context.put("PER_INCOME_MONTH", perMonth.toString());//PER_INCOME_MONTH 人均月收入
context.put("ALL_INCOME_MONTH", fMonth.toString());//ALL_INCOME_MONTH 月总收入
}
context.put("D_INCOME_SOURCE", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("D_INCOME_SOURCE")
)?applyMap.getString("D_INCOME_SOURCE"):"");//收入来源
context.put("STU_HOME_ADDRESS", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_HOME_ADDRE
SS"))?applyMap.getString("STU_HOME_ADDRESS"):"");
context.put("STU_HOME_POST", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_HOME_POST"))?ap
plyMap.getString("STU_HOME_POST"):"");//
context.put("STU_HOME_TEL", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("STU_HOME_TEL"))?apply
Map.getString("STU_HOME_TEL"):"");
context.put("APPLY_REASON_SV", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("APPLY_REASON_SV"))?
applyMap.getString("APPLY_REASON_SV"):"");
String applyDate = applyMap.getString("APPLY_DATE");
if(!Validate.isEmpty(applyDate)) {
String[] applyStr=applyDate.split("-");
context.put("year", applyStr[0]);
context.put("month", applyStr[1]);
context.put("day", applyStr[2]);
}else {
context.put("year", "");
context.put("month", "");
context.put("day", "");
}
context.put("GRANT_GRADE_NAME", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("GRANT_GRADE_N
AME"))?applyMap.getString("GRANT_GRADE_NAME"):"");
context.put("SCHOOL_YEAR_SV", !Validate.isEmpty(applyMap.getString("SCHOOL_YEAR_SV"))?a
pplyMap.getString("SCHOOL_YEAR_SV"):"");
//添加每个步骤的审核日期
HashMap dataMap = AuditDataUtils.getAuditDate(getSession(), AuditObjTypeEnum.supportgrant.getKey(), grantUid);
context.putAll(dataMap);
String stuNo = applyMap.getString("STU_NO");
//组装数据
wordToPdfUtils.assembleMap(context);
String fileName = stuNo+"_ 助 学 金 申 请 表
_"+DateSource.getTradedate("yyyyMMddHHssmm")+ ".docx";
//生成 pdf
// File outputFile = new File("D:/ok_template.pdf");
// OutputStream outputStream = new FileOutputStream(outputFile);
// wordToPdfUtils.createPdf(outputStream);
wordToPdfUtils.downWord(surestream.response(), fileName);
// wordToPdfUtils.downPdf(surestream.response(), fileName);
Logs.log( ).info("*********************"+stuNo +"的助学金申请表导出成
功" );
} catch (IOException e) {
Logs.log( ).error("助学金申请表导出，读取 Word 模板异常",e);
// logger.error("读取 Word 模板异常",e);
} catch (XDocReportException e) {
Logs.log( ).error("助学金申请表导出，模板生成失败",e);
} catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}finally {
if(in!=null){
try {
in.close();
} catch (IOException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
}
}
return true;
}
}

@Plugin(
transcode = "grantTransferManage", transname = "助学金发放记录", author = "lcx", createDate = "2023-05-04"
)
@Transactional
public class GrantTransferManage extends AbstractSessionComponent<ESurestream> {
/**
* 列表查询
* **/
@Route
public boolean query(ESurestream surestream) {
String collegeSelvalue=null;
String isE="0";//是否导出
List<Condition> otherParamList = LayUiTableUtils.getOtherParam(surestream);
if(otherParamList!=null&&otherParamList.size()>0) {
for(Condition c:otherParamList) {
if("COLLEGE_SELVALUE".equals(c.getName())) {
collegeSelvalue = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}else if("isE".equals(c.getName())) {
isE = String.valueOf(c.getValue());
}
}
}
String[] arrCode = BaseDataUtils.getSplit2Arr(collegeSelvalue,null);
QResultSet pager = LayUiTableUtils.getQResultSet(surestream);
List<Object> arrayList = new ArrayList<Object>();
// Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("DATA_STATUS",DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,Condition.noteq,new
JoinCondition("AND"));
// arrayList.add(otherCondition);
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[0])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_COLLEGE_CODE",arrCode[0],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[1])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_SPECIALTY_CODE",arrCode[1],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(arrCode[2])) {
Condition otherCondition = new
Condition("STU_CLASS_CODE",arrCode[2],Condition.eq,new JoinCondition("AND"));
arrayList.add(otherCondition);
}
String optUid = Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String roleType = AccountPowerUtils.getAccountRoleById(this.getSession(), optUid);
//账户数据权限控制方法一
String roleSql = null;
if(RoleTypeEnum.college.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_COLLEGE_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.counselor.getKey().equals(roleType)) {
roleSql = " STU_CLASS_CODE IN (SELECT CODE_UID FROM
BASE_ACCOUNT_POWER WHERE ACCOUNT_UID='"+optUid+"' AND CODE_TYPE='"+roleType+"') ";
}else if(RoleTypeEnum.student.getKey().equals(roleType)){
roleSql = " STU_NO = '"+optAccount+"' ";
}else if(!RoleTypeEnum.school.getKey().equals(roleType)) {//无权限进行操作
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "无权限进行操作");
return true;
}
if(!Validate.isEmpty(roleSql)) {
Condition collCondition = new Condition(new ConditionValue(roleSql));
arrayList.add(collCondition);
}
LayUiTableUtils.conditionList(surestream, arrayList);
LayUiTableUtils.orderByList(surestream, arrayList);
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM",true));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM",true));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX",true));//性别代码
formats.put("DATA_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("DATA_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
// formats.put("UPDATE_UID", new FormatAccountUid2Name("UPDATE_UID",""));
pager.formatsMap(formats);
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* FROM ( SELECT T.TRANSFER_UID,
T.SCHOOL_YEAR, T.TERM_NUM, T.STU_NO, T.ACTUAL_AMOUNT, T.MONTH_NUM, T.MONTH_AMOUNT, T.DATA_STATUS, T.UPDATE_UID, T.UPDATE_DATE ");
sqlBuild.append(", T.CREATE_UID, T.CREATE_DATE, T.STU_COLLEGE_CODE, T.STU_SPECIALTY_CODE, T.STU_CLASS_CODE ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_TRANSFER T ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.DATA_STATUS!='-1' ");
sqlBuild.append(" ) T ");
pager = this.sqlConditionQuery(pager, sqlBuild.toString(), arrayList.toArray());
LayUiTableUtils.putDataOut(surestream, pager);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* map 信息获取
* **/
@Route
public boolean getMap( ESurestream surestream ) {
String transferUid = surestream.getString("transferUid");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(transferUid, "【ID】不能为空");
Map<Object, IFormatField> formats=new java.util.HashMap<Object, IFormatField>();
formats.put("SCHOOL_YEAR", new FormatDic2Str("SCHOOL_YEAR", "SYS_YEAR_NUM"));
formats.put("TERM_NUM", new FormatDic2Str("TERM_NUM", "SYS_TERM_NUM"));
formats.put("STU_SEX_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_SEX_CODE", "SYS_DM_SEX"));//性别代码
formats.put("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", new FormatDic2Str("STU_POLITICAL_CODE", "SYS_DM_POLITICAL"));//政治面貌代码
formats.put("STU_BANK_NAME", new FormatDic2Str("STU_BANK_NAME", "SYS_DM_BANK"));//开户行
formats.put("DATA_STATUS", new FormatDic2Str("DATA_STATUS", "SYS_DATA_STATUS"));
formats.put("UPDATE_DATE", new FormatDate2Str("UPDATE_DATE","yyyy-MM-dd
HH:mm:ss",true));
StringBuilder sqlBuild = new StringBuilder(" SELECT T.* ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoFieldSql(sqlBuild, true);
sqlBuild.append(" FROM SUPPORT_GRANT_TRANSFER T ");
StuDataUtils.appendStuInfoTableSql(sqlBuild);
sqlBuild.append(" LEFT JOIN STUDENT_INFO_EXT E ON E.STU_NO_EXT=T.STU_NO ");
sqlBuild.append(" WHERE T.TRANSFER_UID = ? ");
HashMap transferMap = this.queryForMapByFormat(sqlBuild.toString(), formats, transferUid);
surestream.put("data", transferMap);
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000,"查询成功");
return true;
}
/**
* 信息修改
* **/
@Route
public boolean saveOrUpdate(ESurestream surestream) {
String transferUid = surestream.getString("TRANSFER_UID");//
String schoolYear = surestream.getString("SCHOOL_YEAR");//学年
String termNum = surestream.getString("TERM_NUM");//学期
String stuNo = surestream.getString("STU_NO");//学号
// Double actualAmount = surestream.getDouble("ACTUAL_AMOUNT");//实发总金额
// Integer monthNum = surestream.getInteger("MONTH_NUM");//月数
// Double monthAmount = surestream.getDouble("MONTH_AMOUNT");//每月发放金额
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(stuNo, "【学生学号】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(schoolYear, "【学年】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(termNum, "【学期】不能为空");
try{
SupportGrantTransfer transfer = null;
if (!Validate.isEmpty(transferUid)) {
transfer = this.get(SupportGrantTransfer.class, transferUid);
}
//填充值
// transfer.setTransferUid(transferUid);
// transfer.setSchoolYear(schoolYear);
// transfer.setTermNum(termNum);
// transfer.setStuNo(stuNo);
// transfer.setActualAmount(actualAmount);
// transfer.setMonthNum(monthNum);
// transfer.setMonthAmount(monthAmount);
// transfer.setStuCollegeCode(stuCollegeCode);
// transfer.setStuSpecialtyCode(stuSpecialtyCode);
// transfer.setStuClassCode(stuClassCode);
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
if (!Validate.isEmpty(transfer)&&!Validate.isEmpty(transfer.getTransferUid())) {
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), transfer);
if(DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX.equals(transfer.getDataStatus())) {
transfer.setDataStatus("1");
}
transfer.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
transfer.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.update(transfer);
} else {
transfer = new SupportGrantTransfer();
this.hashMap2Obj(surestream.getDownbuf(), transfer);
transferUid=DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("granttransferuid");
transfer.setTransferUid(transferUid);
transfer.setDataStatus("1");
transfer.setCreateDate(nowDate);
transfer.setCreateUid(optAccountUid);
transfer.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
transfer.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
this.save(transfer);
}
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
// @output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "操作成功");
// @output
return true;
}
/**
* 批量删除
* id 以逗号,拼接
* **/
@Route
public boolean delete(ESurestream surestream) {
String transferUid = surestream.getString("transferUid");
try{
if (!Validate.isEmpty(transferUid)) {
List<String> uidList= new ArrayList<String>();
Collections.addAll(uidList, transferUid.split(","));
String optUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
for(String id:uidList){
//判断为空
if(!Validate.isEmpty(id)) {
this.update("UPDATE SUPPORT_GRANT_TRANSFER SET
DATA_STATUS=?, UPDATE_UID=? ,UPDATE_DATE=SYSDATE WHERE TRANSFER_UID=?", DicConst.DIC_DATA_STATUS_SX,optUid,id);
}
}
}else{
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897, "【ID】不能为空");
}
//@composite
}catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "删除成功");
//@output
return true;
}
@Route
public boolean importExcel(ESurestream surestream) {
HttpServletRequest request=surestream.request();
// HttpServletResponse response=ResponseUtils.getResponse(surestream);
// if (!ServletFileUpload.isMultipartContent(request)) {
// throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897, "Request is not multipart, please
'multipart/form-data' enctype for your form" );
// }
String schoolYear = surestream.getString("oneParam");//学年
String termNum = surestream.getString("twoParam");//学期
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(termNum, "【学期】不能为空");
ValidatorSupport.isEmpty(schoolYear, "【学年】不能为空");
try{
MultipartHttpServletRequest fileRequest = (MultipartHttpServletRequest)request;
for (Iterator<?> it = fileRequest.getFileNames(); it.hasNext();) {
String key = (String) it.next();
MultipartFile multipartFile = fileRequest.getFile(key);
String
filesuffix=UEditorConfigUitl.getFileSuffix(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename());//获取上传文件的
后缀名
if(!".xlsx".equals(filesuffix.toLowerCase())){
throw new RWarn(RWarn._999897,"[非.xlsx]类型文件不允许上传");
}
InputStream fileIS = multipartFile.getInputStream();
String excelname = multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().substring(multipartFile.getOriginalFilename().indexOf("."));
//得到部署路径
// String rootPath =
SingletonService.getRealPath().replace("/",System.getProperty("file.separator")).replace("\\", System.getProperty("file.separator"));
// excel 列结构
List<ExcelColumn> excelColumns = new ArrayList<ExcelColumn>();
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(0, "XH", "学号"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(1, "XM", "姓名"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(2, "MONTH_NUM", "实发月数"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(3, "MONTH_AMOUNT", "每月金额"));
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(4, "ACTUAL_AMOUNT", "实发金额"));
ExcelHead head = new ExcelHead();
head.setRowCount(1); // 头所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
List<HashMap> stuList=null;
try {
stuList = ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().importToObjectList(head, multipartFile.getInputStream());
} catch (Exception e) {
throw new RWarn( RWarn._999897,"导入国家助学金发放记录失败" );
}
String stuNo = null;//学号
String stuName = null;//姓名
Integer monthNum = null;//月数
String monthAmountStr = null;//每月金额
String actualAmountStr =null;//金额
int countAdd = 0 ; //新增条数
int countUpdate = 0;//更新条数
int failcnt = 0;//导入失败计数
Date nowDate=DateSource.getTradedate();
String optAccountUid=Accountmgt.getAccountUid(surestream);
// String optAccount = Accountmgt.getAccount(surestream);
String remark = "";
for(HashMap stuMap : stuList){
remark = "";
int errcnt = 0;
//学号
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XH"))){
stuNo = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XH").trim());
}else{
remark +="学号不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//姓名
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("XM"))){
stuName = StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("XM").trim());
}else{
remark +="姓名不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//发放月数
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("MONTH_NUM"))){
String monthNumTep =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("MONTH_NUM").trim());
if(!NumberUtil.isInteger(monthNumTep) ||
Integer.valueOf(monthNumTep)<=0){
remark+= "导入失败,发放月数【" + monthNumTep + "】必须
是大于 0 的整数.";
}
monthNum = Integer.valueOf(monthNumTep);
}else{
remark +="发放月数不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//每月发放金额
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("MONTH_AMOUNT"))){
String monthAmountTep =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("MONTH_AMOUNT").trim());
if(!NumberUtil.isInteger(monthAmountTep) ||
Integer.valueOf(monthAmountTep)<=0){
remark+= "导入失败,每月发放金额【" + monthAmountTep + "】
必须是大于 0 的整数.";
}
monthAmountStr = monthAmountTep;
}else{
remark +="每月发放金额不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
//发放金额
if (!Validate.isEmpty(stuMap.getString("ACTUAL_AMOUNT"))){
String actualAmountTep =
StringUtil.trim(stuMap.getString("ACTUAL_AMOUNT").trim());
if(!NumberUtil.isInteger(actualAmountTep) ||
Integer.valueOf(actualAmountTep)<=0){
remark+= "导入失败,发放总金额【" + actualAmountTep + "】
必须是大于 0 的整数.";
}
actualAmountStr = actualAmountTep;
}else{
remark +="发放总金额不能为空！";
errcnt++;
}
BigDecimal monthAmountB = new BigDecimal(monthAmountStr);
BigDecimal monthNumB = new BigDecimal(monthNum);
BigDecimal actualAmountB = new BigDecimal(actualAmountStr);
BigDecimal allB = monthAmountB.multiply(monthNumB);
if(actualAmountB.compareTo(allB) !=0) {
remark +="【发放总金额】与【后台计算的总金额】不一致！请
核实！";
errcnt++;
}
//效验学号和姓名是否一致
HashMap stuValidateMap = this.queryForMap("SELECT
STU_NO,COLLEGE_CODE,SPECIALTY_CODE,CLASS_CODE FROM STUDENT_INFO WHERE STU_NO=?
AND STU_NAME=? ", stuNo,stuName);
if(stuValidateMap==null) {
remark +="学号【" + stuNo + "】和姓名【"+ stuName +"】对应的
学生不存在.";
errcnt++;
}
/**
* 1、实发是要发放的学生
* 2、发放的标准和金额是否一致
* **/
String grantSql = "SELECT T.STU_NO,T.SHOULD_AMOUNT FROM
SUPPORT_GRANT_APPLY T " +
" WHERE T.STU_NO=? AND T.SCHOOL_YEAR=? AND
T.AUDIT_STATUS=? " +
" AND T.STU_NO NOT IN (SELECT A.STU_NO FROM
SUPPORT_SUBSIDY_APPLY A WHERE A.SCHOOL_YEAR=? AND A.TERM_NUM='2' AND
A.AUDIT_STATUS=? ) ";
HashMap grantValidateMap = this.queryForMap(grantSql, stuNo, schoolYear, AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_pass.getKey(), schoolYear, AuditStageStatusEnum.stage_pass.getKey());
if(grantValidateMap!=null) {
String shouldAmount =
grantValidateMap.getString("SHOULD_AMOUNT");//发放标准
BigDecimal shouldAmountB = new BigDecimal(shouldAmount);
BigDecimal monthAmountTB = shouldAmountB.divide(new
BigDecimal(5));//每月发放标准
if(monthAmountB.compareTo(monthAmountTB) !=0) {
remark +="【每月金额】与【申请的每月标准】不一致！请
核实！";
errcnt++;
}
}else {
remark +="学号【" + stuNo + "】的学生助学金申请记录不存在.";
errcnt++;
}
//没错就进行保存操作
if(errcnt==0) {
try{
SupportGrantTransfer transfer =
this.findSingle(SupportGrantTransfer.class, DBCondition.form("stuNo", stuNo), DBCondition.form("schoolYear", schoolYear)
, DBCondition.form("termNum", termNum), DBCondition.form("dataStatus", "1"));
boolean isUpdate = true;
if (transfer == null) {
transfer = new SupportGrantTransfer();
transfer.setTransferUid(DcKeyGenerate.getStringKeyCode("granttransferuid"));
transfer.setSchoolYear(schoolYear);
transfer.setTermNum(termNum);
transfer.setStuNo(stuNo);
transfer.setStuCollegeCode(stuValidateMap.getString("COLLEGE_CODE"));
transfer.setStuSpecialtyCode(stuValidateMap.getString("SPECIALTY_CODE"));
transfer.setStuClassCode(stuValidateMap.getString("CLASS_CODE"));
transfer.setCreateUid(optAccountUid);
transfer.setCreateDate(nowDate);
transfer.setDataStatus("1");
isUpdate = false;
}
//填充值
transfer.setMonthNum(monthNum);
transfer.setMonthAmount(monthAmountB.doubleValue());
transfer.setActualAmount(actualAmountB.doubleValue());
transfer.setUpdateUid(optAccountUid);
transfer.setUpdateDate(nowDate);
if(isUpdate) {
this.update(transfer);
remark = "学号[" + stuNo + "]更新成功.";
countUpdate++;
}else {
this.save(transfer);
remark = "学号[" + stuNo + "]新增导入成功.";
countAdd++;
}
}catch (Exception e) {
failcnt++;
}
}else {
failcnt++;
}
stuMap.put("IMPREMARK", remark);
}
String rootPath = Configurations.instance().getString("easy.upload.file.path").replace("/",System.getProperty("file.s
eparator"));
//生成处理结果文件
String zdypath = DicConst.IMPSUPPORT_PATH+File.separator;
String excelpath = rootPath + zdypath;;
File fDbfpath =new File(excelpath);
//如果文件夹不存在则创建
if (!fDbfpath.exists() && !fDbfpath.isDirectory()){
Logs.log().info( "[" + excelpath + "]不存在,创建" );
fDbfpath .mkdir();
}
String wdbffilename = DicConst.IMPSUPPORT_PATH+"_GRANT_" +
DateSource.getTradedate(CFrame.DatePattern5 ) + excelname;
String wdbffilepath = excelpath + wdbffilename;
String cdbffilepath = zdypath + wdbffilename;
File outputFile = new File(wdbffilepath);
// 需要特殊转换的单元
excelColumns.add(new ExcelColumn(excelColumns.size(), "IMPREMARK", "导
入提示备注"));
head.setRowCount(1); // 模板中头部所占行数
head.setColumns(excelColumns); // 列的定义
head.setColumnsConvertMap(null); // 列的转换
ExcelHashMapHelper.getInstanse().exportExcelFile(head, fileIS, outputFile, stuList);
//返回数据
surestream.put("resultinfo", "导入助学金发放处理结果,成功[" + countAdd
+"]条,更新["+ countUpdate +"]条,失败["+ failcnt +"]条请下载处理结果文件" );
surestream.put("retfilename", wdbffilename);//处理结果文件名
surestream.put("retfilepath", cdbffilepath);//处理结果文件存放路径
}
} catch ( RWarn e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch ( RException e) {
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}catch (Exception e) {
e.printStackTrace();
TryThrowable.agent( e, this );
}
//@output
surestream.putReason(RWarn._000000, "导入操作成功");
//@output
return true;
}
}
